Red Eagle Redoubt

**Red Eagle Redoubt** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") and two exterior camps east of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). It contains only one zone, *[Red Eagle Ascent](#Red_Eagle_Ascent)*.

Looking down over the altar area in Red Eagle Ascent

The map marker is near the highest point of the small mountain range southwest of [Sundered Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Sundered_Towers "Skyrim:Sundered Towers"). The surrounding area is populated by a large number of Forsworn of increasing skill as you approach the peak, which itself is home to several [elk](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer#Elk "Skyrim:Deer").

#### Miscellaneous Quests

- **[Rebel's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn_(quest) "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn (quest)")**: Find [Red Eagle's](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle "Skyrim:Red Eagle") [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Red Eagle's Bane").

#### Radiant Quests

- **[Bounty: Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Forsworn "Skyrim:Bounty: Forsworn")**: Kill a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") leader for a bounty reward.
- **[The Ghost of Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:The Ghost of Old Hroldan")**: Put an [ancient ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:Ghost of Old Hroldan") to rest.
- **[The House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors")**: Help [Molag Bal](/wiki/Lore:Molag_Bal "Lore:Molag Bal") take revenge upon a servant of [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah").
- **[Kill the Forsworn Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Forsworn_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Forsworn Leader (Jarl)")**: Do a favor for [Jarl Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund") by killing a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") leader.
- **[Lisbet's Missing Shipment](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet%27s_Missing_Shipment "Skyrim:Lisbet's Missing Shipment")**: Retrieve a missing Dibella Statue for a struggling store.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior: Lower Camp

Two leveled Forsworn guard the approach from the northwest. One of them is next to a campfire, with an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") and a rack for drying hides nearby. The second Forsworn is on top of a rock with a small wooden table and chair and wooden steps up to it. The entrance to Red Eagle Ascent is to the left of this raised area.

### Red Eagle Ascent

This cave is a typical Forsworn encampment with the normal sharpened stakes and goat head decorations as well as vegetation throughout. Upon entering, there is a tunnel that twists and turns, until you pass a tree stump with a patch of [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") growing from it, after which the tunnel opens up. There is an elk head off to the left with a lit lantern in front of it, with a [deer hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Hide "Skyrim:Deer Hide") nearby. Just after this, on your right is an iron ore vein behind some of the sharpened stakes, next to a tree with a couple taproot ornaments. Across the path by this is a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") that drops an [oil lantern](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Oil Lanterns") on an [oil slick trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slicks "Skyrim:Oil Slicks"). Setting this off will alert the two Forsworn that are guarding this part of the cave and can be used to your advantage in dealing with them. Behind the previously mentioned tree is a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on the ground. Near where the two Forsworn are standing is a lit brazier with a random healing potion next to it, while an adept-locked chest is behind some roots on the opposite side of a tunnel entrance heading east.

Through the tunnel there are [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") and several [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") fungi before a flight of stone steps up to the next cavern. There is a [bear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") just after entering this cavern, hidden among some of the vegetation. Three more Forsworn make this room their home; the first is at the top of another flight of stone stairs, and the other two are at the rear of the room. Before reaching the stairs, you pass another white cap patch on your right, and just before the stairs, a [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") is on your left.

At the top of the flight of stone stairs is a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that activates a [dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") fired from your right across the path in front of you, and on your left is a handle that can be used by the Forsworn to activate a [falling boulders](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") trap below. Off on your left behind a tall pillar is a lit brazier with a random [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe") and [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") lying beside it. Following the path up over a few wide steps, you reach an area with a blood-covered altar holding a leveled [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow"), a random potion of magicka, and a decapitated skeever. Also on this plateau are a chair and a flight of wooden stairs with an unlocked chest and random stamina potion underneath.

The stairs lead up to a corridor that branches off to your right to the exit, and ahead to a blocked corridor with a fly amanita, two [bleeding crowns](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), a [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), and a medium coin purse. Taking the branch to the right and up a few more steps, you reach an unlocked iron door that leads outside to the upper camp of the redoubt.

### Exterior: Upper Camp

Upon exiting, you are at the bottom of several flights of stairs up. There is a campfire with a pile of firewood behind. Each flight of stairs has Forsworn guarding them, each increasing in skill as you go higher. Before climbing, if you travel around to the left of the first flight of stairs, underneath a fallen stone tower you will find a large coin purse.

At the top of the first flight of stairs there is a Forsworn either wandering or sitting on a wooden bench. Taking this one out can alert the Forsworn at the top of the next flight. Before climbing again, at the top of the first flight, turn right and double back to find a novice-locked chest. Climb the third flight and start the next flight; now there are three Forsworn, two at the top of the fourth flight, and one above you to your right on higher ground. It is possible to take out the first two without the third finding you if your Sneak skill is high enough. The one above you is always an archer.

Ahead are more steps passing under three arches. Growing from the second of these is a [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") plant. As you pass under the third, there is a small Forsworn camp on your left with two open tents and two long wooden tables and benches between them. There is a Forsworn sitting at the tables and a second sitting in a chair in the farthest tent. Too much noise taking these out can alert a Forsworn wizard from a tent farther behind on the next plateau up. The first tent contains a single hay pile and a barrel, while the second tent contains the chair the Forsworn was sitting on.

Back on the path, you pass a stone pillar and a lit brazier on a stand on your left. Here the camp splits, with a single tent with the wizard on your left and the main part of the camp to your right. Inside the tent with the wizard are an unowned single bed, an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), and a food barrel with a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") and a copy of the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Reality & Other Falsehoods](/wiki/Skyrim:Reality_%26_Other_Falsehoods "Skyrim:Reality & Other Falsehoods")* on top and random boots beside it.

The main camp consists of four tents around a campfire with a [blacksmith forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") beside the nearest tent. Between the nearest tent and the forge is an adept-locked chest. Three Forsworn are guarding this area: one sleeping in the nearest tent, one wandering or sitting on a wooden bench, and the third behind on a raised area. On top of the forge anvil is a random [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"). Each of the tents contains a hay pile, with the first also containing a wooden bench, the next two also containing chairs, and the last also containing a dresser. There are also a wooden table with a mead barrel and sack on top and several other sacks and wooden benches around the camp. To the right of the last tent is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"). If you are here seeking the priest of Boethiah for the quest [The House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors"), he will be found kneeling in the tent next to the table with the mead barrel.

The path continues heading east toward Sundered Towers and the boss of this redoubt along with one other Forsworn and another raised area reached via stone stairs. Before that, traveling south down the side of one of the tents, you'll reach a melee practice area including two dummies and a wooden table holding a random [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"). On your left before reaching the stairs up to the boss is an archery practice area including two archery targets and a wooden table holding a random bow.

Climbing the stone stairs, you'll encounter the last Forsworn before the boss, and pass a wooden flight of stairs up to Sundered Towers, with a tree stump with a mora tapinella growth on the left of these stairs. Ahead, the Forsworn boss will be sitting on a throne, or if alerted, searching for you near an altar. The boss will have [Red Eagle's Fury](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle%27s_Fury "Skyrim:Red Eagle's Fury"). Past the throne and altar are a few steps down to another tent containing an unowned single bed, a boss leveled chest, a chair and wooden table holding a mead barrel, a copy of *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")*, a leveled stamina potion, a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"), and a lit lantern. This chest will hold any item you have been sent to Red Eagle Redoubt to find.

## Notes

- One [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") is 120 feet east of the entrance, slightly uphill.

## Bugs

- Looking at the world map when inside Red Eagle Ascent places your marker north-northwest of Markarth.
- If you have previously killed the leader of Red Eagle Redoubt and get the task to kill him again, you must reanimate the body and kill him a second time. You may get this task while trying to purchase a house in Markarth from the Jarl.
- The book *[Red Eagle's Rite](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle%27s_Rite "Skyrim:Red Eagle's Rite")* on the altar might clip beneath the surface, making it unreachable without the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
  - It is sometimes possible to move the book out of the altar by using an explosive spell such as [Fireball](/wiki/Skyrim:Fireball "Skyrim:Fireball").

Red Road Pass

**Red Road Pass** is a [giant camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps") south-southwest of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").

## Related Quests

- **[Bounty: Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Giant "Skyrim:Bounty: Giant")**: Kill a problematic [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") for a bounty reward. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Kill the Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Giant_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Giant (Jarl)")**: Do a favor for the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") by killing a [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

One [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") and one [mammoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth") occupy the camp. When you approach the camp for the first time, three randomly leveled [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") are attacking the giant and mammoth. A large campfire in the center of the camp features three [charred skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide") cooking on stakes. A large stone bowl and a set of steps are south of the fire; a [mammoth cheese bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Cheese_Bowl "Skyrim:Mammoth Cheese Bowl") and three large leather pouches filled with mammoth cheese can be found at the top of the steps. An unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") is in a hollowed-out tree to the west, with a patch of [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") growing next to the chest. The camp is decorated with the painted stones, [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes"), and mammoth skulls typical of giant camps. Several [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes also grow in the area.

## Overview

Red Scar Cavern

**Red Scar Cavern** is a [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") located east of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone"), occupied by the [Mythic Dawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Mythic_Dawn "Skyrim:Mythic Dawn") cult. The entrance is southeast of [Ruunvald Excavation](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruunvald_Excavation "Skyrim:Ruunvald Excavation") and northwest of [Champion's Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Champion%27s_Rest "Skyrim:Champion's Rest")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Umbra "Skyrim:Umbra"). [Vonos](/wiki/Skyrim:Vonos "Skyrim:Vonos"), the leader of the Mythic Dawn, can be encountered within. The cave is added by [The Cause](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation "Skyrim:Creation").

The cave has two interior zones: *[Red Scar Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Scar_Cavern#Red_Scar_Cavern "Skyrim:Red Scar Cavern")* and *[Mythic Dawn Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Scar_Cavern#Mythic_Dawn_Temple "Skyrim:Red Scar Cavern")*.

## Related Quests

- **[The Cause](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause_(quest) "Skyrim:The Cause (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause"): Investigate the activities of the [Mythic Dawn](/wiki/Lore:Mythic_Dawn "Lore:Mythic Dawn") cult.
- **[The Consequences](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Consequences "Skyrim:The Consequences")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause"): Enter the [Deadlands](/wiki/Skyrim:Deadlands "Skyrim:Deadlands") to face Dagon's champions.

### Exterior

The cave entrance is located in the [Velothi Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Velothi_Mountains "Skyrim:Velothi Mountains") of the northeastern Rift, across the valley from [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone"). It is located on the same mountain slope as another [Creation Club](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") location, [Champion's Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Champion%27s_Rest "Skyrim:Champion's Rest"), which is close by to the southeast. It can be reached easily by the player and their followers by climbing the mountain from the southeast and up onto the snowy plateau, or by jumping up the rocky slope directly to the west. A Mythic Dawn Guard keeps watch at the entrance, but can be deceived into letting you pass if you wear a full set of Mythic Dawn apparel (robes, gloves, and boots) as directed by the optional quest objective, and will respond with generic NPC dialogue if approached or spoken to. She is also present before you receive the letter that starts the questline, and will be hostile on sight. Once defeated, she can be looted for a full set of Mythic Dawn Robes which would otherwise only spawn during the quests.

### Red Scar Cavern

The large chamber

Just inside the entrance, there is a cluster of Blisterwort on the right side of the tunnel. The tunnel curves to the right at a torch sconce. As soon as you turn the corner, a Mythic Dawn Cultist is visible at the end of the tunnel where it opens into a large chamber. Like the guard at the door, the cultist will not attack if you are wearing your Mythic Dawn gear, and will give generic greetings if spoken to. Another blisterwort cluster is on the left near the end of the tunnel. To the right of the cultist is a cluster of White Cap and an unlocked boss-level chest (at least once you are leaving the cavern).
From here, a long path leads along the left wall and crosses to the other side via a natural bridge, over a pool at the bottom of a waterfall. The path turns left again on the other side, leading to a small campsite just below where you came in. A Guard patrols this area.
Either sitting beside the fire in a chair or sleeping in the right-hand tent is a Mythic Dawn Cultist. Several Fish Barrels around the fire are sources of ingredients and food.

After the campsite, the path spirals to the right again, leading you to and through the shallow pool you saw from above. There's a quicksilver ore vein on the east side. A narrow tunnel to north has been dug through the far wall. The tunnel winds its way down to a mining chamber, where two cultists dig at the floor. There are total of 6 iron ore veins available; another ore vein is visible but cannot be activated. The paths splits into two here: one leads straight ahead, while the other leads to the right. There are two barrels on the left.

The path to the right leads to a dead-end room with several more Mythic Dawn members milling about. Two Imp Stool clusters are along the right-hand wall, and the rightmost of two wooden platforms holds a chest.

On the other hand, the path going straight ahead leads to a deep mine shaft with a spiraling path of wood leading downward. On the third landing, a Quicksilver Ore vein is exposed in the wall. You will pass more Guards and Cultists as you proceed. Near the bottom, a tunnel leads to the right and to the door of the next chamber, the Mythic Dawn Temple. At the shaft floor, red mist steams above a chest and another Quicksilver Ore vein.

The door to the Temple is adept-locked, and none of the NPCs nearby can be asked for the key. However, one of the Mythic Dawn Guards patrolling the ramp carries the key and can be pickpocketed for it, A Mythic Dawn Guard stands at the entrance to the tunnel, with a clear line of sight, so sneaking if you choose to pick the lock may be prudent.

### Mythic Dawn Temple

The Oblivion Gate

As soon as you enter the temple, you will see that the tunnel ahead opens into a large chamber with a round dais of brick in the center. Two wooden platforms on either side hood minor loot.
A few steps in, you will be given the quest objective to defeat Vonos. Skorvild's brother, Sune, lies dead on an altar in the middle of the room; having clearly been stabbed with the Daedric dagger found next to him. Beyond is Vonos, supervising two Mythic Dawn Cultists on either side of him. The Cultists will come to Vonos's aid in the fight if they are not dispatched first by sneak attacks. To the right, a skeleton lies among collapsed rocks.

Immediately after Vonos is killed, an Oblivion Gate to the [Deadlands](/wiki/Skyrim:Deadlands "Skyrim:Deadlands"), the very one you were trying to close, will open on the far wall. [Vonos' Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Vonos%27_Journal "Skyrim:Vonos' Journal"), in his inventory, reveals he and his lord Dagon anticipated and counted on your intervention (as the Dragonborn) to unwittingly sacrifice Vonos so that the gate will reopen. A [new quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Consequences "Skyrim:The Consequences") will start, and you must activate the Gate to enter and stop the gathering forces preparing to invade from the other side.

On your successful return, the Vigil of Stendarr will be storming the cavern and wiping out the Mythic Dawn.

The cavern becomes a mine well-guarded by the Vigil. You can enter and leave its Oblivion gate as you wish to continue gathering ingredients and loot. Within the gate, the [spiddal stick](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiddal_Stick "Skyrim:Spiddal Stick") ingredient does not renew but its poison gas does reset. The [harrada](/wiki/Skyrim:Harrada "Skyrim:Harrada") ingredient resets but the [bloodgrass](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodgrass "Skyrim:Bloodgrass") does not. Several Daedric minions respawn there as well.

# Skyrim:Red Wave

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Ship: Red Wave ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Red+Wave)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Occupants | |
| Captain [Safia](/wiki/Skyrim:Safia "Skyrim:Safia") and her crew | |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[Legend of Krately House](/wiki/Skyrim:Legend_of_Krately_House "Skyrim:Legend of Krately House")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |

| Region | |

| Special Features | |
| # of [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") | 1 |

The Red Wave

The **Red Wave** is a pirate [ship](/wiki/Skyrim:Ships "Skyrim:Ships") docked at [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). It contains only one zone, *[Red Wave](#Red_Wave)*.

The Red Wave, with Solitude and the Blue Palace in the background

It is commanded by [Safia](/wiki/Skyrim:Safia "Skyrim:Safia"), a pirate captain targeted in a [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Safia "Skyrim:Kill Safia").

## Crew

| Crew |
| --- |
| [Dorian](/wiki/Skyrim:Dorian "Skyrim:Dorian")\*  [Eris](/wiki/Skyrim:Eris "Skyrim:Eris")  [Sabine Nytte](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabine_Nytte "Skyrim:Sabine Nytte")\*  [Safia](/wiki/Skyrim:Safia "Skyrim:Safia") (Captain)  [Xander](/wiki/Skyrim:Xander "Skyrim:Xander") |

\* These people are essential.

## Related Quests

- **[The Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:The Dainty Sload")**: Frame a [ship's](/wiki/Skyrim:Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:Dainty Sload") captain to get revenge for a [jilted merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur "Skyrim:Erikur").
- **[Kill Safia](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Safia "Skyrim:Kill Safia")**: Kill a [pirate captain](/wiki/Skyrim:Safia "Skyrim:Safia") on her own ship.

### Exterior

The Red Wave is moored at the Solitude Docks. During the quest [The Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:The Dainty Sload"), [Sabine Nytte](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabine_Nytte "Skyrim:Sabine Nytte") can be found on the deck, ready to supply you with illicit substances. With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, some [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies") can be found just off the gangplank, while farther down the docks is some [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and a fishing pole on a barrel, with a bucket of harvestable [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") on the dock.

### Red Wave

The interior of the ship is messy, with [empty wine bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle") all over the place and many [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels around the quarters. Upon entering the ships quarters on the deck level, you will normally find all of the crew except the captain. There is a stack of food barrels in the northeast corner with a basket on top containing a common book. Against the hull to the west is a square wooden table and a couple chairs, with a cupboard behind holding two [potions of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") and two random [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"). Against the bulkhead to the south is a second table and chairs.

To the left of the second table is a flight of stairs leading down to the middle deck. At the bottom of the stairs is a cupboard holding a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), three bulbs of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a single loose [coin](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a set of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"), and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"), with a small set of shelves holding four bottles of Nord mead to the left. There is a stack of food barrels farther to the left and a door to the right. Through the door is a bedroom containing a double bed in the southeastern corner, with an empty [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of the bed and a tall wardrobe against the south bulkhead. Against the north bulkhead is a long wooden table and chair.

The corridor follows the hull of the ship to the east, with stacks of barrels of food on both sides. Ahead is a large cupboard holding a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack"), an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), with a copy of the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Legend of Krately House](/wiki/Skyrim:Legend_of_Krately_House "Skyrim:Legend of Krately House")* on top, and a chair beside it against the north bulkhead. At this point, the corridor doglegs to the left.

Around the corner to the west is the dining area, with a long counter against the south bulkhead full of clutter, and a pair of random boots and a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") on the floor to the right. A cupboard against the same wall holds two more potions of minor healing and two random healing potions. Against the hull to the west is a long table with two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), a [pheasant breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast"), several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and pieces of cheese on top. Hanging above this table are two racks holding a total of five whole salmon, with a further three slightly to the right hanging from another rack over some food barrels. Against the north bulkhead is a long wooden table and two chairs, with two portions of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a raw rabbit leg, a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), three [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), two loaves of bread, and a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel") on top. To the right of this against the east bulkhead is another cupboard.

Continuing down the corridor, the first room on the right contains two owned single beds and a random [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"). There is an end table between the beds with a bottle of wine on top. The last room on the right contains two owned single beds and a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"). At the end of the corridor is a sleeping area with a total of four single owned beds against the walls. A set of shelves against the south bulkhead holds two potions of minor healing and a bottle of wine on top, and in front on the floor is a potion of minor stamina.

The last doorway on the left leads into a room and corridor with a wardrobe and a barrel against the south bulkhead on the immediate left. To the right of the wardrobe is a set of shelves holding two pieces of [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") and four [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), with a stack of food barrels farther to the right with two random potions on top of one of them. On the right as you enter is a long wooden table with a chair in front, with a food barrel to the left and a counter around the corner. Against the hull to the west is a series of sets of shelves. The first holds several mead barrels, a bottle of wine, and two bottles of Nord mead. The second holds fifteen [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"), a piece of iron ore, four [steel ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Ingot "Skyrim:Steel Ingot"), two [silver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot"), and a leather strip, with a pair of random boots on the floor to the right. Farther to the right, a smaller set of shelves holds a woodcutter's axe, two bottles of Nord mead, and an empty wine bottle, with a food barrel to the right with a random shield on top. The last set of shelves is filled with mead barrels, two bottles of Nord mead, and an empty wine bottle, with a sword on top. At the far end of the ship are more barrels of food on and under a large shelf at the rear, in front of which is a chair next to a crate with a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") on top. Opposite the shelf is a flight of stairs leading down to the cargo deck.

The cargo deck is full of food barrels, a single empty chest, and a master-locked [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Safe "Skyrim:Safe"), the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Wave_Safe_Key "Skyrim:Red Wave Safe Key") for which is carried by Sabine Nytte. In the safe, among the other loot is a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Balmora_Blue_Note "Skyrim:Balmora Blue Note") from someone named Dyryn. The note mentions a chest under the ship that contains something called [balmora blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Balmora_Blue "Skyrim:Balmora Blue"), which is needed for the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") [reputation quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:The Dainty Sload") in Solitude. The chest under the ship can be unlocked using another [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabine%27s_Footlocker_Key "Skyrim:Sabine's Footlocker Key") carried by Sabine.

## Notes

- The chest under the ship doesn't respawn.
- [Dorian](/wiki/Skyrim:Dorian "Skyrim:Dorian"), [Eris](/wiki/Skyrim:Eris "Skyrim:Eris"), and [Xander](/wiki/Skyrim:Xander "Skyrim:Xander") all have the same face paint of three stripes near their eye (Xander's may be hard to see, as his is light green on dark skin). Neither Safia nor Sabine Nytte share this trait.
- [Redwave](/wiki/Oblivion:Redwave "Oblivion:Redwave") was also the name of a unique [cutlass](/wiki/Oblivion:Cutlass "Oblivion:Cutlass") in *[Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Oblivion "Oblivion:Oblivion")*, a [quest](/wiki/Oblivion:The_Ghost_Ship_of_Anvil "Oblivion:The Ghost Ship of Anvil") reward for recovering a family heirloom from a [ship](/wiki/Oblivion:The_Serpent%27s_Wake "Oblivion:The Serpent's Wake") haunted by the ghosts of a crew murdered by a Dark Brotherhood member. It is unknown if there is any intended connection between the two.
- Crewmembers will not say their usual dialogue to you while inside the ship, and will act as if you are trespassing, but will never turn hostile or call for the guards.[*verification needed — May be a bug - See [talk page](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Red_Wave#NPCs_at_Location_Say_.22You_Shouldn.27t_Be_Here.22 "Skyrim talk:Red Wave")*]
- Version 1.3.3 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") allows 3 crew members to visit the [Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever"), making them available for brawl targets, and enabling several lines of unique dialogue that otherwise would have been unavailable.

## Bugs

- The beds here are owned by the wrong faction, preventing 5 of the pirates from being able to sleep, even though they'd go to and stand next to the beds when they were supposed to be.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.7, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Redbelly Mine

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Mine: Redbelly Mine ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Redbelly+Mine)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Occupants | |
| [Frostbite Spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| ShorsStoneRedbellyMine | |
| Region | |
| [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | |
| Location | |
| [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") | |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Ore "Skyrim:Ebony Ore") | 3 |

Redbelly Mine

**Redbelly Mine** is a small [ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") in western [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") initially containing [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). It contains only one zone, *[Redbelly Mine](#Redbelly_Mine)*.

The villagers describe the mine as the lifeblood of their settlement. It gets its name from the red mist said to flow throughout the mine; the mist's smell is described as similar to the sulfur vents in the volcanic tundra. The local [blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Skyrim:Blacksmith"), [Filnjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Filnjar "Skyrim:Filnjar"), will request your aid in clearing the mine of a group of frostbite spiders that recently invaded after the discovery of some [unusual ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore"). The miners will return to work after the mine has been cleared. [Grogmar gro-Burzag](/wiki/Skyrim:Grogmar_gro-Burzag "Skyrim:Grogmar gro-Burzag") will [buy iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore") from you, despite the fact that the mine contains only ebony ore.

## Related Quests

- **[Mine or Yours](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_or_Yours "Skyrim:Mine or Yours")**: Help [Filnjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Filnjar "Skyrim:Filnjar") by ridding the Redbelly Mine of [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider").
- **[Mine Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore")**: Get paid to [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") ore. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

A [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") and three pieces of [ebony ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Ore "Skyrim:Ebony Ore") are outside the mine entrance, which is west of [Filnjar's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Filnjar%27s_House "Skyrim:Filnjar's House").

### Redbelly Mine

Mine interior

The mine features one ebony ore vein on the ground on the descent just before the bottom level and two more ebony ore veins on the ground on the bottom level.

## Notes

- Redbelly Mine [appears](/wiki/Online:Shor%27s_Stone "Online:Shor's Stone") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online") as an ebony mine named "Shor's Stone Mine".
- Printed literature and dialogue in-game refer to this as an iron mine. Additionally, Grogmar gro-Burzag will buy iron ore from you, however the veins produce ebony ore. It is debated whether or not this is a bug or intentional.

## Bugs

- The thick red mist described by the miners living in Shor's Stone is not present; the mine is clear inside.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.
- There are several desiccated corpses in the mine despite Filnjar stating that nobody had been harmed by the frostbite spider infestation.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.
- The frostbite spiders may respawn. See the [quest page](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_or_Yours#Bugs "Skyrim:Mine or Yours") for more details.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.

## Maps

Redbelly Mine

# Skyrim:Redoran's Retreat

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Redoran's Retreat ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Redoran%27s+Retreat)) | | |

| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |

| Special Features | |

Redoran's Retreat

**Redoran's Retreat** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") west-northwest of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and a [dog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog "Skyrim:Dog"). It contains only one zone, *[Redoran's Retreat](#Redoran.27s_Retreat)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Bandits) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Bandits)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a bandit hideout. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The cave is on the plains west of Whiterun, at the end of a path that winds behind the rock into which the entrance is built. The entrance is thus concealed from the road between [Fort Greymoor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greymoor "Skyrim:Fort Greymoor") to the south and [Hamvir's Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Hamvir%27s_Rest "Skyrim:Hamvir's Rest") to the north. An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") is above the cave entrance to the southeast. Three unusable barrels and a crate are on either side of the entrance.

### Redoran's Retreat

Many fungi grow in the cave, comprising a total of twelve [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), two [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), two [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), one [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), two [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot"), and one [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap"). Food barrels and sacks, crates, and unusable barrels are found throughout the cave. The entrance leads into a passage that descends to the west, turns north, and passes a narrow braced section to enter the first chamber, which is lit by strings of lanterns. A set of shelves on the left holds four bottles of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), a bandit patrols near a rock pillar, and a [dog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog "Skyrim:Dog") (see [bugs](#Bugs)) wanders the area. Behind the pillar to the east is a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and a small wooden table to the left holding six loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") and two [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow").

Loot chamber

To the west is a narrow twisting passage that opens into a second chamber, where another bandit patrols and a bandit boss is seated at the rear. The chamber features a central rock pillar and two [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") hanging from the ceiling. Some wooden planking on the ground to the left supports three unowned bedrolls, and a small wooden table holds a bottle of ale. To the right is a small shelving unit holding a [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat") and two [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"). A second shelving unit to the right of the first holds a random [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), or [stamina potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"). At the rear of the chamber is a campfire with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit"). A copy of the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Last Seed, v8](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Last_Seed,_v8 "Skyrim:2920, Last Seed, v8")* sits on a crate to the east. To the right, an unlocked boss chest is protected by a [bear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") in front. The chest holds [Treasure Map IV](/wiki/Skyrim:Treasure_Map_IV "Skyrim:Treasure Map IV"). Along the north wall are many food barrels on more wooden planking.

## Notes

- The cave's name may refer to [House Redoran](/wiki/Lore:House_Redoran "Lore:House Redoran") of [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind").

## Bugs

- The dog will not respawn after being killed.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.

Redwater Den

**Redwater Den** is a [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") northwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). It contains two zones: *[Redwater Den](#Redwater_Den)* and *[Redwater Spring](#Redwater_Spring)*.

Beneath the shack is a drug den supplying [Redwater skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Skooma "Skyrim:Redwater Skooma"), which you will discover is a front for a group of vampires who use the particularly nasty and addictive drug to ensure a constant supply of blood from helpless addicts.

## Related Quests

- **[The Bloodstone Chalice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bloodstone_Chalice "Skyrim:The Bloodstone Chalice")**: Fill the [Bloodstone Chalice](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodstone_Chalice "Skyrim:Bloodstone Chalice") from the Bloodspring at Redwater Den.
- **[Culling the Beast](/wiki/Skyrim:Culling_the_Beast "Skyrim:Culling the Beast")**: Kill the thin-blooded [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request")**: Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

At first sight, this appears to be only a dilapidated shack, guarded by a [lookout](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Lookout "Skyrim:Redwater Lookout") out front. So long as you do not attack or approach as a full-fledged vampire, he will direct you into the den, assuming you are after a [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") fix. If you enter through a hole in the side wall of the shack, you will find another lookout seated in front of a fireplace. A copy of the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Battle of Red Mountain](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_Red_Mountain "Skyrim:Battle of Red Mountain")* and an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe") can be found on the nearby table. There is a [charred skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide") cooking on a spit in front of the fireplace. Somewhat hidden behind low walls in the corner is a trapdoor which leads into the interior of the den below. An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") is also nearby.

### Redwater Den

The trapdoor leads to a short passage and stairs down to an empty room, except for a [doorman](/wiki/Skyrim:Doorman "Skyrim:Doorman"), who warns you to keep your [weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") sheathed before opening the door and letting you in. There is a small room to the right of the guarded door, containing an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and two rows of weapon racks holding a couple of [iron swords](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"). The room through the guarded door and down more stairs features a [dealer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dealer "Skyrim:Dealer") behind an expert-locked, caged counter. She will sell you [Redwater skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Skooma "Skyrim:Redwater Skooma") and can even be persuaded to give you a free sample. Behind her is a door, which appears to lead to a basic storeroom. Past the counter is an alcove containing a well, two sets of shelves holding clutter, several crates, a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sack, and a whole [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") hanging above the well. To the right is a corridor with a slight red mist pervading it, and four rug-covered booths, with two on either side. An [attendant](/wiki/Skyrim:Attendant "Skyrim:Attendant") walks the corridor, while in each booth you'll find a skooma addict, including a [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Bandit (Dawnguard)"), a [Nobleman](/wiki/Skyrim:Nobleman_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Nobleman (Dawnguard)"), a dead [Addict](/wiki/Skyrim:Addict "Skyrim:Addict"), and an [Imperial Deserter](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Deserter "Skyrim:Imperial Deserter"). They have all been drinking Redwater skooma, with many [empty skooma bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Skooma_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Skooma Bottle") scattered over the floor of each booth. In the back right corner of the booth with the deserter are an [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield") and a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") that are free to loot. At the end of the corridor is an adept-locked gate, which the attendant warns you not to tamper with.

Attacking either the dealer or attendant, regardless of whether or not you are seen, will cause the other to become hostile. Both carry a bottle of Redwater skooma and a copy of a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Den_Backrooms_Key "Skyrim:Redwater Den Backrooms Key"), which opens most of the doors and gates in this zone. Inside the caged counter area is a [steel war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_War_Axe "Skyrim:Steel War Axe"), a low-quality bow, a quiver of arrows, a bottle of Redwater skooma, two [honey nut treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat"), a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), three loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), three loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), four bottles of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), three bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). All items apart from a bottle of ale are marked as owned, and taking them is considered [stealing](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime "Skyrim:Crime"). The storeroom behind the dealer contains four food sacks and a set of shelves holding a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick"), a bottle of alto wine, and four bottles of Nord mead. There is also a doorway through to an area with a couple of large vats and a dead [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers") lying in front of a sarcophagus with a concealed door behind, but no obvious way of opening it from this side.

From here, there are two options to continue forward: If you drink the Redwater skooma you got from the dealer, your vision will blur and fade to black, and you will wake up in a large dim room filled with vampires, with one and the dealer discussing the potency of the water from the Wellspring and its effects on creating [thralls](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire%27s_Thrall "Skyrim:Vampire's Thrall"). Attempting to speak to the vampire guarding the cell will cause him to tell you that he doesn't talk to his prey. Unlocking the gate nearby will alert the vampires and put you back on the same path as above, allowing you to continue forward from the same point.

Alternatively, you can pick the lock on the gate, either before or after dealing with the dealer and attendant. If they observe you doing so, they will instantly turn hostile. After dealing with them, you will be able to proceed through the gate. The room beyond contains a set of shelves holding a [cure poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Poison "Skyrim:Cure Poison") potion, two random [potions of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), an unlocked chest, and several sacks of food. Beside the shelves is a wooden table with a medium coin purse on top. A tunnel heads south, opening into a large multi-leveled room, with a vampire's thrall on a raised section opposite, and the same red mist rising above large boiling vats. A pair of wooden ramps on the left lead down to the cavern floor, and [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") grows from the walls around the cavern. At the bottom, on the right is a table with two open crates on top; one contains three bottles of skooma, and the other several empty skooma bottles. Under the wooden ramps are several sacks, crates, and barrels, as well as a random potion and an adept-locked chest. To the west is an adept-locked cell containing a dead novice [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer "Skyrim:Conjurer"), with a *[Spell Tome: Telekinesis](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Telekinesis "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Telekinesis")* beside them. This is where you will awaken if you choose to drink the Redwater skooma. Outside the cell is a cart containing a dead [Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") and a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Den_Backrooms_Key "Skyrim:Redwater Den Backrooms Key"). Paths lead toward the rear of the room along either side of a central raised section. At the front of the raised section, on the left is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") built into a wooden table, which holds a bottle of [Sleeping Tree sap](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Tree_Sap "Skyrim:Sleeping Tree Sap"), a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), and a total of four bowls of [moon sugar](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Sugar "Skyrim:Moon Sugar"), three of which are in an open crate. At the rear of the raised section is a set of shelves holding a [beehive husk](/wiki/Skyrim:Beehive_Husk "Skyrim:Beehive Husk"), a [bee](/wiki/Skyrim:Bee "Skyrim:Bee"), a sample of hanging moss, a [swamp fungal pod](/wiki/Skyrim:Swamp_Fungal_Pod "Skyrim:Swamp Fungal Pod"), a bowl of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"), a bowl of moon sugar, a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), a [skeever tail](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever_Tail "Skyrim:Skeever Tail"), a piece of [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), a bowl of [ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm"), a [silverside perch](/wiki/Skyrim:Silverside_Perch "Skyrim:Silverside Perch"), a bowl of [spriggan sap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan_Sap "Skyrim:Spriggan Sap"), and a sample of [hawk feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hawk_Feathers "Skyrim:Hawk Feathers").

At the rear of the room is an alcove featuring two unowned single beds separated by a dresser. There is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") and a barrel of food at the foot of the right-hand bed. On the right is a ramp leading up, passing an empty set of shelves. At the top, you will find a vampire and a thrall near a [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), complete with a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"). The passage leading to the forge is filled with crates and an unowned bedroll, with a copy of *[The Aetherium Wars](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Wars "Skyrim:The Aetherium Wars")*[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") on one of the crates. Beside the workbench is a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"), while to the left of the forge is a square wooden table holding a bottle of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead"), a [knife](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Knife "Skyrim:Specialty Gear"), and a [fork](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Fork "Skyrim:Specialty Gear"). Around to the east is a raised bridge that crosses over the previous multi-leveled room. On your right is a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") and some cheese, with a bunch of [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam") hanging above. The lever to lower the bridge is in another alcove to the north. At the entrance to the alcove is a crate holding a potion of minor magicka and a potion of minor stamina opposite a long wooden table holding a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), a helmet, a joint of [cooked beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooked_Beef "Skyrim:Cooked Beef"), and two lockpicks.

On the far side of the bridge, the passage turns north and descends, passing a wooden table with two more pickaxes on top. Beyond this the chamber widens, with an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") and a [gold ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein") in the southeast corner. Ahead the architecture changes, and begins to resemble that of an ancient [Nord barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins"). A doorway to the north gives access to a small area containing two large [urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") and one [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") among the rubble from a cave-in, with a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") in front that triggers [poison darts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") to shoot from either side. The passage continues to the south, where you will find a thrall and a [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") on guard, and a couple of [oil lanterns](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Oil Lanterns") hanging above them. The passage ends with a crate holding two random potions of healing and a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel") beside a concealed door, which is opened using a pull chain.

The tunnel beyond twists and turns before opening into a room with an open coffin in the center, which if you are a vampire, you are free to sleep in. There are two [death hounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Hound "Skyrim:Death Hound") and a leveled vampire guarding the room. To the west is a fireplace, with an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") built into a sideboard to the right of it. On the sideboard are a random filled [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") and a [ruined book](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book"). Opposite this, to the east is another concealed door, with the chain in a recess on the right. Behind the door is a small alcove with a plinth holding a random enchanted weapon, and a sideboard behind it with a [potion of cure disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Potion of Cure Disease") and a random potion of magicka on top. Back in the first room, to the south is a set of shelves holding a burial urn. A passage heads north, past two open sarcophagi with dead draugr lying in front of them. A flight of stairs climbs to a pair of double iron doors with a puddle of red water seeping underneath it. The doors lead to *Redwater Spring*.

### Redwater Spring

The Bloodspring

Through the doors, the puddle continues off to the left before disappearing under some rubble. Ahead at a T-junction is a long sideboard filled with candles and in the middle a lit brazier, with a banner hanging above it. To the right of the brazier is a medium coin purse, [Venarus Vulpin's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Venarus_Vulpin%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Venarus Vulpin's Journal"), and three loose coins. The journal, written by the vampire who rediscovered the **Bloodspring**, explains his reasoning behind setting up the skooma racket. To the west is a lowered gate blocking the only doorway, with no visible means to open it. To the east is a window, with another lowered gate to the right. As you approach the window, you will overhear someone asking why they don't just drink directly from the spring, rather than using the skooma addicts. There are two sideboards, one on either side of the window. The right-hand sideboard has three more loose coins on top. To the north is a balcony with a wooden paneling surround, and a passage leading down to the room below. There is a large cage to the south containing death hounds, with a leveled vampire and a thrall wandering the room. Hanging from the ceiling above them are several oil lanterns, with an [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slick "Skyrim:Oil Slick") underfoot. There are two stone pillars in the room, with a wooden ramp spiraling around the left-hand pillar leading up to a stone bridge crossing to the right-hand pillar. By the start of the wooden ramp is a candle holder with a random potion of healing and a small coin purse on top, and under the ramp are an urn and two food sacks.

Take care, as there is a [trap door](/wiki/Skyrim:Trap_Door "Skyrim:Trap Door") in the floor a couple of paces into the room. It opens and drops you into a [spike pit](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Pit "Skyrim:Spike Pit"). There is a passage leading away from the stakes, but [swinging blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades") start slicing across the passage as soon as you drop into the pit. At the far end of the passage is an unlocked chest with a [tension cable](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") attached, which triggers poison darts from behind unless disarmed before opening. The passage turns to the right to end at the bottom of a wooden spiral staircase, with a large urn, a barrel of [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), and three food sacks underneath. The stairs lead back up to the room containing the caged death hounds. Beside the stairwell, against the east wall is a narrow table holding a copy of *[Fall from Glory](/wiki/Skyrim:Fall_from_Glory "Skyrim:Fall from Glory")* and a [potion of resist fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire"). In the northeastern corner is a firepit with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front, which is flanked by a food barrel with a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") on top and a wrapped draugr corpse. There are several empty sets of shelves, sideboards, and a long blood-soaked stone table around the room.

Climbing the ramp and crossing to the top of the right-hand pillar, you will see to the north a balcony with an unlocked chest on it. A single word of [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") or the [Vampire Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Lord "Skyrim:Vampire Lord") "Bats" ability will allow you to reach it. Alternatively, you can reach the chest by jumping up the slightly inclined slope of the ruined wall, then jumping onto the wooden beam sticking out of the wall, then onto the platform where the chest is. Crossing from the first pillar over the bridge to the east will bring you to a balcony with several open upright sarcophagi, thrones, and sets of shelves holding clutter as well as two burial urns. At the western end of the balcony is the window seen from the other side; a chain to the left opens both lowered gates seen at either end of the previous room. There are two sideboards nearby to the south, by the now open gate at this end. On one is a small coin purse, while the other holds an unlocked chest.

Through the other open gate at the far end to the west, you enter brightly lit catacombs, where the passage turns north and starts to climb. At the top you will find yourself in a large, two-level chamber containing several upright [coffins](/wiki/Skyrim:Coffin "Skyrim:Coffin"), guarded by two death hounds, two leveled vampires, and three [infected bones](/wiki/Skyrim:Infected_Bones "Skyrim:Infected Bones") traps. The stairs to the upper level are on your left after you turn left past the first infected bones trap. In the southern corner on one of the upper sections is an alchemy lab, while in the northwestern corner is a lowered gate blocking access to a smaller room. The chain to open it is on the right.

The room beyond is in a half circle with three closed doors: one is across the room, and the remaining two are on either side of a central raised section. The raised section features a lit brazier, a [human heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Human_Heart "Skyrim:Human Heart"), a piece of [human flesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Human_Flesh "Skyrim:Human Flesh"), a bowl of frost salts, a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), two bowls of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), and a random empty soul gem, with yet another alchemy lab at the front, and an urn nearby. The wooden door to the right of the raised section has a tension cable that will trigger a spear trap from the wall in front of you, and opens into a small alcove containing an unlocked chest. The wooden door to the west opens into another alcove containing the bones of a skeleton and a sideboard holding a potion of cure disease and a burial urn. The iron door to the left of the raised section opens into more brightly lit catacombs. Take care, as the floor of this section holds pressure plates that trigger three [spike walls](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall"), with two that swing down from the ceiling, and one that swings horizontally across the passageway. Around the corner are two more pressure plates, these triggering multiple [flamethrowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Flamethrower_Statue "Skyrim:Flamethrower Statue") from the walls, in front of another iron door.

This door opens into a huge chamber containing two leveled vampires including the boss vampire, [Venarus Vulpin](/wiki/Skyrim:Venarus_Vulpin "Skyrim:Venarus Vulpin") (or a generic boss-leveled vampire if you haven't started the quest [The Bloodstone Chalice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bloodstone_Chalice "Skyrim:The Bloodstone Chalice")), as well as their thralls and skeletons. Venarus Vulpin will be carrying the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Wellspring_Key "Skyrim:Redwater Wellspring Key") to the iron door at the end of this chamber, which leads to a large grotto containing the Bloodspring, required for the quest The Bloodstone Chalice. There are several upright coffins around the room and on either side of a throne against the western wall. Opposite the throne is an arcane enchanter, with an altar behind it holding a random [light armor cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor"), Venarus Vulpin's [research](/wiki/Skyrim:Venarus_Vulpin%27s_Research "Skyrim:Venarus Vulpin's Research") regarding the Bloodspring, and a bowl containing a random filled soul gem, an [amethyst](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst "Skyrim:Amethyst"), a [garnet](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet"), an [emerald](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald "Skyrim:Emerald"), and sixteen loose coins. To the right of the altar is an unlocked boss-level chest, and along the rear of the room is a long stone table with two bottles of Redwater skooma on top. Beyond the table is a passage leading to a master-locked iron door, which opens with the key carried by Venarus Vulpin into the cavern containing the Bloodspring.

‎Drinking directly from the spring as a vampire gives you the effect [Tainted Blood of the Ancients](/wiki/Skyrim:Tainted_Blood_of_the_Ancients "Skyrim:Tainted Blood of the Ancients"), while as a non-vampire it will infect you with [Sanguinare Vampiris](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguinare_Vampiris "Skyrim:Sanguinare Vampiris") and another [disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Diseases "Skyrim:Diseases"). Repeated drinking will eventually infect you with every disease in the game (which can all be cured simultaneously with a single [Cure Disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Cure Disease") potion). However, if one decides drink as a [Werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Lycanthropy "Skyrim:Lycanthropy"), you will not contract any disease due to the character with Lycantrophy having [Disease Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Disease "Skyrim:Resist Disease"). At the rear of the cavern is a door back into Redwater Den.

This door opens into a room with a row of open upright sarcophagi along each side and two sideboards flanking a concealed door at the end. There are four dead draugr that can be looted on the floor, and an empty random soul gem on the sideboard to the right. A pull chain next to the concealed door opens it to the Redwater skooma dealer's storeroom, behind the caged counter; from there, you can retrace your steps to the ladder and trapdoor you entered through. If you have not already killed them, the doorman near the den exit and the two lookouts outside will become hostile to you. (See below for a workaround)

## Notes

- Without the *[Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")* add-on installed, the ruined house is still present, and its contents appear identical. However, it is instead inhabited by two leveled bandits and their [dog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog "Skyrim:Dog"), and the trapdoor to the den doesn't exist.
- All key-locked gates in this location can be unlocked with the [Redwater Den Backrooms Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Den_Backrooms_Key "Skyrim:Redwater Den Backrooms Key"), which can be found on the dealer, the attendant, and some of the vampires and thralls within. An additional copy can be found on a table next to the prisoner cell in the first cave-like chamber.
- This area exists and can be cleared no matter which side you align with for the *Dawnguard* [main quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Quests "Skyrim:Dawnguard Quests"). Venarus Vulpin will still be here if you side with the Dawnguard and never come here for the Volkihar quest, but [Stalf](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalf "Skyrim:Stalf") ‎and [Salonia Caelia](/wiki/Skyrim:Salonia_Caelia "Skyrim:Salonia Caelia") will not, as they only appear here during the quest The Bloodstone Chalice.
- After completing the quest The Bloodstone Chalice, or after siding with the Dawnguard and clearing the dungeon, every remaining living inhabitant (such as the doorman and lookouts) except the dealer will turn into a vampire's thrall, though they won't be hostile to you.
- After you clear the dungeon, the vampires, thralls, death hounds, and Venarus Vulpin will all respawn, though the other occupants (such as the addicts and attendant) won't, even if you didn't kill them earlier. If you are unaffiliated with either main faction in the *Dawnguard* main quest, Vulpin will instead respawn as a Master Vampire.
- If a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") is present when you drink the Redwater skooma the dealer gave you, your follower will transfer into the cell with you.

## Bugs

- The Redwater Skooma may give you frost resistance, even though it shouldn't.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.3, fixes this bug.
- Should the Redwater Lookout NPCs be startled, their dialogue "I'm getting out of here!" comes up as being said by Vampire's Thrall, not Redwater Lookout.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.4, fixes this bug.
- The occupants of here don't use their aliased names when the control quest is active because the aliases were never set to store the text.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.4, fixes this bug.
- Your follower will always transfer into the cell when you drink the Redwater skooma, even if you told them to wait somewhere else.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.
- After you kill Venarus Vulpin, his corpse may display "Master Vampire" instead of his name. **?**

## Maps

- 

  Redwater Den
- 

  Redwater Spring

# Skyrim:Reeking Tower

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Dwarven Ruin: Reeking Tower | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 18 |
| Occupants | |
| [Frostbite Spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| BlackreachZcell01 | |
| Region | |
| [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") | |
| Location | |
| Northern part of Blackreach | |

Reeking Tower

**Reeking Tower** is a small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") occupied by [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). It is along the north-northwest boundary of Blackreach, near several spider nests and north of a quarry comprising four [geode veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Geode_Vein "Skyrim:Geode Vein").

### Exterior

The tower is approached from the northeast. The path crosses a bridge over a crevasse featuring several spider egg sacs, then circles the tower clockwise, passing two [crimson nirnroots](/wiki/Skyrim:Crimson_Nirnroot "Skyrim:Crimson Nirnroot"), one by the southwest side of the tower, and the other by the north side of the tower near the entrance.

### Reeking Tower

Upon entering, you emerge in a corridor that rises and spirals counterclockwise. At the top of the second ramp, there are several spider egg secs, one of which can be harvested, with a few loose [spider eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Egg "Skyrim:Spider Egg") on the ground. At the top of the next ramp is a [frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") and another harvestable egg sac. To the west is a doorway into a typical wide Dwemer corridor, with pillars along the edges and a ramp up to a T-junction. There is another frostbite spider at the T-junction. As you pass the doorway, there is a third harvestable egg sac in the corner to the north. There is a frostbite spider to the north up a ramp that ends at a cave-in. The last frostbite spider inside the tower guards a lift that is down the west ramp on the left. Before taking the lift, continue to the west to find an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") concealed behind some webbing at another cave-in.

The lift takes you to an otherwise inaccessible ledge high above the main cavern of Blackreach, west of the main entrance to the tower. There are two frostbite spiders on the ledge, and a third that descends from the cavern ceiling. There are two harvestable spider egg sacs on the ledge: one is to the right as you leave the lift, and the second is around a corner to the north where the ledge widens and the spider descends. There is also a crimson nirnroot growing in the middle of the ledge. It is possible to climb down from the ledge without the use of [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal"), with the easiest starting point to the right of the first egg sec where you leave the lift. Obviously, care must be taken.

## Notes

- It is possible to kill all three of the frostbite spiders at the top exterior of the tower before entering using a bow or ranged magic.

## Maps

- 

  Reeking Tower

# Skyrim:Refugees' Rest

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

Refugees' Rest

**Refugees' Rest** is a small ruined [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Towers "Skyrim:Imperial Towers") east of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals").

## Related Quests

- **[Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination_(B) "Skyrim:Animal Extermination (B)")**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to clear out a beast den. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Walkthrough

The *Decree of Monument*

The tower is easily found by taking the road northeast from Windhelm, passing [Brandy-Mug Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Brandy-Mug_Farm "Skyrim:Brandy-Mug Farm"), [Hlaalu Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Hlaalu_Farm "Skyrim:Hlaalu Farm"), and [Hollyfrost Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Hollyfrost_Farm "Skyrim:Hollyfrost Farm") and continuing toward the border with [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind"). It is the last building before the border is reached and was once an important meeting place for refugees from Morrowind following the [Red Year](/wiki/Lore:Red_Year "Lore:Red Year"). However, years of abandonment and neglect have taken their toll on the tower, as its foundation is beginning to collapse and it has tipped and sunken into the ground.

The doorway into the tower on the southwestern side leads into the ground floor, where bones and rubble are strewn about along with copies of *[Ancestors and the Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestors_and_the_Dunmer "Skyrim:Ancestors and the Dunmer")* and *[The Firsthold Revolt](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Firsthold_Revolt "Skyrim:The Firsthold Revolt")*. A stone spiral staircase leads up to the top of the tower, which features an adept-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") but nothing else of interest.

Outside on the northeastern side of the tower is a small graveyard partially surrounded by a broken stone wall. At its base along the road is a plinth holding the *[Decree of Monument](/wiki/Skyrim:Decree_of_Monument "Skyrim:Decree of Monument")*, issued by all the [jarls](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of Skyrim to commemorate the tower's past.

Many [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes and varieties of [mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") grow around the tower. On the opposite side of the road to the entrance are the remains of a wagon partially buried in the snow.

## Bugs

- The animals may not respawn. **?**
