# Skyrim:Rejoining the College

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by multiple users, *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Demonfang](/w/index.php?title=User:Demonfang&action=edit&redlink=1 "User:Demonfang (page does not exist)"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Make amends for breaking the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") rules.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Automatic after committing a serious [crime](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime "Skyrim:Crime") against a College member OR Automatic after committing a serious [crime](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime "Skyrim:Crime") to any citizen |
| Location(s): | [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") |
| Reward: | Reentry into the College |
| ID: | MGRejoinQuest |

*"Ah, yes. There was an incident, wasn't there?"*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Find [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir").
2. Pay the fine.

## Detailed Walkthrough

This quest will automatically begin after killing another College member, provided you have already joined the College yourself. The quest description will inform you that you have been suspended from the College. It is a very short quest, requiring you only to find [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir") in the College and speak to him. Tolfdir lectures you about behaviors that the College finds inappropriate, and states that he will have your suspension lifted if you pay a fine. Paying the fine results in immediate reinstatement into the College's ranks and completion of the quest.

## Notes

- This quest may begin even if you have completed the College of Winterhold questline and became Arch-Mage.
- Murder is the only crime that will trigger this quest; lesser crimes, such as pickpocketing and theft, will not.
- The fine for the first incident is 250 gold. If you commit another crime and receive the quest again, the fine climbs to 500 gold. It increases to 750 gold for the third incident, and 1,000 gold for each incident thereafter.
- Tolfdir increases the amount of the fine according to the number of past incidents, not their severity. Therefore, as long as it's your first such incident, you can murder a non-essential member of the College and only have to pay 250 gold, one quarter of the bounty that would be charged in any hold for murder.
- Tolfdir may instead be found in [Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal") if you are between starting [Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal") and finishing [Hitting the Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Hitting_the_Books "Skyrim:Hitting the Books").
- The [Wizard Duel](/wiki/Skyrim:Wizard_Duel "Skyrim:Wizard Duel") random encounter may lead to your expulsion from the College, triggering this quest.

## Bugs

- [J'zargo](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27zargo "Skyrim:J'zargo") and [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") will not trigger this quest if killed.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=18972))
-  If you have an old version of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") installed [J'zhar](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27zhar "Skyrim:J'zhar") will incorrectly trigger this quest if raised and you kill him.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.6, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=20995))
-  If you have an old version of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") installed [Endrast](/wiki/Skyrim:Endrast "Skyrim:Endrast") will also trigger this quest if raised and you kill him.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.6, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=21011))
- This quest will trigger even if you kill a raised dead member of the College, among the ones that can trigger this quest. You can do this multiple times with the same corpse if you re-raise it with [the power](/wiki/Skyrim:Powers#The_Ritual_Stone "Skyrim:Powers") of the [The Ritual Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ritual_Stone "Skyrim:The Ritual Stone"), since it doesn't reduce the corpses it raises to an ash pile after wear off.
- Sometimes killing yourself will trigger this quest. On PC, it can be accomplished, by typing the console command `player.placeatme 00000007` (Dovahkiin's base ID), then killing the newly created NPC.

## Quest Stages

| Rejoining the College (MGRejoinQuest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 5 |  | I've been suspended from the College for my actions. I should speak with Tolfdir about having it lifted. *Objective 5:* Speak with Tolfdir |
| 10 |  | I've been suspended from the College for my actions, and will need to pay Tolfdir 250 gold in order to have it lifted. *Objective 10:* Give Tolfdir 250 gold to lift your suspension |
| 20 |  | I've been suspended from the College for my actions, and will need to pay Tolfdir 500 gold in order to have it lifted. *Objective 20:* Pay Tolfdir 500 gold to lift your suspension |
| 30 |  | I've been suspended from the College for my actions, and will need to pay Tolfdir 1000 gold in order to have it lifted. *Objective 30:* Pay Tolfidr 1000 gold to lift your suspension |
| 200 | ☑ | I have paid Tolfdir and my suspension from the College has been lifted. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MGRejoinQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MGRejoinQuest`.

# Skyrim:Relics of the Crusader

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article could benefit from an image**. See [Help:Images](/wiki/Help:Images "Help:Images") for information on how to upload images. Please remove this template from the page when finished. |

|  |  |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Location(s): | [Four Skull Lookout](/wiki/Skyrim:Four_Skull_Lookout "Skyrim:Four Skull Lookout") |
| Reward: | Crusader's Relics (see [below](#Reward)) |
| ID: | ccMTYSSE001\_StartupQuest\_Alt |
| Added by: | [Divine Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Divine_Crusader "Skyrim:Divine Crusader") |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | |  | **Next →** [The Pilgrim's Path](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pilgrim%27s_Path "Skyrim:The Pilgrim's Path") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | → Next | [The Pilgrim's Path](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pilgrim%27s_Path "Skyrim:The Pilgrim's Path") | | |

## Quick Walkthrough

**Note**: This quest does not appear in your journal.

1. Travel to [Four Skull Lookout](/wiki/Skyrim:Four_Skull_Lookout "Skyrim:Four Skull Lookout").
2. Kill [Eigorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Eigorn "Skyrim:Eigorn") and [Oren](/wiki/Skyrim:Oren "Skyrim:Oren") and take the Crusader's Relics.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Upon arriving at [Four Skull Lookout](/wiki/Skyrim:Four_Skull_Lookout "Skyrim:Four Skull Lookout") for the first time, you will encounter hostile bandits wearing the Relics of the Crusader and the Reforged Relics of the Crusader. The former are the holy relics of [Pelinal Whitestrake](/wiki/Lore:Pelinal_Whitestrake "Lore:Pelinal Whitestrake"), while the latter are a new set of light armor pieces styled after the originals.

Four Skull Lookout is a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") den. In addition to the regular bandit enemies, [Eigorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Eigorn "Skyrim:Eigorn"), [Oren](/wiki/Skyrim:Oren "Skyrim:Oren"), [Remy](/wiki/Skyrim:Remy "Skyrim:Remy") and [Viparth](/wiki/Skyrim:Viparth "Skyrim:Viparth") can be found here. They are your targets, as Eigorn and Oren possess the Relics and will use them in battle. Kill the thieves and loot all twelve of the new items from their bodies to complete the quest. You can optionally also loot [Viparth's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Viparth%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Viparth's Journal") for some explanation as to how bandits are wearing these divine relics.

### Reward

The items you receive from this quest are as follows:

- [Mace of the Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Mace of the Crusader"), [Shield of the Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Shield of the Crusader"), [Boots of the Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Boots of the Crusader"), [Cuirass of the Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Cuirass_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Cuirass of the Crusader"), [Gauntlets of the Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Gauntlets of the Crusader"), [Helm of the Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Helm_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Helm of the Crusader")
- [Sword of the Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Sword of the Crusader"), [Fastened Shield of the Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Fastened_Shield_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Fastened Shield of the Crusader"), [Reforged Boots of the Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Reforged_Boots_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Reforged Boots of the Crusader"), [Reforged Cuirass of the Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Reforged_Cuirass_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Reforged Cuirass of the Crusader"), [Reforged Gauntlets of the Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Reforged_Gauntlets_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Reforged Gauntlets of the Crusader"), [Reforged Helm of the Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Reforged_Helm_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Reforged Helm of the Crusader")

If you commit any crime whatsoever, at any point in the game, you will receive a message advising that your crimes have made you unfit to wield the Crusader's Relics. Attempting to wear any of the relics after this point will result in a significant debuff to your stamina and health regeneration and your carry weight. The quest [The Pilgrim's Path](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pilgrim%27s_Path "Skyrim:The Pilgrim's Path") will be automatically started, directing you to nine remote [shrines](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines "Skyrim:Shrines") to repent for your sins and regain the ability to wear this equipment.

## Notes

- At release, this quest appeared in your journal and was started automatically upon installing the [Divine Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Divine_Crusader "Skyrim:Divine Crusader") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"), or as soon as you left [Helgen Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen_Keep "Skyrim:Helgen Keep") as a new character. This was changed in the [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition").
- Unlike in *[Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Oblivion "Oblivion:Oblivion")*, the Crusader's Relics could originally be used by evil characters, including the bandit thieves. This was changed with the Anniversary Edition update, which added the quest The Pilgrim's Path.
  - With the Anniversary Edition update, an explanation was added as to how bandits were able to wield the Crusader's Relics: the two bandits, Eigorn and Oren, were new recruits and hadn't committed any crimes yet.
- Prior to the Anniversary Edition update, there were no named bandits at this location. Eigorn and Oren were instead two generic [Bandit Thief](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Thief "Skyrim:Bandit Thief") enemies.

## Quest Stages

| Relics of the Crusader (ccMTYSSE001\_StartupQuest\_Alt) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Bandits have stolen the fabled Relics of the Crusader. I should find and reclaim them. *Objective 0:* Obtain the Relics of the Crusader  *Objective 10:* Obtain the Reforged Relics of the Crusader |
| 75 | ☑ | I've reclaimed the Relics of the Crusader. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccMTYSSE001_StartupQuest_Alt stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccMTYSSE001_StartupQuest_Alt`.

# Skyrim:Reluctant Steward

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Find a new steward for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth"), or finding [Varona Nelas](/wiki/Skyrim:Varona_Nelas "Skyrim:Varona Nelas") (see [notes](#Notes)) |
| Location(s): | [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)"), [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") |
| Reward: | 500 gold, Access to the [staff enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_Enchanter "Skyrim:Staff Enchanter") and the Black Book *[The Hidden Twilight](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Hidden_Twilight_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Hidden Twilight (book)")* |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth")) =1 ([Drovas Relvi](/wiki/Skyrim:Drovas_Relvi "Skyrim:Drovas Relvi")) |
| ID: | DLC2TT1 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | |  | **Next →** [A New Debt](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Debt "Skyrim:A New Debt") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | → Next | [A New Debt](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Debt "Skyrim:A New Debt") | | |

Varona Nelas, dead in the ash wastes

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") in [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)").
2. *(Optional)* Talk to [Elynea Mothren](/wiki/Skyrim:Elynea_Mothren "Skyrim:Elynea Mothren") or [Ulves Romoran](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulves_Romoran "Skyrim:Ulves Romoran").
3. Find [Varona Nelas](/wiki/Skyrim:Varona_Nelas "Skyrim:Varona Nelas").
4. Find a [new steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Drovas_Relvi "Skyrim:Drovas Relvi") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").
5. Return to Neloth for your reward.

### The Missing Steward

The eccentric founder of [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)") is master-wizard [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") who works his few employees hard and expects them to carry out even the most unfair duties. His current steward is named [Varona Nelas](/wiki/Skyrim:Varona_Nelas "Skyrim:Varona Nelas") and is constantly challenged by the demanding wizard, who has a weak spot for tea brewed from [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"). Once you have spoken with Varona and left Tel Mithryn at least once, she will be nowhere to be found. Pay a visit to Neloth in his [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)") and he will wander around saying: *"Where is that ash sucking steward of mine? Varona!"* As it turns out, the wizard is quite hungry and will task you with finding Varona: *"Well find her. Tell her I want apple cabbage stew, with some canis root tea."* He will not take 'no' for an answer, regardless of which option you choose:

*"Where is that ash sucking steward of mine?"*

**Why don't you just make your own tea?**
*"What? Make my own tea? I am a master wizard of the House Telvanni. Other people make tea for me."*

**Hey, I'm not your servant.**
*"Obviously not, or you would have a cup of tea in your hands. I supposed you want to be asked nicely. Very well. Please, oh hero of Skyrim. Please find Varona. I shall be ever so grateful."*

**Of course, Master Neloth. As you command.**
*"Finally. Someone who recognizes my importance around here."*

Neloth will then return to his daily routine and you will have no choice but to search for the missing steward. No map marker will be provided, so look around for the other inhabitants of the settlement.

### Ash Spawn Attack

Outside, Neloth's apprentice [Talvas Fathryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Talvas_Fathryon "Skyrim:Talvas Fathryon") will refuse to talk about Varona until you complete his quest [From the Ashes](/wiki/Skyrim:From_the_Ashes "Skyrim:From the Ashes"). Even so, he will point you towards local apothecary [Elynea Mothren](/wiki/Skyrim:Elynea_Mothren "Skyrim:Elynea Mothren") for information. Alternatively, you can talk to [Ulves Romoran](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulves_Romoran "Skyrim:Ulves Romoran") inside [Tel Mithryn Kitchen](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_Kitchen "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn Kitchen"). Both he and Elynea will tell you that Varona just departed for [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") in order to gather supplies. Bringing this information to Neloth will net you nothing, as he only cares if his tea is hot or not. After speaking to Elynea or Ulves, a map marker will now point you towards Varona who will most likely (see [bugs](#Bugs)) be in the area west of the [Sun Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sun_Stone "Skyrim:Sun Stone"), not far from a dead [reaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver"). Unfortunately, she never made it to Raven Rock as she was killed by three [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn"), all of them still gathered around her dead body. Kill the ash spawn and investigate her body for a quest update.

### A Popular Wizard

Back in his tower, Neloth will have a hard time showing any emotion when you tell him the sad news: *"Dead? Well that's annoying. How did she die?"* When you tell him about the ash spawn attack, he will reflect a bit but will quickly get over it: *"There are more and more of those things showing up around here lately. I suppose you'll have to find me a new steward. Try Raven Rock. They are in awe of me there. I'm sure almost anyone would be willing to serve me."* Three options will be available and the two top options will always lead to the third:

*"Try [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"). They are in awe of me there."*

**You can't just order me around.**
*"Well, somebody needs to get me a new steward. It might as well be you. But if you don't want to help a master wizard of House Telvanni, possibly earning his favor, you're a fool."*

**What's in it for me?**
*"So gaining the favor of a Telvanni wizard isn't enough? I suppose I'll have to pay you. Heroes. They get greedier every century."*

**What kind of a person should I look for?**
*"Hmm. Excellent question. Once word gets out, there will be a lot of people to choose from. Someone with a brilliant mind and robust physique that is blindly obedient would be ideal. Oh, and they need to know how to brew tea. Ulves always waters it down."*

Once again, you will have to obey orders, so travel to Raven Rock, where a huge amount of the [citizens](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock#Raven_Rock_People "Skyrim:Raven Rock") will have an extra dialogue option, namely to consider a position as Neloth's new steward.

### Unexpected Reactions

When you begin asking the inhabitants of Raven Rock if they want a new job as Neloth's personal steward, it soon becomes quite clear that the wizard may have overestimated both his reputation and popularity, as shown in the table below:

| Name | House | Response |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **[Bralsa Drel](/wiki/Skyrim:Bralsa_Drel "Skyrim:Bralsa Drel")** | [Abandoned Building](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Building "Skyrim:Abandoned Building") | *"Would he give me skooma? I might do it for some skooma."* (see [bugs](#Bugs)) |
| **[Rirns Llervu](/wiki/Skyrim:Rirns_Llervu "Skyrim:Rirns Llervu")** | [Abandoned Building](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Building "Skyrim:Abandoned Building") | *"I'd saw off my own leg for a septim, but you couldn't pay me enough to do that."* |
| **[Dreyla Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Dreyla_Alor "Skyrim:Dreyla Alor")** | [Alor House](/wiki/Skyrim:Alor_House "Skyrim:Alor House") | *"My father needs me. He can't run his market stand alone. Besides, Neloth is as loony as a skooma addict. He wanted my father to import a white mammoth. Alive!"* |
| **[Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor")** | [Alor House](/wiki/Skyrim:Alor_House "Skyrim:Alor House") | *"Don't be ridiculous. Who would run this place? You should ask around at The Retching Netch. Someone there might be crazy enough, or drunk enough, to do it."* |
| **[Aphia Velothi](/wiki/Skyrim:Aphia_Velothi "Skyrim:Aphia Velothi")** | [Caerellius House](/wiki/Skyrim:Caerellius_House "Skyrim:Caerellius House") | *"Me? I hardly think so. That Telvanni wizard is unhinged. I heard he tries to drink the ash."* |
| **[Crescius Caerellius](/wiki/Skyrim:Crescius_Caerellius "Skyrim:Crescius Caerellius")** | [Caerellius House](/wiki/Skyrim:Caerellius_House "Skyrim:Caerellius House") | *"Nah. I don't think so. Anyway, I don't think he'd take on anyone that isn't a dunmer."* |
| **[Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory")** | [Glover Mallory's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory%27s_House "Skyrim:Glover Mallory's House") | *"Ha ha ha! Gods, that's rich. Work for Neloth. Ha ha ha!"* |
| **[Garyn Ienth](/wiki/Skyrim:Garyn_Ienth "Skyrim:Garyn Ienth")** | [Ienth Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ienth_Farm "Skyrim:Ienth Farm") | *"And leave my farm? No thank you."* |
| **[Milore Ienth](/wiki/Skyrim:Milore_Ienth "Skyrim:Milore Ienth")** | [Ienth Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ienth_Farm "Skyrim:Ienth Farm") | *"Not on your life! I'd sooner try to swim back to Windhelm."* |
| **[Adril Arano](/wiki/Skyrim:Adril_Arano "Skyrim:Adril Arano")** | [Morvayn Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvayn_Manor "Skyrim:Morvayn Manor") | *"I'm perfectly content with my current position."* |
| **[Cindiri Arano](/wiki/Skyrim:Cindiri_Arano "Skyrim:Cindiri Arano")** | [Morvayn Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvayn_Manor "Skyrim:Morvayn Manor") | *"I could never leave Adril behind, and he will never leave Lleril. Besides, I'd never work for Neloth! I heard he cut the heart out of his [former apprentice](/wiki/Skyrim:Ildari_Sarothril "Skyrim:Ildari Sarothril")."* |
| **[Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri")** | [The Retching Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch") | *"Are you nuts? Neloth is crazy! I hear he talks to mud crabs."* |
| **[Mogrul](/wiki/Skyrim:Mogrul_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Mogrul (Dragonborn)")** | [The Retching Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch") | *"Ha, ha, ha! Not on your life! I'd have to be truly desperate to do that."* |
| **[Mirri Severin](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirri_Severin "Skyrim:Mirri Severin")** | [Severin Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Severin_Manor "Skyrim:Severin Manor") | *"Now why would I want to work for House Telvanni? Besides, Neloth is a madman!"* |

*"There's got to be more to life than sweeping and cleaning all day."*

While Neloth seems to be the laughingstock in town, three citizens will prove helpful and point you towards [Drovas Relvi](/wiki/Skyrim:Drovas_Relvi "Skyrim:Drovas Relvi") who works as a cook at the [Retching Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch"). These citizens are [Dreyla Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Dreyla_Alor "Skyrim:Dreyla Alor"), [Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri"), and [Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory") (see [notes](#Notes)).

### The Unhappy Cook

Drovas is quite unhappy with working at the Retching Netch, as Geldis Sedri doesn't allow him to drink on the job. When presented with the idea of acting as Neloth's new steward he will therefore accept right away: *"Uh... you mean leave Raven Rock? For good? To go work for a crazed Telvanni wizard? Sure. Just let me get my things. On second thought, nevermind. I can get new stuff."* Drovas will then set off at a running pace and head towards Tel Mithryn where he will begin his life anew, now a steward for Neloth. If you speak to Drovas before he leaves the inn, he will simply say *"I'm off to take up my new position with Master Neloth."* When you tell Neloth, he will hatefully comment: *"That Drovas man? I suppose he'll do. He makes dreadful canis root tea though. But, I should be grateful. Here, take this for your efforts. Oh, and you may use my staff enchanter if you want."*

He will then hand you the reward, a leveled amount of gold and a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_Enchanter_Key "Skyrim:Staff Enchanter Key") that provides free access to his unique [Staff Enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_Enchanter "Skyrim:Staff Enchanter") in the locked southern chamber. The chamber also holds his [Black Book](/wiki/Lore:Black_Book "Lore:Black Book"), *[Hidden Twilight](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Hidden_Twilight_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Hidden Twilight (book)")*. Lastly, you can now hear the eccentric wizard calling for his steward: *"Where is that lazy steward of mine? Varona! No, wait. She's dead. Drovas!"* You can also ask Neloth how Drovas is doing, and he will respond: *"The man makes a dreadful cup of canis root tea. However, he seems run the place well enough. Oh. Were you fishing for a compliment? A sign of gratitude? Don't waste your time. Those things are for the weak and foolish."* You can also ask Drovas how things are going, and his response will be: *"Neloth is a real task master. And the tea. The thrice damned tea! I don't think I'll ever learn to make it properly."*

## Notes

- Drovas' eagerness to accept the position also seems driven by a desire to escape a debt owed to [Mogrul](/wiki/Skyrim:Mogrul_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Mogrul (Dragonborn)"), a debt that you are now [expected to pay](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Debt "Skyrim:A New Debt"). Be prepared for a confrontation the next time you return to Raven Rock.
- If you start the quest by examining the dead body of Varona, Neloth will instead say: *"What! Who's going to make my tea? Why do these things always happen to me? Well, don't just stand there. Go find me another steward. I'm sure there's plenty of people in Raven Rock to choose from."* He will then send you to Raven Rock (start the walkthrough from [this section](#Unexpected_Reactions)).
- Glover Mallory will only help you find a new steward if you have completed [Meet the Family](/wiki/Skyrim:Meet_the_Family "Skyrim:Meet the Family").
- After the quest, you'll no longer be able to ask Drovas if he wants to test out [Sadri's Sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sadri%27s_Sujamma "Skyrim:Sadri's Sujamma") if [It's All In The Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:It%27s_All_In_The_Taste "Skyrim:It's All In The Taste") is active.
- This quest is normally a prerequisite for [Put A Fork In It](/wiki/Skyrim:Put_A_Fork_In_It "Skyrim:Put A Fork In It")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Sheogorath "Skyrim:Staff of Sheogorath") and [The Arms of Chaos](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:The Arms of Chaos")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:Arms of Chaos") due to the requirement to use the Staff Enchanter during those quests. However, you can avoid this quest if you have access to a Staff Enchanter elsewhere, such as the one added by the [Myrwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch "Skyrim:Myrwatch") Creation.

## Bugs

- If this quest is finished and the [Sun Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sun_Stone "Skyrim:Sun Stone") has been cleansed, Drovas's sleep package will always be active, and therefore he will be found sleeping indefinitely in [Tel Mithryn Steward's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_Steward%27s_House "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn Steward's House").
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.5, fixes this bug.
- Varona will sometimes not end up dead in her intended place, but instead somewhere around Tel Mithryn. The quest will progress normally upon examining her body.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
- [Bralsa Drel](/wiki/Skyrim:Bralsa_Drel "Skyrim:Bralsa Drel") claims she'll take the job for some [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma"), but even if you have some, you can't give it to her. There is an unused line of dialogue in the game data that suggests it may have been possible one point, however she mistakenly refers to Neloth as a female, and the line might have been deliberately made unavailable: *"Skooma! Lovely skooma. But I'd sooner give it up than go work for her*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*. That dunmer is crazy!"*
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
- If this quest is finished and the [Sun Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sun_Stone "Skyrim:Sun Stone") has been cleansed, Drovas's sleep package may still have him trying to sleep at the Retching Netch, even though he doesn't work there anymore.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.3, fixes this bug.
- [Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory") is supposed to be able to provide a lead for who could be Steward for Neloth, but his dialogue was mistakenly assigned to [Crescius Carellius](/wiki/Skyrim:Crescius_Caerellius "Skyrim:Crescius Caerellius").
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, fixes this bug.
- Sometimes Varona's body will show up without clothes.
- Varona can die in a place where you might be unable to get to her body, preventing you from completing the quest. For example, the quest marker will show her location, but she might have been set under an obstacle such as a rock. Another possibility is that her body simply never appears and you do not get a quest marker guiding you to her. The quest marker for her body has also appeared off the map of Solstheim, with just an arrow pointing the direction (this area is inaccessible through normal means). Reloading a previous save will not fix the issue. (Note: the quest marker being off the map may be fixed by reloading to a save before Varona died)
  - If this bug occurs, you will unable to retrieve the black book *[The Hidden Twilight](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Hidden_Twilight_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Hidden Twilight (book)")* from the staff enchanting room. You will also be unable to enchant [staves](/wiki/Skyrim:Staves "Skyrim:Staves"), as this staff enchanting room is the only one in the entire game (excluding Creation Club content).
  - To get her body from under the object, try using the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout. In some cases her body will be blown clear, and you can finish the quest.
  - Another way to get her body from under an object is to use a power or spell with reanimating abilities. Once she is reanimated, you can kill her and finish the quest.
  -  Use the console by typing in `prid xx0177DD` (where 'xx' is a number that depends on how many DLCs you have installed, determine it by opening the console and clicking on an object in Solstheim) and then `moveto player` to move her directly to you, or `moveto xx017E8E` to move her to where she was supposed to be.

## Quest Stages

| Reluctant Steward (DLC2TT1) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 150 |  | Neloth has asked me to locate his steward, Varona Nelas. She is probably somewhere around Tel Mithryn. *Objective 150:* Find Varona |
| 170 |  | Neloth has asked me to locate his steward, Varona Nelas. Last time anyone in Tel Mithryn saw her, she was on her way to Raven Rock. |
| 200 |  | Neloth asked me to locate his steward, Varona Nelas. I found her body on the road to Raven Rock. *Objective 200:* Tell Neloth that Varona is dead |
| 210 |  | I found Neloth's steward, Varona, dead on the road to Raven Rock. *Objective 200:* Tell Neloth that Varona is dead |
| 300 |  | I found Varona's dead body on the road to Raven Rock, apparently killed by ash spawn. Now Neloth wants me to find someone in Raven Rock willing to be his new steward. *Objective 300:* Find a new steward |
| 310 |  | Neloth asked me to locate his steward, Varona Nelas. I found her dead body on the road to Raven Rock. Now Neloth wants me to find someone in Raven Rock willing to be his new steward. I've heard Drovas Relvi might be willing. |
| 400 |  | Neloth asked me to locate his steward, Varona Nelas. I found her dead body on the road to Raven Rock. Neloth sent me to Raven Rock to find a new steward. I found Drovas Relvi, who seemed very eager to take the position. *Objective 400:* Report back to Neloth |
| 500 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 90, 100.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2TT1 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2TT1`.

# Skyrim:Repairing the Phial

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Acquire the materials necessary to repair the [White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |

| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(quest) "Skyrim:The White Phial (quest)") [The Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:The Throat of the World") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(quest) "Skyrim:The White Phial (quest)") [The Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:The Throat of the World") | | |

The White Phial

## Quick Walkthrough

**Note**: This quest can only be started after gaining full access to the [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World") during the quest of the [same name](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:The Throat of the World").

1. Talk to [Quintus Navale](/wiki/Skyrim:Quintus_Navale "Skyrim:Quintus Navale") about repairing the White Phial.
2. Find the items required.
3. Return to Quintus Navale.

### One Last Attempt

[Nurelion](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion "Skyrim:Nurelion") on his deathbed

A few days after the [failed attempt](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(quest) "Skyrim:The White Phial (quest)") to help the alchemist [Nurelion](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion "Skyrim:Nurelion") realize his life's ambition (so long as you have unlocked the top of the [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World") by completing the [similarly named quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:The Throat of the World")), a [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") will seek you out with a [letter from Quintus Navale](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Quintus_Navale "Skyrim:Letter from Quintus Navale") (Nurelion's assistant) who has grave news, and seeks your help.

Head to Windhelm and locate [The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(place) "Skyrim:The White Phial (place)") in the market district. In there, Nurelion will still be in his bed, coughing and slowly dying. Quintus, however, will be more than ready to explain what is needed to repair the Phial: *"I have some thoughts. There are three crucial elements. Some may be easier to find than others. On the top of the Throat of the World is a patch of Unmelting Snow. No heat can touch it. Then we need the tusk of a mammoth, ground to a fine powder as only the giants know how. The final step is tricky. It requires the briar heart from a Forsworn of the Reach. If you can bring me these materials, the Phial can again be made whole."*

### Gathering the Items

Although he claims not to be as skilled as his master, Quintus will provide quite a bit of information on each of the items to explain why they are needed for his plan to repair the Phial:

| Item | Description |
| --- | --- |
| [Mammoth Tusk Powder](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Tusk_Powder "Skyrim:Mammoth Tusk Powder") [SR-icon-misc-MammothTuskPowder.png](/wiki/File:SR-icon-misc-MammothTuskPowder.png) | *"The ivory produced by those beasts is as hard as iron. But the giants have found ways to make it yield. They're able to grind it down so fine that it can be infused into the lattice of packed snow. The finished material has the delicate nature of fresh powder snow, but the strength of the hardest steel."* |
| [Unmelting Snow](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmelting_Snow "Skyrim:Unmelting Snow") [SR-icon-misc-UnmeltingSnow.png](/wiki/File:SR-icon-misc-UnmeltingSnow.png) | *"On top of the Throat of the World is a patch of snow that's never melted. They say the Greybeards taught it to ignore the sun, and heat simply washes over it. The original Phial was made from this snow. We'll only need a small bit for the repairs."* |
| [Briar Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Briar_Heart "Skyrim:Briar Heart") [SR-icon-ingredient-Briar Heart.png](/wiki/File:SR-icon-ingredient-Briar_Heart.png) | *"The final tempering of the Phial was performed with a type of old magic that's been lost since the Dragon War. The nearest modern incarnation of it is the strange rituals practiced by the Forsworn. With the heart of one of their Briar Warriors, I can lock the Phial's magic into its physical form. It's difficult to explain to the layman -- forgive me if I begin waxing alchemic."* |

Repairing the Phial

*"Master, look. It's the Phial."*

The rather unremarkable patch of Unmelting Snow can be found at the [Throat of The World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World"). Mammoth Tusk Powder is in a large vat beside the giants at [Stonehill Bluff](/wiki/Skyrim:Stonehill_Bluff "Skyrim:Stonehill Bluff"), and it is possible to pick up the powder without aggravating the giants. Note that the Mammoth Tusk Powder is different from the alchemy ingredient [Powdered Mammoth Tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Powdered_Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Powdered Mammoth Tusk"). A Briar Heart can be acquired from a dead [Forsworn Briarheart](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Briarheart "Skyrim:Forsworn Briarheart") and can be obtained from multiple Forsworn camps; one will be marked on your map.

### Repairing the Phial

When you return to Quintus with the three items, he will be relieved: *"Thank the gods. I'll get to work on the Phial straight away."* He will then leave his spot behind the counter and get to work at the [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") in the corner. Once he is finished repairing the Phial, he will head upstairs, eager to show his master what he has accomplished:

**Quintus**: *"Master, look. It's the Phial."*
**Nurelion**: *"What? How?"*
**Quintus**: *"It doesn't matter. Look, it's refilling with your tonic as we speak."*
**Nurelion**: *"Marvelous."*

Nurelion will then die peacefully and Quintus will turn around and express his gratitude: *"He is gone. But thanks to you, he died knowing his life's work was not in vain."* When you say you are sorry to hear that old Nurelion is dead, he will respond: *"As am I. You acted very nobly in helping my master realize his life's work. Thank you for that. As for myself, I've always been content to simply be an alchemist. I fear keeping the Phial would just remind me of Nurelion's obsession, and how it consumed him. Here, keep it. You are as much a part of its legend now as [Curalmil](/wiki/Skyrim:Curalmil "Skyrim:Curalmil") was. I hope it brings you the happiness that my master desired."*

### The Reward

You have a number of options for which kind of liquid the Phial will be able to regenerate:

- I'd like it to have the power of healing. ([restore health](/wiki/Skyrim:Restore_Health "Skyrim:Restore Health") for 100 points)
- I want to resist the forces of magic. (20% [resist magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Magic "Skyrim:Resist Magic") for 60 seconds)
- I want to be tougher in battle. (+20 [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Stamina "Skyrim:Fortify Stamina") for 300 seconds)
- I want to strengthen my magical skills. (+20 [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Magicka "Skyrim:Fortify Magicka") for 300 seconds)
- I want to deal more damage in battle. (+50% to [one-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_One-handed "Skyrim:Fortify One-handed") damage for 60 seconds)
- I want to be better hidden in the shadows. (20% [harder to detect](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Sneak "Skyrim:Fortify Sneak") for 60 seconds)

You will be given [The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)"), which functions as a potion of the nature you chose. Drinking it moves it to the Miscellaneous section of your items menu as The White Phial (Empty). It refills after 24 hours. Attempting to use the empty phial duplicates it, but only one phial will fill after the time has passed.

## Notes

- Nurelion's dead body will disappear after some time. You can find his remains inside the coffin in the [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Windhelm) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Windhelm)").
- After Nurelion is dead, many of the contents of his store will be free for the taking, including many useful ingredients. You can also loot his key to the shop.
- If you are on an assignment for the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") involving The White Phial (the shop), complete it and turn it in prior to completing this quest. Nurelion's passing at the end of the quest, though not caused by you, will still trigger you to fail the job for "killing".
- It is possible to reach the peak of the Throat of the World early, by using a horse to climb the mountain; however, doing so will not let you start this quest early - you have to advance the main questline in order to get the letter from Quintus Navale.

## Bugs

- The courier may fail to deliver the note from Quintus even after you've gained access to the Throat of the World, making this quest unavailable.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
  - This bug is likely to occur if you have killed the Forsworn leader of Red Eagle Redoubt before (probably during [find Red Eagle's sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn_(quest) "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn (quest)")). If so, use the following [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") commands: `prid 2c9a0` and `resurrect 1` to resurrect him. Wait a few real-world minutes then fast travel to any major city and the courier should show up. If the courier still fails to appear, try the command `setstage MS12b 10`.
- The courier bearing Quintus' letter may fail to arrive and instead loiter at [Sarethi Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Sarethi_Farm "Skyrim:Sarethi Farm"). Traveling there and speaking to him may start the quest.
  - You may be able to find the courier by using the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command `player.moveto 39fb7` to move yourself to him.
- After you have started the quest, when you pick up a briar heart, the quest may not update, and no option to turn it in will appear when talking to Quintus. This can be caused by already having a briar heart in your inventory when you start this quest.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4.15, fixes this bug.Note that this recurs in Skyrim Special Edition and appears not to be fixed by the Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch (4.1.0)
  - Keep the briar heart in your inventory, collect the other two ingredients and use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command: `setstage MS12b 60`.
- The quest may not start if you already have unmelting snow, mammoth tusk powder, or a briar heart in your inventory when attempting to talk to Quintus.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4.15, fixes this bug.
- If you finish the quest with more than one briar heart in your inventory, the remaining hearts will still be marked as quest items, making them impossible to drop or store.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9.26.0.8, fixes this bug.
- If you already have a briar heart in your inventory before starting the quest, it will not be given to Quintus at the end of the quest; it will not be marked as a quest item immediately, but any briar hearts retrieved later on will become a quest item.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
  -  If you don't want to install the unofficial patch, you can manually reset all of the items' *quest item* status through the console command `resetquest MS12b`, followed by `completequest MS12b`.
- Sometimes talking to Quintus will not update the quest, and trying to talk to him again will yield a result of "this person is busy". **?**
  - Use the `setstage` console command to advance the quest.
- When you return to Quintus with all three ingredients, there may be no dialogue option to turn them in, meaning you are stuck with an uncompleted quest, the three quest items, and no White Phial.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
  - This may happen because the [Mammoth Tusk Powder](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Tusk_Powder "Skyrim:Mammoth Tusk Powder") was not marked as a quest item, allowing you to drop or store it before you brought it to Quintus. If you stored it, retrieve it and talk to Quintus again.
  - This can also happen if you've used the briar heart in a potion. Find or buy another and the quest will continue.
  -  If you can't retrieve it, you can manually spawn it by using the console command `player.additem 6bc10 1`.
- If you have initiated the quest to [find Red Eagle's sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn_(quest) "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn (quest)"), the same Forsworn Briarheart might be the target of both quests. It will carry both Red Eagle's sword and a briar heart. However, even if you pick up both, it will only complete the Red Eagle quest. You will need to find a different Forsworn camp to complete the briar heart part of this quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, addresses this issue. An alias on this quest was requiring him to be alive. This alias is now marked as optional since it is not necessary for that one particular Briarheart Warrior to be the target.
- If you have killed the Forsworn Briarheart leader at the designated camp prior to this quest, collecting his heart may not clear the quest objective leaving you stuck. **?**
  -  The following console command will fix this issue: `setobjectivecompleted ms12b 50 1`. NOTE: "50" is the objective number NOT the quest stage!
- It is possible to receive more than one White Phial from Quintus if, after choosing what type of solution you want in the Phial, you quit the conversation and re-initiate it.
- After Quintus Navale shows him the Phial, Nurelion suddenly stands up and acts like he's dying, and you can't finish the quest.
  - You can avoid this happening by removing his essential status before Quintus shows him the Phial. Open the console and type in `SetEssential 14148 0`.

## Quest Stages

| Repairing the Phial (MS12b) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Nurelion's assistant, Quintus, believes he's found a way to repair the White Phial. *Objective 10:* Speak to Quintus Navale |
| 30 |  | Nurelion's assistant, Quintus, believes he's found a way to repair the White Phial, and has enlisted me to track down some materials for him. *Objective 30:* Retrieve the Unmelting Snow  *Objective 40:* Find some Mammoth Tusk Powder  *Objective 50:* Take a Forsworn Heart |
| 60 |  | *Objective 60:* Return to Quintus Navale |
| 100 | ☑ | I helped repair the White Phial in time for Nurelion to see it before he died. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MS12b stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MS12b`.

# Skyrim:Reparations

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Make reparations for breaking the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") rules.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Automatic after assaulting against to member [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") |
| Location(s): | [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") |
| Reward: | Restored membership of the Thieves Guild |
| ID: | TGBan |

Vex isn't pleased with your behavior, but she'll forgive you... for a price

## Quick Walkthrough

1. After offending the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), wait for them to calm down.
2. Talk to [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") and pay 1,000 gold.
3. Pay your way back into the guild.

## Detailed Walkthrough

You get this quest for offending the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), usually by assaulting/murdering one of their members, attempting to steal from them and getting caught or murdering someone during a guild quest. This will result in an expulsion, meaning no more training sessions or fencing services and limited conversations with guild members. To rejoin the guild, speak to [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") in [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon"), who will reprimand you and demand 1,000 gold as reparations. Return when you have the money and you will be let back into the guild.

If you've been expelled for assault, you may need to wait 48 hours outside the Ragged Flagon for hostile guild members to calm down.

## Bugs

- This quest may incorrectly trigger as a result of doing Dark Brotherhood quests.

  **Mod Notes**: Could also have something to do with having previously triggered Reparations (see [discussion](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Reparations#Dark_Brotherhood_quest_interference_and_large_bounty_problem.3F "Skyrim talk:Reparations")), but DB seems more likely.

## Quest Stages

| Reparations (TGBan) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've been banned from the Thieves Guild for breaking one of their cardinal rules. Once everyone in the Guild calms down, I should ask Vex what she recommends I do to make reparations. |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Speak to Vex |
| 30 |  | *Objective 20:* Bring gold to Vex (1000) |
| 200 | ☑ | I've paid my reparations and I have been reinstated to the Thieves Guild. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TGBan stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TGBan`.

# Skyrim:Repentance

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Help [Illia](/wiki/Skyrim:Illia "Skyrim:Illia") prevent her mother [Silvia](/wiki/Skyrim:Silvia "Skyrim:Silvia") from transforming into a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Illia](/wiki/Skyrim:Illia "Skyrim:Illia") |
| Location(s): | [Darklight Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower "Skyrim:Darklight Tower") |
| Reward: | [Staff of Hag's Wrath](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Hag%27s_Wrath "Skyrim:Staff of Hag's Wrath"), Illia as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Illia](/wiki/Skyrim:Illia "Skyrim:Illia")) |
| ID: | dunDarklightQST |
| Suggested Level: | 8 |

In the heat of Repentance

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Help [Illia](/wiki/Skyrim:Illia "Skyrim:Illia") reach the top of [Darklight Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower "Skyrim:Darklight Tower").
2. Defeat [Silvia](/wiki/Skyrim:Silvia "Skyrim:Silvia") on the top of Darklight Tower.

### A View to a Kill

The standoff

While travelling southwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), you may come across the ominous [Darklight Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower "Skyrim:Darklight Tower"). The guards in Riften are concerned about the place, stating: *"There's a foul presence coming from Darklight Tower... Some say the place is home to necromancers."*
When you enter the tower, you will be witness to a murder; an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [elemental mage](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageElemental "Skyrim:CombatMageElemental") has killed a witch. Seeing you, the mage, [Illia](/wiki/Skyrim:Illia "Skyrim:Illia"), tries to explain. Illia is near desperate, trying to escape the depravity of the coven within the tower. She was tasked with locating a human sacrifice so that her mother, [Silvia](/wiki/Skyrim:Silvia "Skyrim:Silvia"), can conduct a ritual to become a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"). Illia takes responsibility for the horrific things she has done in the tower, but makes a stand against taking an innocent life. She asks you to help her stop her mother's vile plan.

### Witch Hunt

Hagraven duel

If you agree to help her, Illia will start ascending the stairs, but will typically wait for you to catch up. On each level of the tower you'll encounter a [witch](/wiki/Skyrim:Witch "Skyrim:Witch") or [hag](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag") and an assortment of creatures such as [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), or [trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll"). Despite being casters, witches and hags are very weak and Illia, unlike them, is a very capable [frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Damage "Skyrim:Frost Damage") mage.
Battling through to the third floor, you may notice a locked door requiring a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower_Closet_Key "Skyrim:Darklight Tower Closet Key") on the way up. Illia has this key, and it can be pickpocketed, however, it's probably not worth the effort to pickpocket her or kill her for this, as the room only contains a cupboard with several potions. Once the quest is over, you can take Illia's key freely if you ask her to be a follower.
Stopping at a portcullis, Illia warns of a hagraven ahead. Pulling the lever will open the gate and allow you to slay the hagraven, as well as any other creatures on this level. A copy of the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") skill book *[2920, Sun's Dawn, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Sun%27s_Dawn,_v2 "Skyrim:2920, Sun's Dawn, v2")* is on the table by the hagraven's tent.

Continue into [Darklight Chambers](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Chambers "Skyrim:Darklight Chambers"), killing the witches. Here you will come to a master-locked door. Illia says that one of the hagravens carries the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower_Key "Skyrim:Darklight Tower Key"). She then hopefully asks if you can pick the lock. If you decide to retrieve the key from the hagraven, Illia will wait at the door for your return. The hagraven you are looking for is in the room off the corridor to the east, accompanied by a hag. Once you have the locked door open, Illia will resume the ascent to the top of the tower. You will meet more hags and creatures on your way up, as well as a copy of the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") skill book *[Mystery of Talara, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystery_of_Talara,_v3 "Skyrim:Mystery of Talara, v3")* on a table on one of the landings.

### The Demise of Silvia

A daughter's betrayal

Once you reach the top, Illia explains that her mother is just on the other side of a closed door; and Illia has a plan. She's going to present you to her mother as the sacrifice and while her mother is preparing, you and Illia can kill her mother together. While a difficult decision, Illia seems resolute. She would rather her mother die at her hands than have her turn into a monster.
Open the door to an open area where Silvia has prepared the ritual. Illia will begin the charade and Silvia will ask you to sit on a chair in order for the ritual to begin. At this point you can either outright kill Silvia or trust that Illia isn't merely playing you for a fool and sit in the chair. If you do sit in the chair, Silvia will begin the ritual and Illia will make good on her promise to stop her.
Silvia is fairly tough, compared to the residents of the tower, but no match for you and Illia combined. Once Silvia's path has ended, Illia will ask for no sympathy; she plans to leave this all behind. Illia thanks you and allows you to keep her mother's [Staff of Hag's Wrath](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Hag%27s_Wrath "Skyrim:Staff of Hag's Wrath") as payment for your help. You can ask Illia if she would like to come with you and she seems eager at the chance to, *"do some good for a change"*. She will then be your [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"). Before leaving, be sure to pick up the Destruction skill book *[Horror of Castle Xyr](/wiki/Skyrim:Horror_of_Castle_Xyr "Skyrim:Horror of Castle Xyr")*, sitting atop the table next to the tent.

## Bugs

- If Silvia is killed before Illia initiates a conversation, Illia will start the conversation regardless and waits indefinitely for a response unless you go sit in the chair (at which point she simply turns and leaves and will not agree to join you).
  -  This can be fixed by `prid 0004B47C`, `moveto player`, `resurrect 1` and finally `enable`.
- If you pick the lock from the top instead and enter via Darklight Chambers, you can fight your way down to Darklight Tower. In there, however, you will eventually come to a gate you can't open from that side. The only way is to turn back, while killing some monsters that have respawned. Upon re-entering Darklight Chambers, Illia will suddenly be at your side (even if you've never met her) and the game will treat you as if you were mid-quest.
  -  The quest can still be completed the normal way, but if you want to be there from the beginning, set the stage to 0 (`setstage dunDarkLightQST 0`) and re-enter from the bottom floor (Darklight Tower) instead. If you entered from the top you probably already killed Silvia as well; to fix that, see the previous point.
- If you go through the stages, go through the door to where the initiation is to start, and a hagraven and a hag in Illia's Mother's place Illia will continue into battle alone killing both of them. If you encounter this Silvia will not appear, not starting the initiation process. Illia will then return to the top door and not offer any options, leaving the quest unfinished.
  -  This can be fixed by `prid 0004B47C`, `enable`. Silvia will appear and act hostile but will not initiate combat. Once you attack, Illia will join the fight and the quest will be marked as completed once Silvia is dead.
  - If this happens, an earlier save must be loaded to complete the quest, before entering Darklight Tower. First, find a way to the top of the tower on the Skyrim map. The gate will be barred, but you can go over it. Kill the hag and hagraven. Return to the bottom of the tower and enter. Proceed normally, and when you reach the top with Illia, her mother will be there.
- This quest was erroneously set up in the story manager, which can cause it to restart itself unexpectedly. In addition, the quest has an unnecessary "allow repeat stages" flag which further exaggerates the problem. It ALSO has multiple shutdown stages selected, which doesn't work.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.6, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Repentance (dunDarklightQST) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I met a witch named Illia in Darklight Tower. She was supposed to obtain a sacrifice for her mother to perform an evil ritual, but rebelled. Illia wants me to help her get to the top of the tower so she can stop her mother. *Objective 10:* Help Illia reach the top of Darklight Tower |
| 20 |  | I met a witch named Illia in Darklight Tower. She was supposed to obtain a sacrifice for her mother to perform an evil ritual, but rebelled. Illia wants me to help her get to the top of the tower so she can stop her mother. At the top of the tower, Illia told me her plan. She planned to present me as the sacrifice to her mother to gain the element of surprise. |
| 25 |  | *Objective 20:* Defeat Illia's mother at the top of Darklight Tower |
| 35 |  | *Objective 20:* Defeat Illia's mother at the top of Darklight Tower |
| 40 | ☑ | I met a witch named Illia in Darklight Tower. She was supposed to obtain a sacrifice for her mother to perform an evil ritual, but rebelled. Illia wants me to help her get to the top of the tower so she can stop her mother. At the top of the tower, Illia told me her plan. She planned to present me as the sacrifice to her mother to gain the element of surprise. We attacked an killed her mother. Illia told me to take her mother's staff from as a reward. |
| 50 | ☑ |  |
| 60 | ☒ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 5, 8, 9, 12, 14, 15, 16, 18, 30, 55.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunDarklightQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunDarklightQST`.
