Planning the attack with Hadvar; Ft. Kastav in background to the east

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Report to [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") at [Winterhold Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Winterhold Imperial Camp").
2. Meet the Imperial scouts near [Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Fort Kastav").
3. Sneak into Fort Kastav.
4. Free the prisoners from their cells.
5. Clear the fort of [Stormcloak soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks").
6. Report back to the scout team commander.

### Report to Rikke

Report for duty to [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") at [Winterhold Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Winterhold Imperial Camp"), east of Dawnstar.

She will tell you to take [Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Fort Kastav") from the Stormcloaks.

As the rebels currently hold some fellow Legionnaires in the fort's prison, you are to meet up with some scouts in the area, infiltrate the prison, release the prisoners, and then use their help to take the fort from the inside.

When you agree to take the mission, the quest will initiate. Rikke will mark the scouts' location on your map (southeast of your location, about halfway to Windhelm), and you will note in your journal that your objective is to "Meet the men near Fort Kastav".

You can successfully complete the quest without first sneaking inside and freeing the prisoners, but to accomplish all of the objectives as ordered, you must meet the scouts within a certain period of time, and you must avoid being detected by the rebels holding the fort before you get inside. The route you take to get there, and what you do on the way, can influence both of these contingencies.

### Meet the Scouts

The meeting point is on a cliff to the southwest of the fort. If your route takes you next to the fort before you reach them, you are likely to be detected by a rebel sentry. While you can successfully complete the quest in this event, you will not be able to complete all the objectives according to the plan.

Accordingly, if you will fast travel to a location near the fort, you may wish to select a location to the west or southwest of the fort, such as the [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn"), [Forsaken Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsaken_Cave "Skyrim:Forsaken Cave"), or [Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dunstad "Skyrim:Fort Dunstad"). This will allow you to approach the meeting point without passing the fort.

| Detailed guide and tips: Main roads route |
| --- |
| If you follow the [Clairvoyance](/wiki/Skyrim:Clairvoyance_(spell) "Skyrim:Clairvoyance (spell)") pathing from the camp, it will take you back into Dawnstar, then south out of town toward [Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dunstad "Skyrim:Fort Dunstad") by the main road that lies west of town. Sometimes the pathing may not go through Dawnstar, but instead take you to the road just southwest of town. Expect a dragon attack in Dawnstar or just to its southwest. Stone pile indicating the left turn, partially visible middle-left Travel quite a distance on the road south from Dawnstar. Eventually, you will likely encounter a [frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") attack. Shortly past the site of this, watch for a pair of stone piles on your left. They may be obscured by a tree and some grass (see photo). Turn left onto the paved road that they mark. If the road takes a curve to the right and you see [Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dunstad "Skyrim:Fort Dunstad") ahead of you, you have missed it. This road will point you due east toward [Fort Fellhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Fellhammer "Skyrim:Fort Fellhammer"), visible a short distance ahead of you. Fort Fellhammer will likely be guarded by bandits who will detect your presence and attack as you pass—unless you successfully sneak by, sticking to the right, and following the road as it curves to the right. If you engage them, then afterwards return to the road (southwest of the fort) and proceed south. There are no significant valuables around the fort's exterior. This road will take you southwards over a low hill and then down a fairly sharp descent. Where you level out, you are likely to be pounced upon by a [snowy sabre cat](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowy_Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Snowy Sabre Cat") or other hostile animal. [Ice Wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith") also inhabit the general area. Before you reach [Weynon Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Weynon_Stones "Skyrim:Weynon Stones"), identifiable by some stone pillars just ahead, turn left (east) at a T-intersection. Although the road you will run across is generally well-maintained, the paving stones are spotty here, so you may have to look around a bit to see it. As you proceed, your compass should show the tree icon marking [Shrouded Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Grove "Skyrim:Shrouded Grove") ahead of you. Continue onward, and as this icon flies off to the right of your compass, you will reach a major crossroads marked by a prominent signpost and known to be a favored ambush point for thieves. After dealing with any such threat, turn left (east-northeast) toward Windhelm.  You will pass the [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn"), on the right side of the road, and may wish to save your game in this area.  At this point, you and the scouting team (of four men) are both nearing the meeting area. The scouts may meet one or more enemies, most likely including a [frost troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll"). If such an attack occurs, it may happen before you arrive, while you are arriving, or just after you arrive. You may have an opportunity to intervene and reduce some or all potential fatalities among the scouts, thus giving you more allies when you eventually engage in the main battle for the fort. In any event, at least their leader will remain when you arrive, and he is all that is required. If you are unhappy with the number of scouts who end up alive, you can later reload a save from here.  From the Nightgate Inn, continue east on the road. After a moderate distance, passing two roads departing up to the left, you will reach an intersection with a stone pile and a signpost marking the road to Winterhold running up to the left. This is another point at which thieves may lie in wait, or you may encounter a wanderer, such as [M'aiq the Liar](/wiki/Skyrim:M%27aiq_the_Liar "Skyrim:M'aiq the Liar"). From the signpost, turn toward your objective marker and head eastward up the hill off-road, and eventually right off a short cliff. Here you may encounter a frost troll, ice wraith, or other hostile, possibly ahead of you and to the right. If you do find enemies here, quick action—especially paralyzing or otherwise quickly incapacitating any frost troll—may help protect the lives of the scouting party. |

| Detailed guide and tips: "Direct" mountain trek route |
| --- |
| Note that getting lost in the mountains can carry two implications for how the quest unfolds. First, if your path ends up taking you past the fort on your way to meeting the scouts (and you are seen by a Stormcloak there), the optional objective of sneaking in to release the prisoners will not appear; however, the quest can still be completed in this event: The rebels will engage you directly and the scouts will come to your assistance. Second, the scouts will not wait for you if you become delayed for too long, either because it takes you too much time to find your way, or because you are too long delayed in battles (e.g., if you near [Mount Anthor](/wiki/Skyrim:Mount_Anthor "Skyrim:Mount Anthor"), you will likely confront more than one of the powerful dragons who nest in the area). In such an event, the objective of sneaking into the prison will not appear, and you will go directly into battling for the fort whenever you finally arrive. Head SE from Frostflow Lighthouse. You needn't get lost, however. The following route can get you to your destination quickly: From the camp, turn toward the objective marker on your compass and trek cross-country on the footpath you will find in the area. You will soon encounter a rocky mountain range extending to the right (southward). If you bear to the left of this, you will pass between [Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse") on your left and the rocky rise on the right. Turn south after passing the rock on the right. Once you pass over a small crest, you will see ahead of you some jagged rocks behind which lies an impassable chasm and some buildings which are part of the sprawling Dwemer ruin, [Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand"). Navigate around this by passing the rocky area on your right, then turning right (south) instead of heading across the open area between you and the jagged rocks. Proceed southward for several hundred yards, ascending several rounded hills that rise in a somewhat step-like fashion, and passing [Alftand Ruined Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand_Ruined_Tower "Skyrim:Alftand Ruined Tower") to your left. Head south until you pass Alftand Ruined Tower (middle-left). You may encounter an [Ice Wraith](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith") or hostile animal in this area. You will almost certainly see a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") who nests on the mountain peak, though the dragon may or may not see you. Your objective marker should now be pointing at a tall mountain peak to the southeast. If you approach its base and then skirt around to the right (southwest) of it, you should find yourself on a mountain path that travels through [Wayward Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Wayward_Pass "Skyrim:Wayward Pass"). As you descend after Wayward Pass, be on the lookout for a path that turns to the left and heads uphill toward your objective marker. This is clearly a footpath, and not simply a clear area upon which you can climb up the mountain. This path will wind down and around, and then ends at a paved road which you can follow due east toward your marker. You may wish to save your game in this area.  At this point, you and the scouting team (of four men) are both nearing the meeting area. The scouts may meet one or more enemies, most likely including a [Frost Troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll"). If such an attack occurs, it may happen before you arrive, while you are arriving, or just after you arrive. You may have an opportunity to intervene and reduce some or all potential fatalities among the scouts, thus giving you more allies when you eventually engage in the main battle for the fort. In any event, at least their leader will remain when you arrive, and he is all that is required. If you are unhappy with the number of scouts who end up alive, you can reload from this point.  Remain on the paved road, heading eastward, until you approach an intersection with a stone pile and a signpost marking the road to Winterhold running up to the left. This is another point at which thieves may lie in wait, or you may encounter a wanderer, such as [M'aiq the Liar](/wiki/Skyrim:M%27aiq_the_Liar "Skyrim:M'aiq the Liar"). From the signpost, turn toward your objective marker and head eastward up the hill off-road, and eventually right off a short cliff. Here you may encounter a frost troll, ice wraith, or other hostile, possibly ahead of you and to the right. If you do find enemies here, quick action—especially paralyzing or otherwise quickly incapacitating any frost troll—may help protect the lives of the scouting party. |

Once you approach the scouts at the meeting point, you'll find [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar") again, commanding them. The number of men under his charge can vary from three to zero, depending on how many may have been taken by the hostile creatures which infest the area.

Speak to Hadvar. His plan is for you to sneak into the prison section of the fort through a grate located outside the walls. You should then find and release the prisoners, after killing the rebels guarding them. Once you release the prisoners, you are to make your way with them to the courtyard and engage the main rebel forces, at which point Hadvar and his men will also join to assist.

If you tell Hadvar that you are not much for sneaking, he will say that he has faith in you, but also that if you get discovered at any point, you should run out into the courtyard and start fighting, at which point he and his scouts will come running.

Hadvar will suggest waiting until nightfall before trying to sneak in. In reality, it's very easy to do this at any time.

Your objective becomes to sneak into the fort through the grate. However, you can successfully complete the quest no matter how you accomplish the fundamental objectives, which are releasing the prisoners and taking over the fort by killing all the Stormcloaks (in either order).

### Sneak Into the Fort

Stealthily enter the grate, to which your objective marker is pointing. If you are detected before entering the grate, the current objective will fail, but those of freeing the prisoners and taking the fort will become active, and you can still successfully complete the quest.

Despite Rikke's and Hadvar's emphasis on sneaking into the fort. It is actually not necessary to sneak at all because there are no sentries who can see in your direction unless you stray quite far out of your way to the north while en route to the grate. Head directly east toward the grate from Hadvar's location, jumping down the cliff and proceeding toward the quest marker. As you approach the fort, while you cannot be seen, you can still be heard by a guard who is stationed just inside the wall. However, you must actually make an effort to generate enough noise to be detected.

If you wish to practice your stealth skills anyway, you may wish to consider these detailed strategies:

| Detailed strategies for sneaking in |
| --- |
| Head toward the left parapet.  Wait until evening, get into sneak mode, and remove your armor or lighten the amount you're wearing. It is safest to have any follower wait for you, but if you want to bring one, you may wish to take from them any especially heavy armor and weapons. If you do bring your follower along, at least take away any torches that they may be carrying. Followers apparently missed a lesson in stealth school, and will readily light up any torch they are carrying while sneaking at night.  Stand on the first set of steps.  If you want to be extra-cautious, you can take further steps to try to [remain undetected](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak#Remaining_Undetected "Skyrim:Sneak"). From the bottom of the cliff, walk to the spottily paved road. Follow that toward the fort until the pavement appears to end (it actually turns to the north [left]). From this point, walk due east—between two flattish-top rocks toward a parapet in the wall—until you reach a few wooden steps. From those, turn to follow your objective marker to the grate. Proceed to the grate (top-left). If you open it without being seen, the current objective will clear, and your next objective becomes to free the prisoners. |

### Free the Prisoners

Open the grate. Once inside, follow Hadvar's plan by killing the guards before releasing the prisoners: The prisoners are unarmed in their cells, and therefore won't be much help if released into a battle. Once the guards are dead, upon release from their cells, the liberated prisoners will equip themselves with armor and weapons from a chest on the level above.

| A detailed strategy for freeing the prisoners |
| --- |
| Having slipped in through the grate, pass through the wooden door and then proceed through the small room toward the doorway at its far side. This opens into a larger room, on the east side of which is a wooden door which may be open or closed. If you wait, one of the three Stormcloaks guarding the prisoners will walk into the room at one end of his patrol beat. If your fight with him is noisy, it may draw in a second guard from further in and below by the prison cells. Pass through the door to the east and, around the next corner. From most of the way down the stairs ahead, you may see the second guard who walks a patrol beat nearer to the prison cells. If that guard is not in sight, you can probably put an arrow in the back of the third guard, who spends most of his time sitting at a table at the very far end of the next room. He probably cannot be seen from the foot of the stairs unless you have [eagle eye](/wiki/Skyrim:Eagle_Eye "Skyrim:Eagle Eye") vision. You should be able to detect a lantern burning in the distance, however, and the guard will generally be sitting just to the right of this, laterally centered through the midpoint of the door between you. This would leave you with just one more to take care of. The chest next to the guard who was sitting at the table contains the prisoners' weapons and armor. In more recent versions of the game, these items are not visible (the chest appears empty), but the prisoners will nonetheless find their items there after they are freed. |

After the three guards are dead, you can either practice some lockpicking to open the cells, or take the [Fort Kastav Prison Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Kastav_Prison_Key "Skyrim:Fort Kastav Prison Key") off any of the guards or the table on the level just above the cells. Once all of the prisoners are all released, your remaining objective is to take the fort by killing the rebels in the exterior courtyard. Make sure that all four prisoners are released: The related objective should clear and you will note in your journal that retaking the fort is your next task.

### Retake the Fort

The prisoners will equip themselves with armor and weapons and await your lead into battle. If you speak with them, however, you will have the option of ordering them to wait where they are.

Lead them up and out into the courtyard and begin the attack. [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar") and his men will join in the attack when the fighting starts.

Unlike the battles at previous forts, no additional enemies will materialize during the battle, and the killed will remain where they fall for some time, giving you a chance to loot their bodies at your leisure.

When all the rebels are dead, report back to Hadvar.

### Report Back to Hadvar

Hadvar will inform you that he will remain to garrison the fort while you go to report the success. He will also lament that none of the prisoners you freed survived the battle if none of them survived.

The quest will complete. If you have the underlying Reunification of Skyrim quest active, you will be directed to report back to [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") at [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") in Solitude.

### Report to General Tullius

Your objective then becomes to report to General Tullius at Castle Dour to receive your reward, but doing so technically occurs under the overarching [Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim") quest. After you have taken the fort, this quest will be complete. If you didn't flee the battle, Tullius will promote you to [Legate](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion#Ranks "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") along with a leveled armor.

## Notes

- If [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") is given to the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") then this quest will not be given to you.
- The prisoners you are sent to rescue will ignore your order if you tell them to wait. This is due to the script that handles them equipping their gear overriding the follow state variable that controls whether they're waiting or following.
- A Stormcloak soldier may remain on the roof of the Captain's Quarters who never becomes hostile during the battle, and does not have to be killed to complete the quest. If you go up to the roof after finishing the quest, but before you travel away from the area, the Stormcloak will warn you to leave since you are not welcome there, and may attack if you do not comply.
- Completing this quest will exile [Korir](/wiki/Skyrim:Korir "Skyrim:Korir") and his family to [Brunwulf Free-Winter's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter%27s_House "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter's House"), and install [Kraldar](/wiki/Skyrim:Kraldar "Skyrim:Kraldar") as [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of Winterhold.
- Completing this quest will also complete the quest [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") and advance the quest [The Fallen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fallen "Skyrim:The Fallen") to the objective "Learn Shout to call Odahviing".
- After completion of this quest, like any Civil War quest under [Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim"), unmarked by in-game references, you can approach Legate Rikke for a [medium leveled gold reward](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Gold_Rewards "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"); this is not always recommended, as entering her cell sets up the next quest in the series and, if triggered improperly, causes the missing *"Reporting for duty."* dialogue option (see [this](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim#Bugs "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim") bug section). Return to Legate Rikke to receive the leveled gold reward only when you want to start the next quest in the series and skip the reward when the game doesn't prompt you to return to her. Don't approach Rikke between quests of different holds.

## Bugs

- When General Tullius sends you to Legate Rikke at the Winterhold Imperial Camp to begin this quest, (the "Regain Winterhold Hold" quest), she may not offer the "Reporting for duty" dialogue needed to proceed.
  - The most reliable way to bypass this bug is to go to any indoor location and wait/rest for 30+ days. This allows all location cells to refresh, and the next time you travel to the Winterhold Imperial Camp, Legate Rikke will offer the "Reporting for Duty" dialogue option.
  - Repeatedly asking General Tullius, "How is the war going?" seems to fix the issue, and Rikke will eventually present the option. You may have to ask him each time you complete the missions, or alternatively you could try attacking her until she retaliates, then sheath your weapon and open dialogue again; this will sometimes work.
  -  You can use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command `setstage CWMission04 10` to start the mission. If nothing else works, you may need to complete the entire Reunification of Skyrim quest via the console command `setstage cwobj 255`. You cannot use the console (setstage) to start the next appropriate quest.
- If you manage to retake Fort Kastav without losing any of the prisoners, the quest may not continue when you report back to Hadvar. **?**
  - Kill all the unnamed imperial soldiers that were prisoners. You should then be able to continue the quest by talking to Hadvar.
-  In the Switch version, if you tell Hadvar to wait for you in the courtyard, the game will crash when you enter the prison. **?**
  - Simply tell Hadvar to follow you again, then proceed.

## Quest Stages

| Rescue from Fort Kastav (CWMission04) | | |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 11, 100, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CWMission04 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CWMission04`.

# Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Neugrad

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Stormcloaks.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Stormcloaks.png) | **Rescue [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") soldiers from the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") and capture the [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Fort Neugrad").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") |
| Location(s): | [Falkreath Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Falkreath Stormcloak Camp"), [Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Fort Neugrad") |
| Reward: | [Hjerim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjerim "Skyrim:Hjerim"), [Bone-Breaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks#Titles "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") title with a leveled sword |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | = 2 ([Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak")) 0→2 ([Dengeir of Stuhn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir_of_Stuhn "Skyrim:Dengeir of Stuhn")) 0→2 ([Tekla](/wiki/Skyrim:Tekla "Skyrim:Tekla")) = -1 ([Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir")) = -1 ([Nenya](/wiki/Skyrim:Nenya "Skyrim:Nenya")) |
| ID: | CWMission04 |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |
| --- | |
| |  |  |  | | --- | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)") | **Concurrent** [Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim") | **Next →** [Compelling Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Compelling_Tribute_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Compelling Tribute (Stormcloaks)") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)") | | Concurrent | [Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim") | | → Next | [Compelling Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Compelling_Tribute_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Compelling Tribute (Stormcloaks)") | | |

A heavily guarded fort... with a back entrance

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist").
2. Meet the Stormcloak rescue party.
3. Sneak in the cave *or* fight your way in through the front gate.
4. Free the prisoners.
5. Eliminate the rest of the Imperials.
6. Return to Ulfric.

## Detailed Walkthrough

The secret entrance under the lake

### Meet the Stormcloak Rescue Band

After reporting to [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") in the [Falkreath Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Falkreath Stormcloak Camp"), he tells you that your current objective is the Imperial-controlled [Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Fort Neugrad") where some of your brother Stormcloaks are being held captive. He has sent scouts ahead to the fort, so meet up with them for further instructions. When you meet up with the scouts speak with [Ralof](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralof "Skyrim:Ralof"), who will be quite happy to see you. He will tell you that they have located a cave under the lake that should lead into the fort's prison. He will ask you to sneak in, kill any Imperials you find, and then release the Stormcloak prisoners. After you have released the prisoners, head to the courtyard where he and his men will join you in fighting the Imperials.

Follow the quest marker around the fort to the lake. Be careful not to get spotted by any Imperials or you will fail that objective and have to storm the fort. Once in the lake, swim down and you will see a small wrecked boat with a locked chest slightly hidden under it. Directly behind you is the entrance to the cave.

### Rescue the Prisoners

The passage at the bottom of the lake will lead into the prison level of the fort, through the natural cave at the southeastern corner. Eliminate the [Imperial soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier") in the prison room and get a [Fort Neugrad prison key](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Neugrad_Prison_Key#Fort_Neugrad_Prison_Key "Skyrim:Fort Neugrad Prison Key") from them (there should also be one lying on top of a chest in the same room).

Open the cells and the Stormcloak soldiers will run to a chest to acquire weapons and armor. Talk to one of them and he will ask you what to do: you can tell them to wait where they are, or follow you.

- To guarantee they all survive, you may instruct them to stay behind, and return to them after the fort has been taken over. If you tell them to follow you, they will participate in the upcoming battle and may die, although this doesn't seem to have an impact on the quest.

### Take Over the Fort

As you leave the Fort Prison level and reach the courtyard, you will engage more Imperial Soldiers. Ralof's band will join the fray once you start the fight. After the fight, you will have to go inside the fort to eliminate the rest of the garrison. You can have Ralof follow you, or tell him to wait out in the yard.

Once the Imperials and the fort commander are dead, talk to Ralof and he says that he will stay and clean up the mess. That ends the quest and starts the next stage in [Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim").

## Notes

- If [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") is as [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"), this quest is one of [two](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice") required to become [Thane of Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Eastmarch "Skyrim:Thane of Eastmarch").
- If [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") is given to the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") then this quest will not be given to you.
- The prisoners you are sent to rescue will ignore your order if you tell them to wait. This is due to the script that handles them equipping their gear overriding the follow state variable that controls whether they're waiting or following.
- Completing this quest deposes [Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir") as [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), and installs [Dengeir of Stuhn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir_of_Stuhn "Skyrim:Dengeir of Stuhn") in that position. Siddgeir will move to the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace"). Dengeir's personal quest [Some Light Theft](/wiki/Skyrim:Some_Light_Theft "Skyrim:Some Light Theft") cannot be started if he is Jarl.
- If you have a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") that is capable of [reanimating](/wiki/Skyrim:Reanimate "Skyrim:Reanimate") dead bodies with you during the assault, such as [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana"), they may reanimate any Imperial soldiers that have already been killed, who must then be killed again to complete the quest.
- If you kill the prisoners, that part of the quest will fail, but Ralof and his men will still join you for the battle in the courtyard.

## Bugs

- Sometimes, instead of Imperial soldiers, you will find bandits holding the Stormcloak prisoners. The prisoners will still speak the usual dialogue lines (*"The guard has the key."*) but there are neither any guards nor a key, and the prisoners may even be unresponsive once freed, hence ruining the Stormcloak questline. This bug may also happen even if the Imperial soldiers are there, but you fail to sneak into the fort. **?**
  - Reload a save from before the quest was received, completely clear out the fort of all bandits, and then receive the quest from Galmar Stone-Fist. Reloading a save from after the quest is received will not fix this bug.
- You may not be able to initiate a chain of events for the mission. **?**
  -  Using the console command `movetoqt CWMission04` will teleport you into the cell of a prisoner you are supposed to rescue. Getting out of the cell will require picking the lock.
- Stormcloak soldiers may appear inside or near the fort as you approach. As fighting starts out right away, you fail the "Sneak into the fort" objective.
  -  To solve this, use the console command `tcai` and `tai` to turn off the combat AI and the AI globally, sneak past the fort and enter the cave. Then when loaded inside, turn both back on again.
- After freeing the prisoners, you may not be able to activate Ralof's dialogue menu. This is a problem because the task that follows freeing the prisoners entails speaking with Ralof and therefore becomes impossible.
  - One possible solution is to transform into a werewolf away from the soldiers surrounding Ralof, and then kill all of the soldiers. Once that is done, Ralof himself will ask you to get him another garrison of troops. After you retrieve his soldiers, you should be able to continue the dialogue. Alternatively, kill all the troops and then use Voice of the Emperor (if your race is Imperial).
  - Another possibility is to fast travel somewhere if Ralof is not at Fort Neugrad, then fast travel to Fort Neugrad. Ralof will be approaching the entrance to the fort and can then be engaged in dialogue.[*verification needed*]
  -  Another possible solution is opening the console and entering `setstage CWMission04 20` if the prisoners lived or `setstage CWMission04 21` if the prisoners died.
- Although you have killed all of the Imperials occupying the fort and freed the Stormcloak prisoners, the Stormcloaks may keep saying that there are Imperials around somewhere.
  - To fix this, simply open the chest on the north side of the room of Fort Neugrad Prison with the prison cells, to the left of the table.
- Although you have already infiltrated the Neugrad prison through the cave in the lake, the "Sneak into the fort" objective will still not be completed and will display two exits to work toward on the compass. **?**
  - To complete the objective, order the freed Stormcloak prisoners to wait in the prison, then climb up the ladder exit to Skyrim and reenter the prison from the same exit.
- If you approach the fort directly via the road, even if you're sneaking and completely invisible at night, you will still fail the "sneak into the fort" objective before the fort even comes into view.

  **Mod Notes**: This is due to a scripting error that causes the objective to fail even if you're not spotted.
- You may fail the objective "Sneak into the fort" even if you approach the cave completely undetected at night, even if not taking the main road. You may also fail the objective if you speak to Galmar too close to the fort.
  -  To fix this, move away from the fort and use the console commands `prid 0001B133` and `moveto player` to move Galmar close to you and away from the fort. Talk to him and initiate the quest. If you plan to sneak into the fort, use the command `setobjectivecompleted cwmission04 12 1` to complete this objective and proceed with the quest.
- Ralof may not be near Fort Neugrad and may be stuck in Helgen trying to get out of the gate. Opening the gate and speaking with him will initiate the next stage of the quest, at which point he may run off to the Stormcloak camp near Whiterun. Before approaching the Fort make a Quicksave as you may get the "Failed: Sneak into the Fort" message. If so, reload the save and see the above mentioned resolution to fix. After taking over the Fort and getting the "Report back to Ralof" message you will need to fast travel to the Whiterun Stormcloak camp to find him.
  -  If he does not advance the quest when talking to him then open the console and enter `setobjectivecompleted CWMission04 50 1` followed by `setstage CWMission04 100`.
- Ralof and the other soldiers may act like the fort already belongs to them if they catch you stealing or picking locks. Despite this, they won't turn hostile. **?**
- If you kill all the soldiers before you interact with Ralof, he will not be at his post and you will have to reload a previous save. **?**

## Overview

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Skjor](/wiki/Skyrim:Skjor "Skyrim:Skjor") or [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") in [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr").
2. Travel to the randomly-determined location.
3. Rescue the citizen from the location's enemies.
4. Escort the citizen back to their hometown.
5. Return to Skjor or Vilkas for your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Either [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") or [Skjor](/wiki/Skyrim:Skjor "Skyrim:Skjor") has received notice that someone has been kidnapped, and the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") have been asked to attempt a rescue. He will send you to the location of the kidnapped individual and tell you to free them from the location and then escort them to their nearby home. See Radiant Options below for possible variations of this quest.

Note that this is a repeating quest: each time you go to Vilkas or Skjor (when told to ask a Companion for work), he will give a different version of the quest.

## Radiant Options

This quest has several radiant options. The criteria used to select victims for this quest are:

- The victim must live in one of the marked habitation areas listed below.
- Must not have unique voice acting.
- Must not be a part of the following factions: [PlayerHousecarlFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:PlayerHousecarlFaction "Skyrim:PlayerHousecarlFaction"), [The Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Companions "Skyrim:The Companions"), [CurrentHireling](/wiki/Skyrim:CurrentHireling "Skyrim:CurrentHireling"), [JobJarlFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:JobJarlFaction "Skyrim:JobJarlFaction"), or [CurrentFollowerFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:CurrentFollowerFaction "Skyrim:CurrentFollowerFaction").
- Must not be marked as an [Essential NPC](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs").
- The victim's faction can not be related to you.
- Must be a unique character (excludes [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Guards "Skyrim:Guards"), etc.).

### NPC Residences

The victim can be randomly selected from over 200 potential NPCs residing in one of the areas listed below:

| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") | [Solstheim](/wiki/Dragonborn:Solstheim "Dragonborn:Solstheim")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Brandy-Mug Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Brandy-Mug_Farm "Skyrim:Brandy-Mug Farm") [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing") [Gloombound Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Gloombound_Mine "Skyrim:Gloombound Mine") [Hlaalu Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Hlaalu_Farm "Skyrim:Hlaalu Farm") [Hollyfrost Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Hollyfrost_Farm "Skyrim:Hollyfrost Farm") [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove") [Mixwater Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Mixwater_Mill "Skyrim:Mixwater Mill") [Narzulbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Narzulbur "Skyrim:Narzulbur") [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") | [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") [Half-moon Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Half-moon_Mill "Skyrim:Half-moon Mill") | [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") [Katla's Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Katla%27s_Farm "Skyrim:Katla's Farm") [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") [Solitude ### Quest Locations

The radiant location is randomly chosen from 50 possible locations, amounting to a large fraction of the [dungeons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") that contain boss-type enemies and have a place where a captive can be locked up. The location will be limited to holds that you have previously visited, so early in the game you may only receive destinations within Whiterun Hold, but later in the game there are many more possible destinations. All possible locations are listed in the table below.

| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") | [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| A [Bandit Camp](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit_Camps "Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit Camps") or [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit")-occupied fort (21 possible locations) | | | | | | | | | |
| [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern") [Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock") [Lost Knife Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Knife_Hideout "Skyrim:Lost Knife Hideout") [Uttering Hills Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Uttering_Hills_Camp "Skyrim:Uttering Hills Camp") | [Bilegulch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Bilegulch_Mine "Skyrim:Bilegulch Mine") [Cracked Tusk Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Cracked_Tusk_Keep "Skyrim:Cracked Tusk Keep") [Embershard Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Embershard_Mine "Skyrim:Embershard Mine") [Knifepoint Ridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Knifepoint_Ridge "Skyrim:Knifepoint Ridge") |  | [Orotheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Orotheim "Skyrim:Orotheim") [Robber's Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Robber%27s_Gorge "Skyrim:Robber's Gorge") | [Frostmere Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmere_Crypt "Skyrim:Frostmere Crypt") |  | [Broken Helm Hollow](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Helm_Hollow "Skyrim:Broken Helm Hollow") [Faldar's Tooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Faldar%27s_Tooth "Skyrim:Faldar's Tooth") [Treva's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Treva's Watch") | [Halted Stream Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Halted_Stream_Camp "Skyrim:Halted Stream Camp") [Redoran's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Redoran's Retreat") [Silent Moons Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Silent_Moons_Camp "Skyrim:Silent Moons Camp") [Valtheim Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Valtheim_Towers "Skyrim:Valtheim Towers") [White River Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River_Watch "Skyrim:White River Watch") | [Fort Fellhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Fellhammer "Skyrim:Fort Fellhammer") [Wreck of the Winter War](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Winter_War "Skyrim:Wreck of the Winter War") | [Bloodskal Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodskal_Barrow "Skyrim:Bloodskal Barrow") |
| A [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") [Hive](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Falmer_Hives "Category:Skyrim-Places-Falmer Hives") (9 possible locations): | | | | | | | | | |
|  |  | [Lost Echo Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Echo_Cave "Skyrim:Lost Echo Cave") | [Chillwind Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Chillwind_Depths "Skyrim:Chillwind Depths") |  | [Gloomreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Gloomreach "Skyrim:Gloomreach") [Liar's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Liar%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Liar's Retreat") | [Darkwater Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Pass "Skyrim:Darkwater Pass") [Tolvald's Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolvald%27s_Cave "Skyrim:Tolvald's Cave") | [Shimmermist Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Shimmermist_Cave "Skyrim:Shimmermist Cave") | [Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse") [Stillborn Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stillborn_Cave "Skyrim:Stillborn Cave") |  |

| A [Warlock](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock") [Lair](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs") (11 possible locations): | | | | | | | | | |

- Note that the categories for each of the location types above will list *all* locations with the given type of occupant, including locations that do *not* have a boss-type enemy or do not have place to lock up captives; therefore, some of the locations listed in the categories are not possible destinations for this quest.

### Reward

| Levels[†](#intnote_LevelNote) | Reward[‡](#intnote_RewardBug) | USLEEP Reward |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 100 | 100 |
| 10–19 | 150 | 150 |
| 20–29 | 300 | 200 |
| 30–39 | 300 | 250 |
| 40+ | 300 | 300 |

[†](#note_LevelNote)Level is based on when the player completed the previous quest (or level one for the first quest), not the player's level when receiving the quest or its reward.

[‡](#note_RewardBug)The reward amounts for radiant Companions quests do not progress as intended.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=20007))

## Notes

- If [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") is installed, some radiant locations may be on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"). If you are in Skyrim, you will not receive a quest marker pointing you to the quest location, but must travel to Solstheim first (at which point any quest markers you have to quests in Skyrim will disappear).
- If you complete this quest successfully, then the citizen you rescue becomes a friend of yours. This may affect thane quests and other aspects of the game.
- Unlike most other radiant Companions quests, this quest starts immediately when it is offered, giving you no chance to refuse it.

## Bugs

|  |
| --- |
| **To meet our site's higher standard of quality, this article or section may require cleanup.**   To leave a message about the cleanup for this article, please add it to this article's [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Rescue_Mission). |

- The hostage may not follow you when you've saved them. Arriving at their hometown should update the quest, though you may have to talk to them afterwards. **?**
  -  You can use the console by targeting them and using `moveto player`.
- The hostage may be at their village/town instead of the area the quest says to go to.
  - This might be resolved by entering their home, then leaving immediately. This fix is reported to not work for [Heimskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimskr "Skyrim:Heimskr"). Heimskr might not spawn at the hostage point and will stay at the shrine, however, this might be resolved by fast traveling to outside Whiterun where he may actually be making his way to his hostage point where he can then be rescued and taken home.
- The hostage may be an NPC who has already died. In this case, the corpse will be found in the radiant location.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.
- The person you are supposed to rescue is invisible (not game invisible, they are NOT there). You can't complete the quest because you can't initiate them to follow you to safety. **?**
  - The missing NPC might appear to be in an undefined spot that hovers over the map. If this is the case, it might be resolved by using the "jump over the wall" glitch in Whiterun. Follow the instructions found [here](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Eorlund_Gray-Mane#Merchant_Chest "Skyrim talk:Eorlund Gray-Mane") to exit the city, and run towards the marker. If successful, you should be able to find the target NPC in a glitched area. Talk to them and then fast travel back to Whiterun.
  - In Whiterun the compass pointer might show that the person you are looking for is within the city (pointer without a gate), however on the map it shows them outside the city. Open the console in Whiterun and type in: "tcl" and run towards the target beyond the city walls. The target may be hovering in the sky, so check all directions once you reach the marker. Talk to them and then fast travel back to Whiterun. Open the console and type in: "tcl" again.
  - Open the game console and type this in to force the next quest line: `setstage cr08 21`. That will have them follow you (even though they do not exist) and fast travel to the location you are asked to go to, or somewhere nearby.
- It says "take your leave of (name)", which again, since (name) does not exist, you can't. **?**
  - Open the console again and type in: "setstage cr08 25" again without quotes. It will tell you to go back to Vilkas and end the quest (which he will accept as complete).
- The civilian may not yet have been captured or may just be walking around. The NPC will not follow you and just walks around and is either busy or gives you default scripting.
- You may complete the rescue mission and escort the civilian back to their home, but the quest will not recognize you have brought them home. Following rescue of Wilhem from Ilinalta's deep, a successful return to Iverstead was accomplished. The marker shows the correct location in front of Vilemyr Inn. However, regardless of where you go in town, Wilhelm fails to recognize he is home and simply repeats -- "Please, get me home!" Based on the Quest Stages below, the quest is stuck in Stage 21. In this case it may help to enter and exit the NPC's home.
- If those don't work, you can find the civilian again and simply kill the person failing the mission **?**
- If the targeted civilian is part of a scripted scene that the player hasn't witnessed yet, they will not be moved to the target dungeon. They will still have the appropriate dialogue but the quest will be rendered unfinishable without console commands. **?**
- The quest objective to talk to the victim may appear after you're already escorting them home, in which case it will remain incomplete until the end of the quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, fixes this bug.
- If the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") add-on is installed and [Gjalund Salt-Sage](/wiki/Skyrim:Gjalund_Salt-Sage "Skyrim:Gjalund Salt-Sage") is the target, his participation in this quest will break the [opening quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_(quest) "Skyrim:Dragonborn (quest)") for the Dragonborn DLC if both quests are active together.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, addresses this issue. Gjalund has been added to the Rescue Mission exempt list to prevent that from happening.

## Quest Stages

| Rescue Mission (CR08) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | <Alias=Victim> has been kidnapped and taken to <Alias=Lair>. I need to get <Alias.PronounObj=Victim> back to <Alias=VictimHome>. *Objective 10:* Rescue <Alias=Victim> from <Alias=Lair> |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Talk to <Alias=Victim> |
| 21 |  | *Objective 21:* Escort <Alias=Victim> back to <Alias=VictimHome> |
| 22 |  | *Objective 22:* Take your leave of <Alias=Victim> |
| 25 |  | I rescued <Alias=Victim> from <Alias=Lair> and escorted <Alias.PronounObj=Victim> back to <Alias=VictimHome>. *Objective 25:* Return to <Alias.ShortName=Questgiver> |
| 50 |  | I found <Alias=Victim> in <Alias=Lair> but <Alias.Pronoun=Victim> died. *Objective 25:* Return to <Alias.ShortName=Questgiver> |
| 100 | ☑ |  |
| 150 | ☒ |  |
| 250 | ☒ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CR08 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CR08`.

# Skyrim:Rescue

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dawnguard Dawnguard.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dawnguard_Dawnguard.png) | **Rescue a victim from [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Florentius Baenius](/wiki/Skyrim:Florentius_Baenius "Skyrim:Florentius Baenius") |
| Location(s): | Radiant [Bandit Camp](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit_Camps "Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit Camps") or [Warlock Lair](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs") |
| Reward: | Leveled enchanted item |
| ID: | DLC1RH06 |
| --- | |
| |  | | --- | | **Prerequisites:** [Bolstering the Ranks](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolstering_the_Ranks "Skyrim:Bolstering the Ranks") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | Prerequisites: | [Bolstering the Ranks](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolstering_the_Ranks "Skyrim:Bolstering the Ranks") | | |

Rescue [Wylandriah](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah "Skyrim:Wylandriah") from a [Master Vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Vampire "Skyrim:Master Vampire").

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with [Florentius Baenius](/wiki/Skyrim:Florentius_Baenius "Skyrim:Florentius Baenius").
2. Rescue a kidnapped victim from [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire").
3. Report back to Florentius.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After [rescuing Florentius Baenius](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolstering_the_Ranks "Skyrim:Bolstering the Ranks"), speak to him, and ask "What can I do to help?" He will either refer you [to somebody else](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Quests#Dawnguard_Side_Quests "Skyrim:Dawnguard Quests"), or he will explain: *"[Arkay](/wiki/Lore:Arkay "Lore:Arkay") has some grave news, friend. Your friend, kidnapped! A vicious night stalker rules over a group of [class] - seeks to gain leverage over the righteous. Arkay's never clear on life and death. Is [s]he still alive? There's always hope..."*

The victim can be nearly anyone with a positive [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") towards you, including [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") and [spouses](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage"). He or she will be held captive at a random [bandit camp](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit_Camps "Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit Camps") or [warlock lair](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs"), bound and helpless.

Travel to the destination and cut your way through the enemies until you reach the victim. To release them from their bindings, simply interact with them. Once you have rescued them, kill the boss-level vampire in the dungeon before returning to Florentius for your reward: a leveled enchanted item.

## Notes

- If [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") is installed, some radiant locations may be on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"). If you are in Skyrim, you will not receive a quest marker pointing you to the quest location, but must travel to Solstheim first (at which point any quest markers you have to quests in Skyrim will disappear).
- If the radiant location selected is [Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock") there will only be Silver Hand members inside; they will also kill the vampire for you.
- Even if the victim dies before or after you rescue them, the objective will still count as completed.

## Bugs

- After completing one quest for [Florentius Baenius](/wiki/Skyrim:Florentius_Baenius "Skyrim:Florentius Baenius"), this quest may trigger unexpectedly when you next talk with the victim.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.1.2, fixes this bug.
- The victim may thank you as if married to you, even if they aren't.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.1.2, fixes this bug.
- Upon entering the dungeon, a fight may ensue between its regular occupants, the vampire and the victim, leading to either vampire's or the victim's death, the latter case being somewhat irritating to the player, who was tasked with saving the victim, but had no chance to accomplish the rescue. UDGP/USSEP fix is partial only, either not all dungeons are fixed, or the fix does not apply for games started without the patch.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- The victim may be your current follower. If this is the case, you can simply talk to them, then go kill the vampire that Florentius points you to.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.2.3, fixes this bug.
- If the victim is your spouse, they may not actually be kidnapped and will remain at your home requesting help, which triggers the quest incorrectly. The target location will have no vampire to kill, or you may not even be informed of a target location at all, so you won't be able to complete the quest. It has been suggested that this also may actually have something to do with being a werewolf, because every time you go to the place of rescue it says you have consumed a heart without actually doing so and you don't even have to be in werewolf form. However, the "spouse" bug has occurred in cases where the player has not joined the Companions, and is not a werewolf.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.
  - Load a save from before talking to your spouse, then go speak with Florentius, and the quest will start and progress normally.
  - Alternatively, open the console and type: setstage DLC1RH06 255 - this will "complete" the quest properly (and even give you a reward item), then go back to talk to Florentius or Gunnar to start the next quest in the series. It is not clear whether this will or will not result in a leftover vampire at the location next time you head there.
  - If you want to stop doing the radiant Dawnguard quests and have none of them remaining in your journal, do it immediately after completing a "Rescue" quest. After that, the notional next one is bound to be a different and less buggy one, and is less likely to be "started incorrectly" without talking to one of the quest givers.
- The victim may continue on with the regular daily routine, and not stay in the dungeon with the vampire in it. If this happens, you can complete the quest by killing the vampire, then going and "rescuing" the victim wherever the victim has moved to.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Rescue (DLC1RH06) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Florentius Baenius has learned that a <Alias=Vampire> has kidnapped <Alias=Prisoner> and is keeping <Alias.PronounObj=Prisoner> prisoner in <Alias=Dungeon>. *Objective 10:* Rescue <Alias=Prisoner> from <Alias=Dungeon>  *Objective 11:* Kill the <Alias=Vampire> |
| 50 |  | *Objective 11:* Kill the <Alias=Vampire> *(if vampire not killed)* |
| 60 |  | *Objective 10:* Rescue <Alias=Prisoner> from <Alias=Dungeon> *(if prisoner not rescued)* |
| 100 |  | *Objective 100:* Return to Florentius Baenius |
| 255 | ☑ | Florentius Baenius learned that a <Alias=Vampire> kidnapped <Alias=Prisoner>. I rescued <Alias.PronounObj=Prisoner> from in <Alias=Dungeon>. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1RH06 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1RH06`.

# Skyrim:Restocking Soul Gems

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Quozar](/wiki/User:Quozar "User:Quozar"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by multiple users, *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Help [Sergius Turrianus](/wiki/Skyrim:Sergius_Turrianus "Skyrim:Sergius Turrianus") to fill his stock with [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Sergius Turrianus](/wiki/Skyrim:Sergius_Turrianus "Skyrim:Sergius Turrianus") |
| Location(s): | [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") |
| Reward: | Various amounts of gold |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | 0→1 (Sergius) |
| ID: | MGR11 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | |  | **Next →** Radiant | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | → Next | Radiant | | |

Sergius Turrianus in his quarters

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Sergius Turrianus](/wiki/Skyrim:Sergius_Turrianus "Skyrim:Sergius Turrianus").
2. Give him a certain amount of [Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"). Type and amount are randomly chosen.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Sergius Turrianus wants *empty* Soul Gems because he's almost out of stock. After giving him the requested number of the type he's asked for, he pays an amount of gold per gem. To start his next quest you must leave the current conversation and start a new one.

Rewards for each empty gem:

- 12 Gold per Petty Soul Gem
- 30 Gold per Lesser Soul Gem
- 60 Gold per Common Soul Gem
- 120 Gold per Greater Soul Gem
- 240 Gold per Grand Soul Gem

Saying that you cannot do this allows you to skip the quest and move on to the next one.

## Notes

- This quest never appears in the journal but you can ask him all the time about his request to get to know what soul gem he wants, and how many.

## Bugs

- Sergius Turrianus doesn't take any Common Soul Gems and pays nothing for them, but the quest will finish and you can start a new one.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Restocking Soul Gems (MGR11) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Sergius has asked for my help in restocking soul gems. |
| 200 | ☑ | I've delivered the soul gems that Sergius requested. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MGR11 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MGR11`.

# Skyrim:Restoration Ritual Spell

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by multiple users, *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Bign0se](/wiki/User:Bign0se "User:Bign0se"), checked by [RobinHood70](/wiki/User:RobinHood70 "User:RobinHood70") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Find the [Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain") and learn more about [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") magic.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Colette Marence](/wiki/Skyrim:Colette_Marence "Skyrim:Colette Marence") |
| Location(s): | [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") |
| Reward: | [Bane of the Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Bane_of_the_Undead "Skyrim:Bane of the Undead"), ability to purchase Master level [Restoration spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration_Spells "Skyrim:Restoration Spells") and Master level [Alteration spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration_Spells "Skyrim:Alteration Spells"), due to a [bug](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration_Ritual_Spell#Bugs "Skyrim:Restoration Ritual Spell"). |
| ID: | MGRitual04 |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |
| --- | |
| |  | | --- | | **Prerequisites:** Level 90 [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") | | **← Previous** [Good Intentions](/wiki/Skyrim:Good_Intentions "Skyrim:Good Intentions") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | Prerequisites: | Level 90 [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") | | ← Previous | [Good Intentions](/wiki/Skyrim:Good_Intentions "Skyrim:Good Intentions") | | |

Augur of Dunlain

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Colette Marence](/wiki/Skyrim:Colette_Marence "Skyrim:Colette Marence").
2. Talk to [Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain").
3. Pass the Augur's test.

### Find the Augur of Dunlain

Once you reach level 90 in the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") skill and have completed [Good Intentions](/wiki/Skyrim:Good_Intentions "Skyrim:Good Intentions"), travel to the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") and speak with [Colette Marence](/wiki/Skyrim:Colette_Marence "Skyrim:Colette Marence"). Ask her if you can learn anything more about Restoration magic. She will tell you to go speak with the [Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain") down in [The Midden](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Midden "Skyrim:The Midden").

### Pass the test

The [Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain") will give you a test. Once you have stepped into the "light", all non-quest items will be taken from your possession. The Augur will summon one ghost, shortly followed by another, and finally a third; each will attack you with destruction spells and/or weapons. It is not possible to attack these [ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost "Skyrim:Ghost"); your only goal is to keep yourself alive using Restoration magic. Alternatively, the [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") shout will leave you invincible for most or all of the test, depending on how many words have been unlocked. If you are still alive when the test stops, you will receive your items back and the [Bane of the Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Bane_of_the_Undead "Skyrim:Bane of the Undead") spell. You will also be able to buy the [Guardian Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:Guardian_Circle "Skyrim:Guardian Circle") spell from [Colette Marence](/wiki/Skyrim:Colette_Marence "Skyrim:Colette Marence") the next time her inventory resets.

## Notes

- If your Sneak skill is high enough, you can simply crouch before the first ghost notices you and remain hidden for the duration of the test.
- The ghosts favor [frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Damage "Skyrim:Frost Damage") spells, so if you are a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") or [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism")—or better yet, both—this will be very easily accomplished.
- You can take along one item (for example, a ring with double magic resist 45%) to the test by dropping the item and then holding it in the air while going to the light.
- If you have completed [Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death") from the Dark Brotherhood quest line, you can [summon](/wiki/Skyrim:Summon_Spectral_Assassin "Skyrim:Summon Spectral Assassin") the [Spectral Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Spectral_Assassin "Skyrim:Spectral Assassin") while crouching and the test will be passed after a few seconds.
- Appearance of the Guardian Circle spell upon the completion of this quest can be bugged. See [Guardian Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:Guardian_Circle "Skyrim:Guardian Circle") for fix.
- You can give as many items as you need to your [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"), and step in to the light. Then, before the first ghost notices you, talk to your follower and trade items to retrieve them. Items with [Fortify Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Restoration "Skyrim:Fortify Restoration"), [Fortify Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Sneak "Skyrim:Fortify Sneak"), and/or [Resist Frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Frost "Skyrim:Resist Frost") enchantments would be good choices.
- Unlike other ritual quests, this one grants you the first spell directly rather than as a spell tome.

## Bugs

- Even after you finish the quest, Colette may still not have the Guardian Circle spell for sale.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9, fixes this bug.
- After meeting the Augur of Dunlain and stepping into the light, the game may hang up.
  - Removing some of the items from your inventory before stepping into the light may help avoid the bug.
- Completing this quest may cause a persistent scripting error to repeat several times a second. It appears to be unintrusive in gameplay, but it will flood Papyrus logs.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
  -  By using the console, the quest can be set to an earlier stage where the faulty script does not occur: `setstage MGRitual04 10`.
- After you survive the test, the Augur's scripted response of *You are worthy. The knowledge is yours* might get stuck in a loop. However, the quest will still be marked as complete and leaving the chamber has no negative side effects.
- One or more of the hostile ghosts might linger after the test is complete. As they are ethereal, they cannot be killed, and will follow you around the Midden Dark attacking you.
  -  Reloading a save previous to the ritual will solve this problem.
- The game will incorrectly flag the [Alteration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Alteration Ritual Spell") quest as being completed, instead of the Restoration quest.
  - This causes the spell tome [Mass Paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Mass_Paralysis "Skyrim:Mass Paralysis") to be available for purchase upon quest completion.
  - The bug doesn't prevent the Dragonborn from completing the Alteration quest at a later date.
  - Bug fixed by the Unofficial Skyrim Patch.
- Sometimes the Guardian Circle spell tome may not appear after successfully completing the quest.
  - Reloading a previous save and interacting with her merchant inventory prior to starting the quest seems to fix this.
  - This may occur because the game incorrectly flags the Alteration ritual quest as being completed instead of the Restoration quest. You can buy the Guardian Circle spell directly after completing the quest because the game also gives her the tome directly so you wouldn't have to wait until her inventory resets, but once it does reset, the book will never appear again.
  -  You can fix this with the console command `set MGRitualRestBook to 0` .
- If you successfully complete the test, the quest will complete, but you may not receive your items back (or they can remain unequipped), nor will the Augur speak with you again.

## Quest Stages

| 200 | ☑ | I've passed the Augur's test, and have been granted the Bane of the Undead spell. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MGRitual04 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MGRitual04`.
