# Skyrim:Restoring Order

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Zebendal](/wiki/User:Zebendal "User:Zebendal"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by multiple users, *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Put an end to the melding of planes under [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Location(s): | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), [Solitude Sewers](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Sewers "Skyrim:Solitude Sewers") |
| Reward: | [Sword of Jyggalag](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword_of_Jyggalag "Skyrim:Sword of Jyggalag"), Four Summoning Spells, [Ring of Disrobing](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Disrobing "Skyrim:Ring of Disrobing"), [Breadcrumb quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Amber_and_Madness_Smithing "Skyrim:Amber and Madness Smithing") to unlock [Amber](/wiki/Skyrim:Amber "Skyrim:Amber") and [Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:Madness "Skyrim:Madness") smithing |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE025\_QuestB |
| Added by: | [Saints & Seducers](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers") |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Balance of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:Balance_of_Power "Skyrim:Balance of Power") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Balance of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:Balance_of_Power "Skyrim:Balance of Power") | | |

Thoron's vile ritual

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Discover the location of [the conjurer's](/wiki/Skyrim:Thoron "Skyrim:Thoron") lair.
2. Investigate the Solitude sewers.
3. Explore the root cave.
4. Defeat [Thoron](/wiki/Skyrim:Thoron "Skyrim:Thoron").
5. Retrieve the Sword of Jyggalag.

## Detailed Walkthrough

While completing the quest Balance of Power, you will learn that the Saints and Seducers are being funded by a conjurer named Thoron. While one journal will mention he is insane and living in the sewers, the other will mention he's located in Solitude. Both journals indicate that Thoron is looking for trinkets and junk, although his motives are a mystery to both bandit leaders. After entering Solitude, the map marker will direct you to a manhole cover leading down into the sewers.

Straight ahead is a grate, and left is a barred door, so turn right and head down. Across the water you'll see that the tunnel is overgrown with strange-looking plant life. Enter this "root cave" and you'll notice pods that you can harvest for new types of flora. To the right is a dead end with a hollowed stump filled with random loot. Turning left will lead you into a tunnel system populated by Elytra and Spriggans. Further into the tunnel you'll reach an intersection. The right path leads to a small cave chamber populated by Spriggans, along with a dead end containing a dead hunter and goat.

Continuing along the root path, you'll see a chamber ahead where some of the Solitude stonework is visible. Kill the Elytra Nymphs in the chamber, and to the left you'll see a chamber with water. From the water, you can either turn right to head up a ramp into further root tunnels, or you can go through a broken sewer wall to re-enter the sewers. If you follow the sewer path, you'll come to a room with a Spriggan and some elytra, as well as a locked chest (in an alcove behind the debris).

Following the root tunnel will take you up and around, coming to an intersection where a fight apparently took place. Scattered around the intersection, you'll find both Golden and Dark armor/weapons... but no bodies. There is a short path to the right, but it's just a dead end with some enemies and a hollow stump. Continuing straight from the battle site, you'll come upon the object of your quest - Thoron, the mysterious benefactor of the Saints & Seducers gangs. The obviously insane conjurer appears to be performing a ritual, opening a doorway of some sort.

Once you're close enough, the objective will update - you must defeat Thoron and stop his ritual. Thoron can be a handful - he will summon both Golden Saints & Dark Seducers, in addition to the usual atronachs. Once you've finished him off, make sure to loot his body for a unique Madness Helm as well as several spell tomes teaching you how to summon Saints or Seducers.

From the 4-way intersection where you encountered Thoron, only the southern path leads anywhere (back to the beginning sewers). The northern alcove is Thoron's workstation, where you can find an arcane enchanter and numerous other items of interest. Make sure to loot it all, as both the note and the [Sheogorath-Shaped Amber](/wiki/Skyrim:Sheogorath-Shaped_Amber "Skyrim:Sheogorath-Shaped Amber") are needed for other quests. The notes begin the [Amber and Madness Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Amber_and_Madness_Smithing "Skyrim:Amber and Madness Smithing") quest, while the Sheogorath-Shaped Amber is needed for [Staada's Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Staada%27s_Quest "Skyrim:Staada's Quest").

In the western alcove, grab the Sword of Jyggalag from the roots in order to complete the quest.

## Notes

- After completing the questline, a courier may track you down and give you [a note](/wiki/Skyrim:Note_on_New_Wares "Skyrim:Note on New Wares"). It's from Ri'saad, letting you know that he now sells Golden/Dark items as well as the new materials added by [the creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers").

- If you have this DLC as part of the Anniversary Edition, the load order, which is the first two digits of all IDs, may not be obvious. You can find it by using console command `player.showinventory` and finding the ID of an item from this DLC, such as amber.

## Bugs

- You may be unable to enter the sewers. **?**
  - Use the console command `coc ccBGSSSE025RootDungeon`.

- When you reach the quest marker in front of the sword, [Thoron](/wiki/Skyrim:Thoron "Skyrim:Thoron") may fail to appear. **?**
  -  Use the console command `prid xx000c3d` to select Thoron, and `enable` to force him to appear.

- During the battle, [Thoron](/wiki/Skyrim:Thoron "Skyrim:Thoron") may drift up through the ceiling. **?**
  -  If he fails to reappear shortly, use the console command `prid xx000c3d` to select Thoron, and `moveto player` to bring him back.

## Map

[(?)](/wiki/Category:Pages_Missing_Data "Category:Pages Missing Data")

## Quest Stages

| Restoring Order (ccBGSSSE025\_QuestB) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 0 |  | I've learned that a powerful conjurer, Thoron, has been funding the Saints and Seducers bandits while conducting dangerous experiments somewhere in Solitude. I should try to learn where Thoron might be found. I've learned that a powerful conjurer, Thoron, has been funding the Saints and Seducers bandits while conducting dangerous experiments somewhere in a sewer. I should try to learn where Thoron might be found. *Objective 10:* Discover the location of the conjurer's lair |
| 10 |  | After studying the journals of the both the Saints and Seducers bandit leaders, I've learned that Thoron is conducting dangerous experiments in the Solitude sewers using a strange sword. I should locate Thoron's lair within the sewers and discover the nature of the conjurer's experiments. *Objective 20:* Investigate the Solitude sewers |
| 20 |  | I've discovered a network of root-like caves that appear to be spreading throughout the Solitude sewers. They may be connected to the experiments that the conjurer Thoron is supposedly conducting here. I should continue to explore the caves to locate Thoron and put a stop to the spread of these unnatural structures. *Objective 30:* Explore the root cave |
| 30 |  | I've found Thoron, who is conducting some kind of ritual using a strange sword. When I entered the chamber, he summoned Daedra and attacked. I will have to defeat Thoron to put an end to this. *Objective 40:* Defeat Thoron |
| 40 |  | I've defeated Thoron, and halted the ritual. *Objective 50:* Retrieve the Sword of Jyggalag |
| 200 |  | I have retrieved the Sword of Jyggalag and put an end to Thoron's ritual. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: [(?)](/wiki/Category:Pages_Missing_Data "Category:Pages Missing Data").

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE025_QuestB stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE025_QuestB`.

# Skyrim:Retaking Thirsk

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Krusty](/wiki/User:Krusty "User:Krusty"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Krusty](/wiki/User:Krusty "User:Krusty"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Help [Bujold the Unworthy](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold_the_Unworthy "Skyrim:Bujold the Unworthy") retake [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Bujold the Unworthy](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold_the_Unworthy "Skyrim:Bujold the Unworthy") |
| Location(s): | [Bujold's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Bujold's Retreat"), [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall"), [Hrothmund's Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrothmund%27s_Barrow "Skyrim:Hrothmund's Barrow") |
| Reward: | Master trainer in [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") |
| ID: | DLC2MH01 |

The assault on [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Bujold the Unworthy](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold_the_Unworthy "Skyrim:Bujold the Unworthy") in [Bujold's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Bujold's Retreat").
2. Join the assault on Thirsk Mead Hall and defeat the rieklings.
3. Meet her at [Hrothmund's Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrothmund%27s_Barrow "Skyrim:Hrothmund's Barrow").
4. Listen to her interaction with [Hrothmund's spirit](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrothmund "Skyrim:Hrothmund").
5. Keep her secret, kill her, or betray her to Kuvar.

### Exiled Warriors

[Thirsk](/wiki/Lore:Thirsk "Lore:Thirsk"), the legendary mead hall founded in the [Third Era](/wiki/Lore:Third_Era "Lore:Third Era") by [Hrothmund the Red](/wiki/Lore:Hrothmund_the_Red "Lore:Hrothmund the Red") of the [Skaal](/wiki/Lore:Skaal "Lore:Skaal"), was built for [Nord](/wiki/Lore:Nord "Lore:Nord") warriors who wanted to live, hunt, and fight in the wilderness, the old way. When you visit [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall"), it is clear that the mead hall has seen better days, as it is currently inhabited by [rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling"), without a single proud Nord in sight. Head east from the Hall and locate [Bujold's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Bujold's Retreat"), where you will find the former Nord inhabitants, clearly exiled from their own Hall and quite frustrated and embarrassed. As you enter the camp, you will witness a heated discussion between [Bujold](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold_the_Unworthy "Skyrim:Bujold the Unworthy") and [Kuvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Kuvar "Skyrim:Kuvar"):

*"We'll act when I say we do and not before."*

**Bujold**: *"It won't be that easy to get rid of the Rieklings, Kuvar."*
**Kuvar**: *"I never said it would be. But either way, we have to try. Whether we succeed or not, it'll stir up some of the old blood in this crowd."*
**Bujold**: *"I'm not going to lead them to their deaths if they aren't ready."*
**Kuvar**: *"Then train them. What are we doing here? We should either get used to staying here, or be preparing to retake the hall. You're having us do neither, and I can't stomach it."*
**Bujold**: *"Your stomach isn't my problem. We'll act when I say we do and not before."*
**Kuvar**: *"Well, you'd better say something. And soon."*

Talking to the other residents reveals that everyone is unhappy about living in the remote camp, instead of the cozy warmth they are used to in the Hall. If you seek out Kuvar, he will explain it: *"We brought ourselves out here, along with our shame. We used to be proud warriors of Thirsk Mead Hall. There, up on the hill. But we let that sweet life get the better of us. We grew soft, and..."* He then tells you what happened: *"Rieklings. Those filthy vermin... they came in numbers. Waves of the things. One at a time, they're pests, but with this many... And so here we are, out of our home."*

### The Unworthy

Locate the leader with the unflattering byname, Bujold the Unworthy, and ask her what is going on. Like Kuvar, she will be painfully honest: *"What's going on here is that we've been kicked out of our home."* She then proceeds to explain that rieklings took over the Hall and will explain how the mighty warriors lost the battle against the small vermin: *"With tenacity and numbers. Didn't help that we'd grown a little too comfortable up there. Too much mead. Too many stories. Too few battles."* While it is clear that the Nords drank themselves out of their home, ask her if she needs any help and she will gladly accept and reason that *"Some new blood should be enough to rouse these layabouts to actually fight again."* At this point, consider completing [a favor quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Elmus_Favor_Quest_(mead) "Skyrim:Elmus Favor Quest (mead)") for camp inhabitant [Elmus](/wiki/Skyrim:Elmus "Skyrim:Elmus") (it becomes unavailable once this quest is started) - and consider if you want to help the Nords or not, as you will miss out on the quest [The Chief of Thirsk Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Chief_of_Thirsk_Hall "Skyrim:The Chief of Thirsk Hall").

### Retaking Thirsk

As soon as you agree to help the Nords, the quest will initiate and Bujold will gather her warriors with the words:

*"Hey, you lazy milk-drinkers, get over here! I know you're all starting to settle in here, and keep up the fat lives you got used to up in the hall. But look here. This outsider has more fire than any of you. All I had to do was mention our little infestation, and he/she volunteered in a second! I don't want to have my spirit outstripped by some wanderer. So let's get up there and kill us some Rieklings!"*

After the speech, all the warriors will draw weapons and set off at a running pace towards Thirsk Mead Hall, determined to reclaim it and wipe out the rieklings. You will have no choice but to tag along and fight a total of nineteen angry rieklings defending their new property. A total of six rieklings will defend the exterior while the rest will be inside, doing everything they can to protect their property, including the [riekling chief](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Chief "Skyrim:Riekling Chief") himself. The chief can only be wounded by the Nords to the point where he drops into the recovery position; it falls to you to finish him off. When all is said and done and dead rieklings lie everywhere in the Hall, locate Bujold who will be exhilarated by the battle and ask how you feel. Regardless of your answer, she will ask you to be her 'second' for a journey, as she needs to get another blessing from [Hrothmund the Red](/wiki/Lore:Hrothmund_the_Red "Lore:Hrothmund the Red") before the Nords again take up residence in the Hall.

### Hrothmund's Barrow

Bujold will lead you to a Nordic ruin called [Hrothmund's Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrothmund%27s_Barrow "Skyrim:Hrothmund's Barrow"), southwest of [Benkongerike](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike "Skyrim:Benkongerike"). Near the entrance she will turn around and ask you whether you are ready or not. You can then ask her what this place is and she will explain the full background: *"The burial place of Hrothmund, who founded Thirsk. He brought a group of true warriors away from the soft life of the Skaal, to know the wilderness, to feel the sting of cold and of steel. I know that... sounds a little silly. It's just the way it's written in the books, and that phrase has always stuck with me."* She will also explain what will happen in the barrow: *"It's pretty simple. Hrothmund's axe is in there with him. Anyone who attempts to take hold of it has their spirit judged by Hrothmund himself."* She will then reveal that she is quite confident that she will receive Hrothmund's blessing once again. After all, she received it before.

### The Spirit of Hrothmund

Inside the barrow, head through the first empty chamber and enter a huge water-filled room. As you approach, the water will disappear, and the now-visible path will lead you right to Hrothmund's Axe, where Bujold will try and grab it, as per tradition. When she does, [Hrothmund's spirit](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrothmund "Skyrim:Hrothmund") will speak:

*"Then... the leadership is not mine?"*

**Hrothmund**: *"You seek my blessing for the leadership of Thirsk Hall?"*
**Bujold**: *"I do. It is I, Bujold. You blessed me in the past, and now I've rid the hall of Rieklings and returned it to its rightful owners."*
**Hrothmund**: *"And well it is that this has happened. But I have always watched, and know that it was your softness that led to your own exile."*
**Bujold**: *"No! I..."*
**Hrothmund**: *"You allowed your fellow warriors to grow weak while the dangers around you mounted."*
**Bujold**: *"Then... the leadership is not mine?"*
**Hrothmund**: *"No. Nor is there any among you fit to serve. For a band in the wilderness, it is better to have no leader than a poor one."*
**Hrothmund**: Go forth and seek your fortunes. Inhabit the hall as you may. In time, a true leader worthy of the Thirsk name may arise."
**Hrothmund**: But I see that new leader's coming is yet far off in the distant horizon."

After her conversation with Hrothmund, an embarrassed Bujold will approach you and two options will be available, although both will lead to Bujold making the decision to return to Thirsk Mead Hall and continue her leadership as if Hrothmund had given his blessing. She will explain why: *"No matter what Hrothmund says, we need a leader. And I'm still the best person for that."* When you point out that she goes against Hrothmund's wishes she will continue: *"Look what's happened to us so far under his watchful eye. He gave his blessing to all the leaders who brought us to this point. Anyway, he's dead and we're alive. It's time to begin a new tradition for Thirsk. And I'm going to do that. All I need is for you to back me up. You don't even need to lie... just don't tell anyone else what you heard here."*

**Your next decision will make a huge difference for Bujold and maybe even cost you a few useful relationships within Thirsk Mead Hall.**

With Bujold determined to keep leading the mead hall regardless of Hrothmund's wishes, you must decide whether to intervene and end her leadership. After she tells you her plan, you will have two options:

**NOTE**: The quest will end right after you make the decision, and no reward will be given, so think carefully what benefits you the most: your relationship with [Kuvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Kuvar "Skyrim:Kuvar") or the old Nord traditions of Hrothmund.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| *"Get out of here. Run to the wilds."*  **Follow Bujold** If you choose to accept Bujold's scheme, she will simply end the quest and walk away with the words: *"Good. See that you do. Now, if you'll excuse me, I have a hall to lead."* When you return to Thirsk Mead Hall, Bujold will wander around carrying a new name, specifically Bujold the Intrepid. As soon as you enter, Kuvar will approach you and say: *"Bujold says you served well. Before we were married, I was her second on the first trip to the barrow. Hrothmund knows strength, in this world and the next."* You can either tell him the truth, that she was rejected by Hrothmund, or lie, saying that it was an honor to accompany her. Think twice before choosing, because Kuvar is a master [trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") in [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor"): **TRUTH**: *"I don't think you know how dangerous it is to say what you've just said. This is a serious accusation. I'm sure Bujold can straighten it out for us.."* He will then seek out Bujold and demand to hear the truth. Bujold will be taken by surprise by your betrayal and will admit everything, much to the regret of her husband. The argument ends with a heartbroken Kuvar asking Bujold to leave Thirsk and run to the wilds.  Trying to talk to Kuvar further will reveal that he now holds a grudge towards you for separating him from his wife, meaning that he will no longer offer training.  **LIE**: *"Yes, I remember how I felt being there with her the first time, before we were wed. I hope to see you more around the hall, friend."*  He will then continue his daily routine and will offer training. | Bujold attacks  **Follow Hrothmund** If you choose to follow ancient Nord tradition and say: *"I can't let you lead Thirsk."*, Bujold will be quite sad when she says: *"I was afraid you might say that. Well, looks as though I'll have to prove my mettle against you now."* She will then draw her [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_War_Axe "Skyrim:Nordic War Axe") and proceed to attack in order to keep her secret. Once she is dead, the quest will finish and Thirsk will be left without a leader. A return to the now cleaned-up mead hall will net you a concerned Kuvar who demands to know what happened to his wife: *"How did things go out there? Where is Bujold?"* You can then choose to tell the truth, that she was rejected, or lie and tell him you don't know what happened to her. Think twice before choosing, because he is a master [trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") in [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor"): **TRUTH**: *"Are you being serious? How... how did she take it?"* When you tell him she attacked you, he will respond: *"Ah. I see. I hope she... fought well. Was it... did Hrothmund recognize anyone else? Was it you? Is that why..."* When you tell him that Hrothmund said the next leader is a long way off, he will accept this, although he will refuse to speak to you again: *"Well, then. I'll do my best to keep the hall together until that day comes. Now, look... I understand you were just defending yourself. And because you helped us retake the hall, I'll look past it this once. But I wouldn't show my face in here again, if I were you. Do we understand each other?"*  Trying to talk to Kuvar further will reveal that he now holds a grudge towards you for separating him from his wife, meaning that he will no longer offer training.  **LIE**: *"Well, let's hope she makes it back soon. This lot doesn't have much patience with me."*  He will then continue his daily routine and will offer training. |

## Notes

- Should you choose to tell Bujold that you will keep her secret, then tell Kuvar the truth, Bujold will be disabled and disappear from the game as soon as she leaves Thirsk Mead Hall.
- If you delay too long in responding to Bujold after her conversation with the spirit of Hrothmund the quest will autocomplete (advance to stage 200) as if you had agreed with her actions.
- Once the warriors have cleaned up the mead hall, three new favor quests will be available. See [this section](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall#Miscellaneous_Quests "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall") for details.
- Before volunteering to assist the Nords in retaking the hall, you can kill all of the Rieklings that currently inhabit it, save the chief who is flagged as essential at this point. When you then join the assault with Bujold, no Rieklings will be waiting outside, and the chief will only have eight warriors inside to help him fight off the attackers.
- The total number of Rieklings to kill given in the relevant quest objective can be as high as twenty, but will vary based on how many are still alive.
- After you finish the quest, Bujold's retreat will become abandoned, and its map marker will be removed.

## Bugs

- Even after you finish the quest, the chairs inside Thirsk may still not work.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- If you've returned [Bilgemuck](/wiki/Skyrim:Bilgemuck "Skyrim:Bilgemuck") to the rieklings before starting this quest, he'll remain outside the hall indefinitely even after it's been retaken by the Nords.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=14953))
- Rieklings may continue to spawn outside and inside the mead hall even after Bujold's visit to Hrothmund's Barrow. It is unclear whether this was intentional, but the presence of rieklings inside the hall can interfere with normal completion of the quest by prematurely ending Kuvar's questions about what happened in the barrow.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
- It is possible to end up in a situation where Rieklings being killed are not properly counted.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.5, addresses this issue. The scripts involved (DLC2MH01QuestScript and DLC2MHRieklingHandlerQuestScript) were using improper operations to change the global variable value.
- [Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri") has a rumor which should have started this quest. Two separate issues prevent the line from being played, however.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.2, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=28409))
- If you kill the Rieklings too quickly before the Nords arrive, the quest may be stuck on the "Kill the Rieklings" objective while Bujold's group stands around in the hall with their weapons drawn.
  -  Open the [Console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") and type `setstage DLC2MH01 25` and hit enter. This should advance the quest to the next stage.
- On [Switch](/wiki/Skyrim:Switch "Skyrim:Switch"), upon your first encounter, Bujold may already be named "the Intrepid" instead of "the Unworthy", and the dialogue option to start this quest will not be available.
- If you have already discovered Hrothmund's Barrow and fast-travel to it, Bujold may not show up at the barrow where the arrow points. This can be solved by using her prid and the "moveto player" command in the console. **?**
- Hrothmund's voice lacks the ghost effect used by other spirits.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.

| 20 |  | I've agreed to help the Nords from Thirsk Mead Hall take their home back from the Rieklings who have infested it. *Objective 20:* Approach Thirsk Mead Hall  *Objective 21:* Kill the Rieklings (<Global=DLC2MH01RieklingsKilled>/<Global=DLC2MH01RieklingsTotal>) *(as you approach the hall)* |

Their leader, Bujold, has asked me to accompany her to Hrothmund's Barrow, where she hopes to receive the blessing of Thirsk's founder to continue her leadership. *Objective 27:* Meet Bujold at Hrothmund's Barrow |

Their leader, Bujold, asked me to accompany her to Hrothmund's Barrow, where she was denied the blessings of Thirsk's founder. She expressed a desire to lead the hall anyway, and when I opposed her fraud, she attacked me. *Objective 40:* Defeat Bujold |

Their leader, Bujold, asked me to accompany her to Hrothmund's Barrow, where she was denied the blessings of Thirsk's founder. She expressed a desire to lead the hall anyway, and plans to begin a new tradition at Thirsk, focused on the present instead of the past. |
| ☑ | I helped the warriors of Thirsk Mead Hall retake their home from the infestation of Rieklings. Their leader, Bujold, asked me to accompany her to Hrothmund's Barrow, where she was denied the blessings of Thirsk's founder. She expressed a desire to lead the hall anyway, and when I opposed her fraud, she became enraged. I was forced to kill her to defend myself. |
| 210 | ☒ | I met a group of Nords who had been exiled from their former home in Thirsk Mead Hall, but chose to help the Rieklings keep them permanently evicted. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2MH01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2MH01`.

| Quest Giver: | [Aela the Huntress](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress") |

| ID: | CR11 |

A fragment of Wuuthrad

## Radiant Options

| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern") [Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock") [Lost Knife Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Knife_Hideout "Skyrim:Lost Knife Hideout") | [Orotheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Orotheim "Skyrim:Orotheim") | [Broken Helm Hollow](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Helm_Hollow "Skyrim:Broken Helm Hollow") [Faldar's Tooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Faldar%27s_Tooth "Skyrim:Faldar's Tooth") [Treva's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Treva's Watch") | [Redoran's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Redoran's Retreat") [Swindler's Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Swindler%27s_Den "Skyrim:Swindler's Den") [Valtheim Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Valtheim_Keep "Skyrim:Valtheim Keep") | [Fort Fellhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Fellhammer "Skyrim:Fort Fellhammer") |

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to the location of the [Fragment of Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fragment_of_Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Fragment of Wuuthrad").
2. Fight the enemies there, and grab the fragment.
3. Return to [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr").

## Detailed Walkthrough

This is a [radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant") quest that will take you to a random camp to retrieve one of the [Fragments of Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fragment_of_Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Fragment of Wuuthrad") that has been acquired by the [Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand"). You will need to fight your way through to the destination's boss chest, where you will find the fragment.

### Reward

| Levels[†](#intnote_LevelNote) | Reward[‡](#intnote_RewardBug) | USLEEP Reward |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 100 | 100 |
| 10–19 | 150 | 150 |
| 20–29 | 300 | 200 |
| 30–39 | 300 | 250 |
| 40+ | 300 | 300 |

[†](#note_LevelNote)Level is based on when the player completed the previous quest (or level one for the first quest), not the player's level when receiving the quest or its reward.

[‡](#note_RewardBug)The reward amounts for radiant Companions quests do not progress as intended.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=20007))

## Notes

- This quest is no longer available once [Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Wuuthrad") is reforged during [Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead"); you will be able to complete this quest only a few times. It is also possible to never receive this quest making 100% completition of the Companions quests impossible.
- To make sure you receive this quest make a save in [The Underforge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Underforge "Skyrim:The Underforge") during [The Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silver_Hand "Skyrim:The Silver Hand") before receiving the objective to participate in the blood ritual. Everytime you reload this save Aela's next radiant quest will be different.

## Bugs

- Accepting this quest while other Companions quests are active may leave you unable to complete it.
- You may receive this quest from Aela despite completing [Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead"). This may be caused after the events of [The Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silver_Hand "Skyrim:The Silver Hand"), accepting Aela's first quest, and accepting one of the other companion's quests. By the time you complete the Companions' quest line, Aela may have the second mission queued.
- After returning and reporting to Aela, your quest will be acknowledged as complete in the journal, but it may remain in your active quest list. If this happens, Aela will not give you any further Silver Hand radiant quest to do (but will still give [Skyrim:Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination "Skyrim:Animal Extermination") quests). This bug can occurr with any Silver Hand radiant quest. **?**

## Quest Stages

| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 100.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CR11 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CR11`.

# Skyrim:Return to Grace

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Convince a mourning [mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Greta "Skyrim:Greta") to go to the [local temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Svari](/wiki/Skyrim:Svari "Skyrim:Svari") |
| Location(s): | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") |
| Reward: | [Leveled Gold](#Reward) |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Greta](/wiki/Skyrim:Greta "Skyrim:Greta"), if Unofficial Skyrim Patch since v2.1.0 are installed) |
| ID: | SolitudeFreeform03 |

[Roggvir](/wiki/Skyrim:Roggvir "Skyrim:Roggvir")'s execution

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Svari](/wiki/Skyrim:Svari "Skyrim:Svari").
2. Speak to [Greta](/wiki/Skyrim:Greta "Skyrim:Greta").
3. Retrieve [Roggvir](/wiki/Skyrim:Roggvir "Skyrim:Roggvir")'s [amulet of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Talos "Skyrim:Amulet of Talos").
4. Return the amulet to Greta.

### A Concerned Child

When first entering [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), you will witness the execution of [Roggvir](/wiki/Skyrim:Roggvir "Skyrim:Roggvir"), the guard that allowed [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") to escape Solitude after murdering [High King Torygg](/wiki/Skyrim:High_King_Torygg "Skyrim:High King Torygg"). During this, a child named [Svari](/wiki/Skyrim:Svari "Skyrim:Svari") is being sent home by her [father](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvar "Skyrim:Addvar") to spare her from seeing her uncle's execution. Svari can always be found in the streets of Solitude between 10am and 8pm when she plays with the other children. Approach her and she will appear quite sad about recent events, specifically with her uncle. When you tell her you are sorry about what happened with Roggvir, she will respond: *"Thanks. Papa talks about it some. Mum doesn't say much since Uncle Roggvir died. She doesn't even go to Temple anymore. I wish she would. At least that way she'd have people to talk to."* When you offer to talk to her mother, Svari will encourage you to do it right away and the quest will initiate.

### The Grieving Sister

Svari's mother [Greta](/wiki/Skyrim:Greta "Skyrim:Greta") can usually be found in the [family house](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvar%27s_House "Skyrim:Addvar's House") across the street from the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College") or browsing the market between 3pm and 6pm. Approaching her will reveal that she is both bitter and sad about the execution of her brother. When confronted with Svari's concerns, she will respond: *"She did, did she? She's going to get a sit down later."* When you tell her that Svari just wants to see her mother return to the [temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines"), she will explain her [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") beliefs: *"Well. I wish it were that simple. Maybe it is. Look, I want to go back but I won't feel right in there without a tie to [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos"). My brother Roggvir wore a symbol of Talos. He kept it hidden on his person. If I had that... I can't go near his body. Would you get it back for me?"* Agree to help her and the quest will update and a map marker will point you towards the body of Roggvir.

### Return to Grace

If you started the quest within three days after entering Solitude, Roggvir's headless body will still lie behind the chopping block where he met his demise. If not, his body will be inside the [Solitude Catacombs](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Catacombs "Skyrim:Solitude Catacombs") behind the [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Solitude) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Solitude)"). Enter the catacombs and fight the [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") then locate Roggvir's coffin near the entrance. Pry it open and claim the [Amulet of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Talos "Skyrim:Amulet of Talos") then exit the catacombs. Locate Greta who will cheer up a bit when you hand her the amulet: *"Thanks so much. I'll return to temple. Here's something for your time and effort."* She will then hand you a [reward](#Reward) and the quest will end. From this point forward, Greta will enter the Temple of the Divines every morning at 6am for nine hours of praying, holding her forbidden Amulet of Talos.

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 250 |
| 10–19 | 400 |
| 20–29 | 500 |
| 30–39 | 600 |
| 40+ | 750 |

## Notes

- If you carry another Amulet of Talos in your inventory, the game identifies them all as quest items. You will have to choose the dialogue option before you can drop, sell, or build with any Amulet of Talos.

## Bugs

- If you wait to loot the Amulet of Talos from Roggvir's corpse until you receive the quest, when you offer to give an amulet to Greta, it does not complete the quest, gain a reward, nor does it remove an Amulet of Talos. The dialogue option disappears nevertheless and the amulet(s) are dropable/sellable.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- If you loot the amulet from Roggvir's corpse before talking to Greta, the same problems occur as above. The dialogue option disappears, but not the quest journal entry. It also makes the amulet(s) dropable/sellable.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, fixes this bug.
  -  A solution is to proceed to talk to Svari, then talk to Greta. Mention going to temple, and after she asks you to retrieve the amulet, exit the conversation. Do *not* choose the "Actually I've got it here" option. Now in the console, type `setStage SolitudeFreeform03 20`, this will set the quest to the moment you are supposed to retrieve the amulet. Since you already have it, go into the console once more and type `setStage SolitudeFreeform03 30` which will set the moment you should have picked the amulet up. Return to Greta and give the amulet. It will complete the quest and will be removed from the log, though the amulet still stays in your inventory and you won't get the reward she mentions.
  -  Another solution is, before talking to Greta (or in some cases Svari), to use the console command `player.drop 000CC846 x` (with x being the number of Amulets of Talos you have in your inventory +1) in order to drop all Amulets of Talos. No matter how many you have, one of it (the one relevant for the quest) will always drop separately. After talking to Greta and promising her to retrieve the amulet, just pick up all the amulets you've dropped and talk to her to finish the quest (you might get a leveled reward and complete the quest using this method).
  -  If you end up with two Amulet of Talos in your inventory, you could try the console command, `player.removeitem 000CC846 1` to eliminate the duplication.
  - You can get rid of the quest journal entry and make the amulet dropable/sellable without any console commands by killing Greta before telling her that you have the amulet.
    - If you tell her you that you have the amulet before you kill her, the amulet is fixed but the quest entry remains in your journal indefinitely.
- When you offer Greta the amulet, sometimes she doesn't take the amulet or give you the reward, but the quest is completed.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- Greta's disposition towards you does not increase after completing the quest as it should.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.0, fixes this bug.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage SolitudeFreeform03 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest SolitudeFreeform03`.

The war is not over yet

## Quick Walkthrough

Regain each of Skyrim's [Holds](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") (depending upon your choices during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending")):

1. Regain [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale").
2. Regain [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift").
3. Regain [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)").
4. Regain [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch").
5. Regain [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath").
6. Regain [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach").
7. Regain [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch").

## Detailed Walkthrough

After defending [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") from the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") during the previous quest, [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Imperial)"), the [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") will finally side with the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). Go to [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") to report your success to [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius"). He will award you your first promotion, the rank of [Quaestor](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion#Ranks "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"), along with a [leveled enchanted weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Enchanted_Weapons "Skyrim:Leveled Lists") and order you to meet [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") at one of many [Imperial Military Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Camps#Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Military Camps") for your next assignment; depending on your progress through the [Main Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Main_Quest "Skyrim:Main Quest") the Camp you will be sent to will change as follows.

### Quest Options

This quest governs the overall progress of the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") for the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). It serves as an "umbrella quest", taking you through a series of individual quests that you receive as it progresses.

The overall goal of the quest is to conquer, for the Empire, each [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") of Skyrim that is currently under Stormcloak control. You will accomplish this one hold at a time, by taking control of the [military fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") in each, ending with one final siege on the enemy's capital, [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), in the order of the following table. The holds to be conquered can be altered by negotiation during the optional quest [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") and therefore only a subset of the following quests needs to be completed.

- Without doing Season Unending, only the Stormcloak-controlled holds in the following table need to be conquered.
- By doing Season Unending:
  - The initially allied-controlled holds only need to be reconquered if given to the enemy during negotiation.
  - The initially enemy-controlled holds will not need to be conquered if taken from the enemy during negotiation.
  - The initially enemy-controlled holds will need to be conquered if not taken during negotiation.
  - If you progress it to the point of a truce, any active quest in the series will auto-complete and cannot be restarted. If that quest involves a Military Fort, the related hold is transferred to allied control.
  - This quest will be put on hold, until you complete [Dragonslayer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonslayer "Skyrim:Dragonslayer").

| Hold | Initial Allegiance | Imperial Camp | Quests |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | Imperial | *None* | Always Imperial-controlled (if you have joined the Imperials) |
| [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | Neutral | [Whiterun Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Whiterun Imperial Camp") | Always becomes Imperial-controlled during the previous quest, [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Imperial)") |
| [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | Stormcloaks [[1]](#intnote_Treaty) | [Pale Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Pale Imperial Camp") | - [A False Front](/wiki/Skyrim:A_False_Front_(Imperial) "Skyrim:A False Front (Imperial)") - [The Battle for Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Dunstad_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Dunstad (Imperial)") |
| [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | Stormcloaks [[1]](#intnote_Treaty) | [Rift Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Rift Imperial Camp") | - [Compelling Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Compelling_Tribute_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Compelling Tribute (Imperial)") - [The Battle for Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Greenwall_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Greenwall (Imperial)") |
| [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") | Stormcloaks [[1]](#intnote_Treaty) | [Winterhold Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Winterhold Imperial Camp") | - [Rescue from Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Kastav") |
| [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | Imperial [[1]](#intnote_Treaty) | [Hjaalmarch Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch Imperial Camp") | - [The Battle for Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Snowhawk_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Snowhawk (Imperial)") |
| [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | Imperial [[1]](#intnote_Treaty) | [Falkreath Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Falkreath Imperial Camp") | - [The Battle for Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Neugrad") |
| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | Imperial [[1]](#intnote_Treaty) | [Reach Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Reach_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Reach Imperial Camp") | - [The Battle for Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Sungard_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Sungard (Imperial)") |
| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | Stormcloaks | [Eastmarch Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Eastmarch Imperial Camp") | Eastmarch is always the final hold that needs to be conquered.  - [The Battle for Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Amol "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Amol") - [Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm") |

[^1](#note_Treaty)These holds can change sides during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending").

### Reporting for duty

Between each hold conquest, you will be prompted to report to your faction leader for a reward and the next hold assignment. Then, to get your orders, you need to speak to [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") at the Military Camp you are assigned to with the *"Reporting for duty."* option.

### The Pale

:   *The Pale does not need to be regained if it was given to the Imperials during Season Unending*

Report to Legate Rikke at the [Pale Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Pale Imperial Camp").

- **[A False Front](/wiki/Skyrim:A_False_Front_(Imperial) "Skyrim:A False Front (Imperial)")**: Find and deliver some forged [documents](/wiki/Skyrim:StormCloak_Documents "Skyrim:StormCloak Documents") to the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks").
- **[The Battle for Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Dunstad_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Dunstad (Imperial)")**: Take [Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dunstad "Skyrim:Fort Dunstad") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

**Reward**: [Praefect](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion#Ranks "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") rank with leveled sword (see [Bugs](#Bugs)).

### The Rift

:   *The Rift does not need to be regained if it was given to the Imperials during Season Unending*

Report to Legate Rikke at the [Rift Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Rift Imperial Camp").

- **[Compelling Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Compelling_Tribute_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Compelling Tribute (Imperial)")**: Use a [corrupt steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Anuriel "Skyrim:Anuriel") to gain intelligence on the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Battle for Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Greenwall_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Greenwall (Imperial)")**: Take [Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greenwall "Skyrim:Fort Greenwall") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) ( 10 pts/Bronze)

**Reward**: [Tribune](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion#Ranks "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") rank with leveled shield (see [Bugs](#Bugs)).

### Winterhold

:   *Winterhold does not need to be regained if it was given to the Imperials during Season Unending*

Report to Legate Rikke at the [Winterhold Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Winterhold Imperial Camp").

- **[Rescue from Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Kastav")**: Take [Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Fort Kastav") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") and rescue the prisoners within. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

**Reward**: [Legate](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion#Ranks "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") rank with leveled armor.

### Hjaalmarch

:   *Hjaalmarch only needs to be regained if it was given to the Stormcloaks during Season Unending*

Report to Legate Rikke at the [Hjaalmarch Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch Imperial Camp").

- **[The Battle for Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Snowhawk_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Snowhawk (Imperial)")**: Retake [Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Snowhawk "Skyrim:Fort Snowhawk") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

**Reward**: leveled sword.

### Falkreath Hold

:   *Falkreath Hold only needs to be regained if it was given to the Stormcloaks during Season Unending*

Report to Legate Rikke at the [Falkreath Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Falkreath Imperial Camp").

- **[The Battle for Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Neugrad")**: Retake [Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Fort Neugrad") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

**Reward**: leveled sword.

### The Reach

:   *The Reach only needs to be regained if it was given to the Stormcloaks during Season Unending*

Report to Legate Rikke at the [Reach Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Reach_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Reach Imperial Camp").

- **[The Battle for Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Sungard_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Sungard (Imperial)")**: Retake [Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) ( 10 pts/Bronze — only if [The Battle for Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Greenwall_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Greenwall (Imperial)") did not need to be completed)

**Reward**: leveled sword.

### Eastmarch

:   *Eastmarch always needs to be regained as it hosts the enemy's capital*

Report to Legate Rikke at the [Eastmarch Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Eastmarch Imperial Camp").

- **[The Battle for Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Amol "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Amol")**: Prepare for the final assault on [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") by taking [Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Amol "Skyrim:Fort Amol") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm")**: Conquer the [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [capital](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") and bring [Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") to justice! ( 30 pts/Silver)

**Reward**: leveled enchanted sword.

After completing [The Battle for Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Amol "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Amol"), return to Rikke who will tell you *"We're taking the city. Meet the soldiers gathering for the attack. Move it!"*. This will automatically start [Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm"). As part of that quest, [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") will have a short dialogue with [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak"), who will request the Dragonborn to be the one who kills him, as it will "make for a better song." General Tullius won't care whether you kill Ulfric or not, just as long as he's dead. If you choose to kill Ulfric, General Tullius will tell you to use his sword (which is a leveled enchanteed sword) to do the deed (this is not required though) and Battle for Windhelm will be complete once you deliver the final blow. If you choose to allow Tullius to do it, Battle for Windhelm will complete after that, when General will reward you with his leveled enchanted sword.
Either way, Reunification of Skyrim will now be complete and you can join Rikke and Tullius outside to hear him delivering the final speech of the Civil War, promising increased pay and freedom for them to return to their families while giving compensation to families who have lost loved ones. Then, you're allowed to talk to Legate Rikke and General Tullius on what will happen next. Congratulations, [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") is now part of the [Empire](/wiki/Lore:Empire "Lore:Empire") once again and peace is restored.

## Notes

- This quest is mainly used to move you between the other Imperial quests.
- This quest and [Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim") are different radiant versions of the same quest.
- Season Unending can be started anytime from prior to starting the Civil War Quest-line to when there are at least 2 holds left for you to conquer for your allied side.
- If, after [Dragonslayer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonslayer "Skyrim:Dragonslayer"), depending on when the truce halted this quest, there is no quest mark, to resume it, you may need to speak to your faction leader.
- It is not possible to receive and complete all the potential quests in the series, as negotiation during Season Unending is limited.
- Trading the wrong holds during Season Unending can prevent obtaining some unique radiant quests from the series, [ranks](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion#Ranks "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") and [War Hero achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements#War_Hero "Skyrim:Achievements").
- Ranks are not automatic, they are rewarded if the conditions are met: successful attack (not fleeing) during the related quest and not obtaining the hold by negotiation during Season Unending.
- Ranks are progressive but not required: if you miss one, you can obtain the following one by completing the relative quest. So it is actually necessary to complete only [Rescue from Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Kastav") to obtain the final rank of Legate.
- Each rank comes with its leveled item reward.
- To check your rank you can spam-speak to any allied soldier until he greets you by your current rank.
- When a hold switches ownership, deposed [Jarls](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") and court/family are exiled, usually to their allegiance side's capital, and replaced by opposing ones, while related [Civil War Forts](/wiki/Skyrim:Forts#Civil_War_Forts "Skyrim:Forts") are re-garrisoned by the new owner's soldiers.
- At any point during this quest, enemy-controlled Civil War Forts are always garrisoned by enemy soldiers and will be garrisoned by allied ones when conquered. However initially allied-controlled ones remain inhabited by generic enemies, needing individual clearing.
- Any allied military camp located within an enemy hold disappears upon conquest of that specific hold.
- Legate Rikke will replace the Officer at any military camp for the duration of the hold assignment. If she is not there but the quest marker is upon an empty spot wait a few hours for her to arrive.
- After every quest of this series (except for [Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm")), unmarked by in-game references, you can approach Legate Rikke for a [medium leveled gold reward](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Gold_Rewards "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"); this is not always recommended though, as this is a cause for the missing *"Reporting for duty."* dialogue option (see [Bugs](#Bugs)).

## Bugs

|  |
| --- |
| **To meet our site's higher standard of quality, this article or section may require cleanup.**  **The user who placed this here had the following concern:** Lots of unlike fixes; need in-game and CK testing, removal of fake ones To leave a message about the cleanup for this article, please add it to this article's [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Reunification_of_Skyrim). |

- Legate Rikke may not offer the *"Reporting for duty."* dialogue option.
  - This is not a proper bug, more like a soft-lock, sometimes deterministically caused by player's actions, and may or may not be solvable. Try the following fixes, listed from the most to least reliable. If you still can't fix it, you may need to identify when you triggered the bug and reload a save file previous to that point, then progress the quests in the series in a different order. The safest way to prevent the hardest version of this bug to happen at all is to do all the quests in the series straight away, skip [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"), do it before the Civil War Quest-line or between completed quests from this series, avoiding as much as possible Legate Rikke, as loading her cell can improperly set up the next quest, even if you don't speak to her.
  - If you progressed Season Unending to the point of a truce, Legate Rikke will offer dialogue only after you complete [Dragonslayer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonslayer "Skyrim:Dragonslayer").
  - Go to any indoor location and wait/rest for 30+ days. This allows all location cells to respawn.
  - If the fort that was supposed to be the target of the next mission is occupied by generic enemies, kill them. Then travel away and spend some time (e.g. wait for 24h).
  - Ask General Tullius *"How goes the war?"* until the phrase is no longer white (the indicator that he has something new to say).
  - Repeatedly talk to Rikke then run into her to interrupt her dialogue.
  - Go to jail and serve time.
  - Activate the [Beast Form](/wiki/Skyrim:Lycanthropy#Beast_Form "Skyrim:Lycanthropy") and wait until it wears out.
  -  The console command `movetoqt CWObj` can be used to teleport you to the current objective of this quest, aka Legate Rikke.
  - If you manage to move Legate Rikke to another location (for example by making her follow you, casting a [frenzy spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Frenzy_(effect)#Spells "Skyrim:Frenzy (effect)") and [pacifying](/wiki/Skyrim:Pacify_(effect) "Skyrim:Pacify (effect)") afterwards), then letting her walk back to the current Imperial Camp can fix it. You can also attack her until she becomes hostile.
    -  The console commands `prid 198BB` to target her then `moveto player` can be used to teleport her to your current location.
  - Triggering her hostility (for example by random enemies) and going outside the camp also resets Rikke.
  -  Head to General Tullius. Talk to him, then exit out and open up the console command `getstage cwobj` to verify the variable is set to 1.00. If it is so, enter `resetquest cwobj`. Use `getstage cwobj` to confirm the quest stage is 0.00. Enter `setstage cwobj 1`.
  -  The console command `coc` followed by location code of the imperial camp (for example `coc MilitaryCampReachImperial`) can be used to teleport to the chosen Military Camp.
  -  It is possible the last fort you captured has not properly registered as Imperial. You can manually set ownership of the fort through console command. First enter an interior location, then use `help 'Fort Dunstad'` (replace with the fort you just tried to capture) to obtain its LCTN: variable (something like 00019182). Then, use `GetKeywordDataForLocation %LCTN% CWOwner` to check the owner of this location; if it shows 0 (nobody) or 2 (Stormcloaks), then use `SetKeywordDataForLocation %LCTN% CWOwner 1`. After that, the 'Reporting for duty' prompt should appear.
  -  At the regain Eastmarch stage, if the *"Reporting for duty."* dialogue is not offered by Rikke to start [Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Amol "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Amol"), travel to Fort Amol and kill every necromancer. After that, sleep in one of the beds and Stormcloaks should occupy the Fort. Use `movetoqt CWObj` to directly teleport to Rikke. If the option doesn't show, talk to Tullius in Castle Dour by entering the following command in the console `coc SolitudeCastleDour`, and then go to Rikke with the previous command.
  -  If nothing else works, you may need complete the entire Reunification of Skyrim quest via the console command `setstage cwobj 255`. You cannot use the console to start the next quest within the series, as the bug applies to the over-arching quest.
  - This may be cleared by saving and resetting the entire system.
- After [The Battle for Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Dunstad_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Dunstad (Imperial)"), if General Tullius will promote you to Praefect rank you are actually promoted to Tribune with related leveled shield. It is not possible to get the actual Praefect rank. Since you already are, this will also "skip" the actual promotion to Tribune after [The Battle for Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Greenwall_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Greenwall (Imperial)").

  **Mod Notes**: mistake in the script TIF\_\_000CE0E8: there is "3", should be "2".
- The war strategy maps located at military bases and command headquarters do not update as intended.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, addresses this issue. Each map needs to be visited twice for the correction to take effect in saved games.
- After retaking Winterhold and upon talking to General Tullius, you will receive a piece of leveled armor. However, General Tullius may give you no further instructions and your journal has the text "Report to General Tullius". This prevents the quest line from continuing.
  - There is a way to force Tullius *"What's next"* option after he gave you the armor by setting ownership of Winterhold and Fort Kastav to the Empire manually through console command. First, use `help 'Fort Kastav'` to obtain LCTN: variable (something like 00019182) and `help 'Winterhold'` (there may be two of them). Then, use `GetKeywordDataForLocation %LCTN% CWOwner` for Fort Kastav and Winterhold LCTNs to check the owner of this locations; if any of them shows 2 (Stormcloaks), then use `SetKeywordDataForLocation %LCTN% CWOwner 1`. After that 'What's next' option should appear.
  - There may still be dialogue issues when you reach Winterhold. To prevent this, work through "Reunification of Skyrim" until you finish regaining Fort Greenwall. Before you report to General Tullius, finish the main questline. During "Season Unending", you will be given the option to put Winterhold on the negotiating table. It will most likely be the only option given, since you have control of the other holds thus far. If you choose that option, then all of the Imperial quests regarding Winterhold will be skipped and will automatically fall under Imperial control, without requiring you to attempt bugged conversations.
  - If there is still no dialogue option from Tullius to continue on in the quest after Winterhold, simply travel to the Eastmarch Imperial Camp and talk to Legate Rikke, that will proceed with the questline and she will give a reward as if you just completed a quest for her, even if it's the first time talking to her.

## Quest Stages

Only stages and objectives relevant to the Reunification of Skyrim (rather than Liberation of Skyrim) are included in the table.

| <Alias=QuestNameLocation> (CWObj) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 1 |  | I will help General Tullius quell the Stormcloak rebellion and reunite Skyrim by restoring Imperial control. |
|  |  | *(Displayed as needed)* *Objective 1001:* Report to General Tullius |
|  |  | *(Displayed as each hold becomes the new target)* *Objective 201:* Regain the Reach  *Objective 301:* Regain Hjaalmarch  *Objective 401:* Regain Whiterun Hold  *Objective 501:* Regain Falkreath Hold  *Objective 601:* Regain the Pale  *Objective 701:* Regain Winterhold Hold  *Objective 801:* Regain Eastmarch  *Objective 901:* Regain the Rift |
| 255 | ☑ | We have successfully quelled the rebellion by killing Ulfric Stormcloak and have reunited Skyrim under Imperial control. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CWObj stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CWObj`.

# Skyrim:Revealing the Unseen

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-College of Winterhold.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-College_of_Winterhold.png) | **Learn the location of the [Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:Staff of Magnus").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
