The Oculory's readings

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with [Mirabelle](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine") at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)").
2. Find the ruins of [Mzulft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzulft "Skyrim:Mzulft").
3. Find the [Synod researchers](/wiki/Skyrim:Synod_Researcher "Skyrim:Synod Researcher").
4. Find the Oculory.
5. Activate the Oculory.
6. Learn the location of the [Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:Staff of Magnus").
7. Report to [Savos Aren](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren") at the College of Winterhold.

### The Synod and the Staff

From the events of [Good Intentions](/wiki/Skyrim:Good_Intentions "Skyrim:Good Intentions"), you have learned from both the Augur of Dunlain and [Savos Aren](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren") that the [Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:Staff of Magnus") is a necessary part of averting the prophesied disaster. After speaking with Savos, ask [Mirabelle](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine") what she knows about the Staff of Magnus and its whereabouts. She is a bit skeptical at first, but does mention that the members of a mystical group, the [Synod](/wiki/Skyrim:Synod "Skyrim:Synod"), recently questioned her about it. While she did tell the mages that the College did not have the Staff she remembers the group talking about the Dwemer ruin [Mzulft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzulft "Skyrim:Mzulft"). She speculates that the Synod group may be traveling there to locate the Staff.

### Your Journey to Mzulft Begins

Mirabelle will mark Mzulft's location on your map: southeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). You may reach it by traveling on the road south from [Windhelm Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Stables "Skyrim:Windhelm Stables") toward [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). As you enter Mzulft's interior, you will find a Synod researcher, [Gavros Plinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Gavros_Plinius "Skyrim:Gavros Plinius"), uttering his final words, *"Crystal... gone.... Find...Paratus...in Oculory..."* Search Gavros to find a [research log](/wiki/Skyrim:Research_Log "Skyrim:Research Log") which indicates he was sent here by the Synod Council with a "focusing crystal" needed to pursue some mysterious effort, and that the crystal needs to get to the Oculory right away. Take the [Mzulft key](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzulft_Key "Skyrim:Mzulft Key") from his corpse to unlock the adjacent door. This man Paratus seems to be an important part of this puzzle, so travel through the extensive ruin to a curious device called the Oculory. Mzulft contains a wealth of Dwemer items and multitudes of the hostile creatures and machines that typically populate Dwemer ruins. A detailed guide to the Oculory is in the table below.

| Getting to the Oculory |
| --- |
| A Chaurus Reaper squashed by boulders  Steam piston trap, floor pressure plates Proceed through the door into a room containing a number of [Dwemer metallic items](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven "Skyrim:Dwarven"). Ascend a ramp at the far end of the room. Around the corner, a pressure plate on the floor activates a ceiling spike trap. Beyond this, the body of another [Synod researcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Synod_Researcher "Skyrim:Synod Researcher") lies on the floor. At the entrance to the next large room, you will encounter two [Dwarven spider workers](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider_Worker "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider Worker"). Two more spiders will attack in the room at the top of the next ramp. Two doors open from this room. The door to the north is guarded by a floor spike trap and contains some minor loot and a [moonstone ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore") vein. The other door takes you up a ramp and into a room where a Dwarven spider will spring from its port at the far end. From here, continue into an area illuminated by natural light. If you turn left next to the exit, jump over the rocks next to the tree, and go to the corner, you'll find a [Dwarven shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven#Dwarven_Armor "Skyrim:Dwarven"). A leveled [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") feasts on another researcher near the far end of the first cavern. The tunnel leading out has a tripwire that activates a [falling boulders](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") trap, and two more chaurus (one of them leveled) are scuttling about. At the top of the next ramp around the corner a [Dwarven sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere") will drop from a port just outside a locked gate. After battling the sphere, move up another ramp and through another door. Beyond this awaits another spider, and beyond that another sphere at the end of the hall. As you move further into the ruin you come to a room with stairs leading down to a pit, a corridor leading north, and a spider. In the next room, a sphere will meet you on the far side of a narrow ledge rigged with a [steam piston traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Steam_Piston "Skyrim:Steam Piston") and pressure plates which will only push you off into the pit below if activated. The door that leads to Mzulft Boilery is up a ramp to the east. A strong leveled Falmer roams the area at the top of the ramp beyond. You will also find another dead researcher before heading up the next ramp. At the top of the ramp, fight another leveled Falmer, and then two more in the room through an open doorway to the north. A gate to the north opens into an empty room. The way forward is through the smaller connected room to the east.  A Falmer chest Heading east will bring you to an area consisting of natural caverns. When you enter a fairly lengthy tunnel, prepare to meet a leveled chaurus. Exit the tunnel through a narrow opening to your left. You will then see to your right the opening to a cavern illuminated with a slightly bluish light. If you wait and watch, you may see the occupants of this cavern walking around: a leveled Falmer attended by a chaurus. A [claw trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Claw "Skyrim:Claw") which swings out from the left wall and is activated by a tripwire is behind a Falmer hut. A second chaurus will probably activate the tripwire on its way to meet you. Continue through the cavern as the path twists and turns. Ahead, there is another dead Synod researcher, and if they hear you, you might encounter two more Falmer here, one of which will be the highest-level variant you can encounter at your level, and the second will likely be nearly as strong. Your next left leads into a cavern containing another Falmer hut, and another dead Synod researcher near the doorway. The tunnel out is along the north wall, but be prepared to meet another chaurus in the next room. Further on, you will face a high-leveled Falmer in a room with a master-locked door leading to a chest and a copy of the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Lunar Lorkhan](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lunar_Lorkhan "Skyrim:The Lunar Lorkhan")*. On the table is a key that will open an expert-locked door just ahead. Continue west until you come to a large rectangular hall divided by a shallow pool. On the far side of the pool await two leveled Falmer. Another researcher lies just before the door in the northeast corner leading to Mzluft Aedrome. |

After a lengthy and adventurous journey, go through the door to the third interior area, Mzulft Aedrome. Ascend the ramp and near the top you will find a leveled Falmer and a chaurus. Continue toward a large, multi-leveled room that can be accessed through either of two open doorways. Inside prowl four leveled Falmer, including one of the strongest variant you will find at your level, and one that will be carrying the focusing crystal mentioned in Gavros's research log. You need to obtain the crystal to complete the quest.

### Mzulft Observatory

Your objective marker will point westward from here, but you should first obtain a key that you will need. To do this, leave the room through the doorway to the east and descend the ramp, then open the door at the bottom. Cross the next room and open another door leading eastward. Proceed until you reach a room containing two dead Falmer. Beyond the next door to the east waits a Dwarven automaton. It can be a [Dwarven Centurion](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Centurion "Skyrim:Dwarven Centurion") of the strongest type you can confront at your level. A Centurion on the other side will not be able to fit through the door to attack you up close, whether the machine breaks open the door or you open the door first. Keeping a distance makes it easy to dodge its steam attacks and pick at the machine with your own ranged attacks. After destroying it, obtain the [Mzulft Observatory key](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzulft_Observatory_Key "Skyrim:Mzulft Observatory Key") from the chest on the east side of the room. Retrace your steps westward, back into the large room where you battled the four Falmer.

Climb the stairs to the west and open the door there with the Observatory key. Beyond this, there is another locked door which you cannot open. When you try to do so, however, you will hear a voice from the other side, and the door will be opened by [Paratus Decimius](/wiki/Skyrim:Paratus_Decimius "Skyrim:Paratus Decimius"), a Synod member who is expecting Gavros, the dying man you met upon entering the ruin. Paratus will be suspicious of you; but whatever the course of your conversation, when he finds out that you have the focusing crystal, he will agree to work together with you and ask you to follow him. You will note in your quest journal that you have reached the Oculory and that your plan now is to follow Paratus to investigate further.

### At the Oculory

As he leads you forward, Paratus will explain that the Synod happened on this machine created by the Dwarves for unknown purposes, and that the Synod now intends to try to use it toward some different end. Ascend a curved ramp along a giant sphere, but be careful not to fall off, as doing so can cause you to become stuck. At the top, Paratus will marvel at the magnificence of the device there and ask you to place the crystal into the central apparatus.

Insert the Crystal into the gap at the bottom of the large ring.

Stand as shown (photo), and place the crystal by activating the "Dwarven Armillary".

When you have done so, the ring will rotate so that the focusing crystal is positioned at the top. Your objective will become to "Focus the Oculory". You will now have two objective markers, one pointing at the device in the center of the room and another at an elevated control console at the southeast part of the room. You can ask Paratus what to do next.

### Focus is the Key

Paratus will indicate that you should direct some fire and frost spells onto the crystal to change the way that it bends the light beams projected by the device.
If you look upward, you will see that the device receives one beam of light vertically, and splits it into three beams projected in various upward directions. The ultimate goal is to converge all of the beams into a pattern that will project an image on the wall below the control console.

| Puzzle Solution |
| --- |
| You may wish to save your game before taking the following steps:  1. You can climb the ramp at the southeast point in the room and obtain one or both spell tomes from the table there if you do not have both the [Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Flames "Skyrim:Flames") and [Frostbite](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite "Skyrim:Frostbite") Destruction spells. Only the Frostbite spell will work; it won't move the beams into the correct position if you use any other type of frost spell. The [Frost Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Breath "Skyrim:Frost Breath") shout will work, but only once, so you can't focus the crystal completely without the use of the Frostbite spell. 2. Return to the same position that you assumed when placing the crystal. 3. Notice that there are three horizontal blue bands circling the upper portion of the room, each with a round reflector positioned at some point around it. 4. Direct a Frostbite spell into the middle of the ring where you placed the crystal. When the beams move, cast a second Frostbite spell. When the beams move again, cast a third Frostbite spell. Note that Frostbite moves the lenses to the next "forward" position and casting Flames will move them "backward". Handy if you cast Frostbite too many times. Do not use other spells. 5. Step 5: Beam configuration after using spells Ensure that each of the three beams of light are now pointing into the middle of each blue band (none of the beams should point to the horizontal gold rims that separate the bands). You will need to move around to check all three beams. The photo indicates a correct configuration as viewed from the control console at the top of the ramp. When the lenses are in the correct position they will shine on the center of each band, not on the edges. 6. A focused Oculary Walk up the ramp at the southeast point in the room and use the buttons to rotate the bands until the round reflector on each band aligns with a light beam. The left button controls the top band, so press that until the beam aimed at the center of the top band meets the reflector. Then use the middle button to do the same for the middle band, and the right button to do so for the lower band. A sequence that will result in the proper alignment is:    1. Activate the left button once.    2. Activate the middle button six times.    3. Activate the right button five times.   When the Oculory is correctly focused, it will appear as shown. |

When the Oculory is correctly focused, Paratus will be initially excited, but then begin to exclaim with distress that there is something wrong. He will communicate that the map should show more, and speculate that there is some kind of interference coming from Winterhold. He may accuse you of attempting to stall his work and suspiciously ask if you knew what they are trying to do.

### Talk to Paratus

Paratus will be looking at a map projected onto the wall under the control console. Speak to him and he will accuse you of trying to sabotage the Synod's efforts and demand that you explain yourself. Whatever the course of the ensuing conversation, Paratus will ask if—or assume that—you have something "powerful" at your college. He will be suspicious about this and toward you, stating that he will be reporting the information to the Synod Council. You'll learn that the Synod intended to use the device to scan the continent for powerful sources of magic, "for the good of the Empire". One way or another, Paratus will let you know that the map indicates that the Staff of Magnus is in [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian"). You must now report this information to the Arch-Mage, Savos Aren.

After that, once you head towards the southern exit, a Psijic Monk called Nerien will briefly spawn to comment:
"You have done well thus far, but trying times are ahead.
It is imperative that you return to your College at once.
You will be called on to take swift action. Rise to the challenge,
and discover what you are capable of.
You are on the right path, and you will prevail."

### Report to Savos Aren

You may now take a shortcut exit or return the long way back through the ruin. To take the shortcut, leave the room containing the Oculory. A short distance ahead, just past the barrels in the hallway, there is an exit door to the right. If you turn toward it, [Nerien](/wiki/Skyrim:Nerien "Skyrim:Nerien"), the [Psijic Order](/wiki/Skyrim:Psijic_Order "Skyrim:Psijic Order") member who appeared to you in Saarthal, will visit you again. He will warn you that you will encounter difficulties ahead, but assure you that you are on the right path and that you will prevail. He will then urge you to return to the College immediately. You will not receive Nerien's visit if you leave through the main entrance, but this will not impact your progress through the quest.

Ancano casting a spell on the Eye of Magnus

As you enter the Hall of the Elements, you'll find Arch-Mage Savos and Mirabelle in a panic. The gate to the room containing [the Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Eye_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Eye of Magnus") is blocked by a barrier that Mirabelle speculates is some kind of ward, and the two of them implicate [Ancano](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancano "Skyrim:Ancano") in possibly creating it. They will then begin casting Destruction spells at the barrier in an attempt to destroy it. If you speak to Savos, he will ask for your help in destroying the barrier, and say that they need to know what Ancano is doing in there. You can help break down the barrier with Destruction spells, but whether you do or not, the door will eventually open, and they will rush in. Savos will approach Ancano, who is casting a spell at the Eye, and command him to stop. Mirabelle will warn Savos not to go near Ancano, but Savos will begin casting a spell at him. At this point, all will go white, and the next thing you experience will be awakening in the Hall of the Elements with Mirabelle asking if you are all right and saying that she needs your help. When you reply that you think you feel well, this quest will complete and the next quest, [Containment](/wiki/Skyrim:Containment "Skyrim:Containment"), will begin with the objective of finding the Arch-Mage, as Mirabelle requests of you.

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked when you complete this quest:

-  **Revealing the Unseen** (10 points/Bronze)

## Notes

- The objective to report to Savos Aren is never completed, and the objective to reach Ancano is never displayed or completed.

## Bugs

- Sometimes Mirabelle is inaccessible. The quest pointer points to the courtyard but she is nowhere to be found.
  - You can teleport her to you using the following console commands:
    - `prid 0001C1B9`
    - `moveto player`
- If you leave the Mzulft Aedrome after inserting the crystal in the armillary but before focusing the Oculory with the spells, it won't respond to them on your next visit, making the quest unsolvable; this may also occur if you save, quit and reload after placing the crystal.
- Mirabelle's second dialogue option in stage 99 may not advance the quest. Additionally, Mirabelle may be stuck on a rock outside the College wall; however, she can be accessed by jumping down toward her. **?**
- If the beams of light do not show up after placing the crystal in the Oculory, try exiting out of the game and restarting.
- At the end of the ruin, when you are in the Oculory, Paratus will sometimes "be busy" or will not have any new dialogue after you tell him you have the focusing crystal and again after you align the lights. **?**
  - Leave the Oculory room and take the right corridor to an exit door to Skyrim. Go out the door and re-enter and try to talk to Paratus again in the Oculory. Either Paratus will respond with new dialogue or a quest message will appear stating the stage has been completed. The audio for the conversation about Labyrinthian may not play, but the follow-up stage to "go tell Savos Aren at Winterhold" will become active.
- Sleeping just prior to adjusting the mirrors while having the Dark Brotherhood quest '[With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...")', active will automatically transport you to an [abandoned shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Shack "Skyrim:Abandoned Shack") in [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch"). After this, the mirrors will not adjust and pressing the buttons will not do anything. **?**
  - Reload a previous save and complete the Dark Brotherhood quest before continuing this one, or don't sleep until you complete the Oculory portion of this quest.
- Once you've cleared Mzulft Aedrome (final stage of the quest on "Reach the Oculory") there is a master-locked door at the bottom of the room, leading to a chest. It is possible to enter the top of the locked room and become stuck permanently, requiring you to reload your last save. **?**
- The Mzulft map marker isn't added by the quest as the scripting for it wasn't set up properly, and Gavros will not be in the entrance to Mzulft to give you the key. Updating the game to a newer version will not solve the problem for existing saved games.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- After returning from Mzulft, it is possible that none of Savos Aren's dialogue options will complete the objective "Report to Savos Aren" and give the next objective, "Reach Ancano". However, the scene continues and the quest completes as normal, but Containment (the next quest) never starts, rendering continuation of the College of Winterhold quest line impossible.
- After meeting Paratus and the journal entry changing to "Follow Paratus," he may not move and only repeat the previous dialogue asking who you are.
  - Kill him and resurrect him through [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") commands.
  - Go to the Oculory, then use the console command `"0007D41B".moveto player`. This will teleport him to you where he will proceed with the quest.
  - Attack him and lure him to the Oculory, then use a Calm spell to get him out of combat and he will proceed with the quest.
- Speaking with Mirabelle and accidentally exiting conversation before she finishes talking about the Staff of Magnus will forever take that dialogue option away. **?**
- Followers may be teleported inside the Hall of the Elements after Ancano knocks everyone unconscious, even if they have been told to wait elsewhere. If you do not tell them to follow you out of the hall before leaving the College, you will be unable to rejoin them until after completing the quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
- If you went and worked on something else prior to finishing this quest, when you go to restart it and select the quest again the map marker doesn't show up anywhere or on the map. If you fast travel back to Mzulft and go inside the doors the marker will come back.
- This quest will not activate if you have already cleared Mzulft by using the platter trick, console command, etc. to enter the unpickable key-locked doors.
  - Load a previous save from before Mzulft was cleared.
  - For the sake of trophy/achievement hunting you can restart/reload and just do the questline only to unlock them, then return to your main file.

| 20 |  | Mirabelle has told me that members of the Synod recently visited the College, mentioning the Staff of Magnus. They were last known to be heading towards Mzulft; they may know more about where to find the staff. *Objective 20:* Find the ruins of Mzulft |
| 25 |  | *Objective 25:* Search for Synod researchers |
| 30 |  | At Mirabelle's suggestion, I entered the ruins of Mzulft searching for the Synod researchers. I found one man who died, and suggested that more people may be inside at something called The Oculory. I should head further into the ruins to see what's going on. *Objective 30:* Reach the Oculory |
| 32 |  | At Mirabelle's suggestion, I entered the ruins of Mzulft searching for the Synod researchers. I found Paratus Decimius, who appears to be the only surviving member of the Synod expedition, and who has insisted that a "focusing crystal" is necessary to finish his experiment but was stolen by the Falmer. *Objective 32:* Find the Focusing Crystal |
| 35 |  | Exploring Mzulft while looking for information about the Staff of Magnus, I've encountered Paratus Decimius, the sole surviving member of a Synod expedition. I've found the focusing crystal he needs to finish his experiment, and should return it to him. *Objective 35:* Return the Crystal to Paratus |
| 37 |  | *Objective 37:* Follow Paratus |
| 40 |  | Paratus Decimius may know the location of the Staff of Magnus, but has asked for my help in completing an experiment in Mzulft. I need to follow him to the top of the ruins. *Objective 40:* Place the Crystal into the Oculory |
| 50 |  | Paratus Decimius may know the location of the Staff of Magnus, but has asked for my help in completing an experiment in Mzulft. I need to use magic to attenuate Paratus' focusing crystal, and then manipulate the dwarven machinery to line up the beams of light. *Objective 50:* Focus the Oculory |
| 55 |  | *Objective 55:* Talk to Paratus |
| 60 |  | Traveling to Mzulft in search of the Synod, I found Paratus Decimius who helped me learn that the Staff of Magnus is located in Labyrinthian. This information needs to get back to Savos Aren at the College immediately. *Objective 60:* Report to Savos Aren |
| 70 |  | After traveling to Mzulft and learning that the Staff of Magnus is located within Labyrinthian, I returned to the College to give the news to Arch-Mage Aren. Aren, however, is more concerned with the Eye of Magnus at the moment, since Ancano has locked himself in the Hall of the Elements with it. I need to help the Arch-Mage reach him at once. |
| 200 | ☑ | After finding the Synod in Mzulft, I learned that the Staff of Magnus can be found in Labyrinthian, and brought this news to the Arch-Mage. |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 70:* Reach Ancano |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 99.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MG06 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MG06`.

# Skyrim:Revenge, Hired Thugs

## Overview

|  |

Contract carried by thugs

## Walkthrough

If you murder an NPC who has a relative, the relative may subsequently send three [hired thugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Hired_Thug "Skyrim:Hired Thug") to hunt you down and teach you a lesson (i.e. kill you in vengeance). The thugs will be carrying a [contract](/wiki/Skyrim:Contract_(Murder) "Skyrim:Contract (Murder)") which reveals the name of the relative who hired the thugs.

## Notes

- You may also be attacked if you steal from someone (see [Steal, Thugs hunt player](/wiki/Skyrim:Steal,_Thugs_hunt_player "Skyrim:Steal, Thugs hunt player")).
- You can attack the thugs at a distance via magic or archery while they are non-hostile (before they get a chance to initiate dialogue with you) individually to make the fight easier; the ones not being attacked will remain non-hostile as they continue to approach, so you can thin their numbers before they actually get to talk to you.

## Bugs

- If you kill someone then kill any of their relatives then you may find that one of the hired thugs sent after you has a contract note from someone you have already killed.
- The thugs may be hired by [children](/wiki/Skyrim:Children "Skyrim:Children").

## Quest Stages

- All of the quest stages are empty: 0, 1, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage WIKill06 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest WIKill06`.

*This [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim")-related article is a [stub](/wiki/UESPWiki:Stub "UESPWiki:Stub"). You can help by [expanding it](https://en.uesp.net/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Revenge,_Hired_Thugs&action=edit).*

# Skyrim:Rielle

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Ayleid Ruin: Rielle ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rielle+%28CC%29)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Rielle "Lore:Rielle")) | | |
| Added by | [The Cause](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause") |

The interior of Rielle

**Rielle** is a medium-sized [Ayleid](/wiki/Lore:Ayleid "Lore:Ayleid") ruin located beneath the [Jerall Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Jerall_Mountains "Skyrim:Jerall Mountains"), just east of the [Pale Pass](/wiki/Lore:Pale_Pass "Lore:Pale Pass"). It straddles the border between [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") and County [Bruma](/wiki/Lore:Bruma "Lore:Bruma") in [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil"). In Skyrim, it is accessed from the north by way of [Varlais Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Varlais_Cavern "Skyrim:Varlais Cavern"), a cave entrance located to the south of [Arcwind Point](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcwind_Point "Skyrim:Arcwind Point"). It contains two zones: *[Rielle](#Rielle)* and *[Rielle Crypt](#Rielle_Crypt)*.

## Related Quests

- **[The Cause](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause_(quest) "Skyrim:The Cause (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause"): Investigate the activities of the [Mythic Dawn](/wiki/Lore:Mythic_Dawn "Lore:Mythic Dawn") cult.

## Walkthrough

The map is the same as it was in *[Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Rielle "Oblivion:Rielle")*, but entered through a different passage this time, as the Mythic Dawn have excavated through the mountains from the north, aiming for the northwest corner of the ruin. You can reach Rielle by entering [Varlais Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Varlais_Cavern "Skyrim:Varlais Cavern"), which is south along the path from the main sarcophagus (and [Word Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Drain_Vitality "Skyrim:Drain Vitality")) at [Arcwind Point](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcwind_Point "Skyrim:Arcwind Point"). Mythic Dawn cultists have dug through the back of Varlais Cavern in order to find the four Elemental Stones in the city, and use them to uncover a Great Welkynd Stone. The power of the great stone could reopen an Oblivion Gate and resume the Oblivion Crisis. However, their plans have been postponed by the hostile Ayleid Wights and Wight Lords who reside in Rielle; the undead have killed the Mythic Dawn's first team, apart from one explorer who lost her life to a [guillotine trap](/wiki/Oblivion:Traps#Falling_Blades "Oblivion:Traps") as she tried to flee. To make sure the Mythic Dawn doesn't get the Great Welkynd Stone on a second expedition and let Mehrunes Dagon in to finish what he started, you will have to obtain it first.

### Rielle

Janus and the other dead Mythic Dawn

Once you enter from Varlais Cavern through the hole that the Mythic Dawn Cultists have dug through the tomb wall, and explore further into the ruin, you will find the expedition leader, Janus lying dead in a large chamber. In his inventory is [his journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Janus%27_Journal "Skyrim:Janus' Journal"), which will explain what the explorers are doing here and what your next objective in turn will be.

Plentiful treasure can be found in the containers throughout the ruin, in Ayleid Casks and Urns. There are two floors in the main area, with the upper level consisting of walkways and the lower level being a larger area with many sarcophagi and containers.

### Rielle Crypt

The Great Welkynd Stone chamber within Rielle Crypt

Two doors into the crypt exist, but both place you in the southern section with a [large square rising pillar and ceiling spike trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Ceiling_Spikes "Skyrim:Traps") between you and the Great Welkynd Stone.

In the crypt, as you progress through the area, various gates will close behind you.

Once you reach the chamber for the four elemental shards, you will see a total of eight Welkynd Stone holders arranged in a square; one holder at each corner, and one in between each corner. The four side holders contain lootable Welkynd Stones, while the four corners are empty and can be used for the elemental shards. Double-check Janus's journal if you need to remember which shard and which element corresponds with which cardinal direction.

Once the shards are in place, they become part of the environment and cannot be removed. At the far end of the room, three pillars slide down to reveal a low passageway with a pressure plate.

As you enter this low passage, you must walk across the pressure plate to open the doorway at the other end, also blocked by sliding pillars. Once you enter the secret chamber, the [Great Welkynd Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause_Items#Great_Welkynd_Stone "Skyrim:The Cause Items") will be directly in front of you, mounted in its holder. To avoid bugs, it is best to take the stone first and take out the enemies second.

[Norion the Undying](/wiki/Skyrim:Norion_the_Undying "Skyrim:Norion the Undying"), the undead sorcerer-king who guards the stone, will burst from his sarcophagus in a rage, awakening his four Wight minions to aid him in stopping you. Beware the double effects of his [staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Ehlno_Ede "Skyrim:Staff of Ehlno Ede"), which will simultaneously cause shock damage and deplete your stamina as he casts [Storm Walls](/wiki/Skyrim:Wall_of_Storms "Skyrim:Wall of Storms") across the floor.

Once you have defeated Norion, you may loot his ashen remains for his staff and the two Welkynd Stones he carries. Pick up anything you want to save before leaving, as gates within the crypt will close off the hallways forever once you exit the area.

## Notes

.jpg)

Dead Orc Adventurer

- A dead Orc Adventurer can be found in Rielle, possibly a reference to how, in *[Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Oblivion "Oblivion:Oblivion")*, an [Orc Adventurer](/wiki/Oblivion:Adventurer "Oblivion:Adventurer") could be encountered within the ruin. Their corpse is at the same spawn point in *Oblivion*.
- Rielle previously appeared in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Rielle "Online:Rielle") and *[Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Rielle "Oblivion:Rielle")*.
- The stairway and door that would lead back into Cyrodiil is present, but blocked off by a cave-in.
- Rielle is added to Skyrim as part of [The Cause](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause") Creation.
- Similar to several other dungeons such as [Wolfskull Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave#Wolfskull_Ruins "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave") within Wolfskull Cave, Rielle itself is quest-locked (inaccessible until a certain point in [The Cause quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause_(quest) "Skyrim:The Cause (quest)")), while the initial Varlais Cavern area is accessible at any time.
- The dungeon ambient track "Wind from the Depths" from the *[Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Oblivion "Oblivion:Oblivion")* soundtrack plays while in this dungeon. It is also used in the [Solitude Sewers](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Sewers "Skyrim:Solitude Sewers"), another [creation club](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") location added by [Saints & Seducers](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers").

## Bugs

- Some of the doors here may not open properly, blocking quest progress.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.323, fixes this bug.
- The pressure plates used to open gates throughout Rielle may not work, blocking quest progress.
  -  The gates can be bypassed by turning off collision using the `tcl` [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command.
- Followers can get stuck inside Rielle Crypt. You can leave them waiting outside the crypt or use console commands to extract them from the stuck position. **?**

Rift Imperial Camp

**Rift Imperial Camp** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Imperial Camps") in [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift"), located south of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") and west of the [Ruins of Bthalft](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Bthalft "Skyrim:Ruins of Bthalft").

Legate Fasendil

The camp is normally commanded by [Legate Fasendil](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Fasendil "Skyrim:Legate Fasendil"), except during the related quests, at which point [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") will assume command.

## Related Quests

- **[Compelling Tribute (Imperial)](/wiki/Skyrim:Compelling_Tribute_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Compelling Tribute (Imperial)")**: Use a [corrupt steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Anuriel "Skyrim:Anuriel") to gain intelligence on the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Rift Imperial Camp

It is a very small and compact Imperial camp, consisting of a central campfire with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") hanging over it, around which the rest of the camp is arranged. Due to the proximity of the [Ruins of Bthalft](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Bthalft "Skyrim:Ruins of Bthalft"), there are regular skirmishes between the Imperials in the camp and the bandits in the ruins. To the northeast and southeast of the camp are barricades, while to the northwest and southwest the camp is butted up against rocks rising above. South of the campfire is the Legate's tent, containing an owned single bed, with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of the bed and an end table beside it. To the right of this tent is the command tent, containing an end table and a large table covered with a map of Skyrim showing the progress of the civil war and the various forts and cities held by each side. This is where the Legate spends most of their time. To the west is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"), while to the north is the hospital tent, which contains three bed rolls occupied by two wounded soldiers and a small table holding a random [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") and a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). Outside is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") and some barrels. Behind the hospital tent are two picketed [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse"). They are owned, and taking them is considered stealing. To the east of the campfire is a row of three small tents containing unowned bed rolls. Behind these tents is the workstation for the [Imperial quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Imperial Quartermaster"). It consists of an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), and a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), with a wooden table covered in various [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron Weapons") and [steel weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Weapons "Skyrim:Steel Weapons") and [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor"). More are behind, on a barrel and some crates.

Any time [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") is controlled by the Imperials, this camp will not be present. As long as you haven't completed [Joining the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Joining the Stormcloaks"), you are free to sleep in the small tents and trade with the quartermaster.

## Notes

- Two ore veins are near the camp: a [corundum ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") vein southeast of the camp, and an [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") vein northeast of the camp.

Rift Stormcloak Camp

**Rift Stormcloak Camp** is a [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") in [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift"), located northeast of [Sarethi Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Sarethi_Farm "Skyrim:Sarethi Farm") and west of [Rift Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Watchtower "Skyrim:Rift Watchtower").

Before Stormcloak occupation

This camp will only be present if the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") hold [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") and the rest of the Rift, whether through martial might or via the negotiation during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"). [Stormcloak soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier") are camped here under the command of [Gonnar Oath-Giver](/wiki/Skyrim:Gonnar_Oath-Giver "Skyrim:Gonnar Oath-Giver"), except during the related quest, when [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") takes command. Like similar military camps that only exist when the hold has changed hands, it has no [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse").

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Gonnar Oath-Giver](/wiki/Skyrim:Gonnar_Oath-Giver "Skyrim:Gonnar Oath-Giver") (commander)  [Stormcloak Quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Stormcloak Quartermaster")  [Stormcloak Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier")  [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") (commander) [†](#intnote_Q) |

## Related Quests

- **[The Battle for Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Greenwall_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Greenwall (Stormcloaks)")**: Reclaim [this fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greenwall "Skyrim:Fort Greenwall") for the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Rift Stormcloak Camp

It is a typical Stormcloak camp, consisting of a central campfire with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") hanging over it, around which the rest of the camp is arranged. Beside the campfire is an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil") and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"). Around the area are three small tents containing unowned hay piles. South of the campfire is the hospital tent, which contains three hay piles occupied by wounded soldiers, a low table holding a random [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") and a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), and an unlocked chest containing various items to treat the sick, including potions of [cure poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Poison "Skyrim:Cure Poison"), potions of [cure disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Cure Disease"), and [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"). To the right of the hospital tent is a table with a built-in [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"). To the left of the hospital tent are some barrels. East of the campfire is the command tent, containing a lit brazier, a round table, and a large table covered with a map of Skyrim showing the progress of the civil war and the various forts and cities held by each side. This is where the commander spends most of their time. West of the campfire is the workstation for the [Stormcloak quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Stormcloak Quartermaster"), consisting of a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"). A long wooden table and a crate hold various [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron Weapons") and [steel weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Weapons "Skyrim:Steel Weapons") and [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor"). Northwest of the campfire is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"). Northeast of the campfire is the commander's tent, containing an owned bedroll, an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), and an end table.

Any time [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") is controlled by the Stormcloaks, this camp will not be present. As long as you haven't completed [Joining the Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Legion "Skyrim:Joining the Legion"), you are free to sleep in the small tents and trade with the quartermaster.

## Notes

- This wiki's current Skyrim satellite map only displays the camp's location; the previous one displayed the camp as well.

## Bugs

- The quartermaster may be missing or tagged as a normal soldier, even though he spends his time using the workstation. **?**

# Skyrim:Rift Watchtower

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Imperial Tower.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Imperial_Tower.png) | Imperial Tower: Rift Watchtower ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rift+Watchtower)) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |
| [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [Bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[Hallgerd's Tale](/wiki/Skyrim:Hallgerd%27s_Tale "Skyrim:Hallgerd's Tale")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| RiftWatchtowerExterior01, RiftWatchtowerExterior02, RiftWatchtowerExterior03, RiftWatchtowerExterior04 | |
| Region | |
| [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | |
| Location | |
| East of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") Southwest of [Clearspring Tarn](/wiki/Skyrim:Clearspring_Tarn "Skyrim:Clearspring Tarn") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Tanning Racks](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning "Skyrim:Tanning") | 1 |

Rift Watchtower

**Rift Watchtower** is a small [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Towers "Skyrim:Imperial Towers") east of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit").

The bandit chief

## Related Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

A set of wooden ramps leads up to the door to the two-story watchtower. An Orc bandit guards the entrance, with another Orc bandit inside on the ground floor. The ground floor features a pile of firewood and a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), a table holding a mead barrel, a [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat"), two [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulbs, a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), two [raw rabbit legs](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), and a copy of *[The Code of Malacath](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Code_of_Malacath "Skyrim:The Code of Malacath")*, and an open fire and a cooking spit with a charred [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") cooking over it which you can harvest for a [charred skeever hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide").

A stone spiral staircase leads to the top level, which is guarded by an Orc bandit and the Orc bandit chief. The top level features an Orc-styled shelter with two chairs and a long wooden table holding a joint of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef"), [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), an enchanted [Orcish warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Warhammer "Skyrim:Orcish Warhammer"), a copy of the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Hallgerd's Tale](/wiki/Skyrim:Hallgerd%27s_Tale "Skyrim:Hallgerd's Tale")*, and a copy of *[The True Nature of Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:The_True_Nature_of_Orcs "Skyrim:The True Nature of Orcs")*. Behind the table is an unlocked chest, and to the left is a small table holding a random [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") and [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows").

## Notes

- There is an [orichalcum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore Vein") to the southeast.

## Bugs

- The Orc bandit chief does not respawn, which makes it impossible to complete [radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant") at this location if he has been killed previously.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
  -  Open the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console"), then use the command `prid d1f56` followed by `resurrect`. This should revive the Orc and allow you to complete the quest as normal.

# Skyrim:Riften Fishery

## Overview

Riften Fishery

**Riften Fishery** is a building owned by [Bolli](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli "Skyrim:Bolli") that is located just outside the city of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), down by the docks.

## Related Quests

- **[Angler Acquaintances](/wiki/Skyrim:Angler_Acquaintances "Skyrim:Angler Acquaintances")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"): Begin your fishing journey.
- **[Catch of the Day](/wiki/Skyrim:Catch_of_the_Day "Skyrim:Catch of the Day")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"): Catch fair weather fish.
- **[In A Pinch](/wiki/Skyrim:In_A_Pinch "Skyrim:In A Pinch")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"): Obtain a juvenile mudcrab for research.
- **[Unfathomable Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfathomable_Depths "Skyrim:Unfathomable Depths")**: Uncover the [memories](/wiki/Skyrim:Lexicon "Skyrim:Lexicon") of the Dwemer.
- **[Helping Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Helping_Hand "Skyrim:Helping Hand")**: Help [Wujeeta](/wiki/Skyrim:Wujeeta "Skyrim:Wujeeta") cure her [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") addiction.

### Exterior

Fishing supplies

This is a detached building built in the middle of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften")'s docks on the eastern edge of [Lake Honrich](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Honrich "Skyrim:Lake Honrich"). There are numerous [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(creature) "Skyrim:Salmon (creature)") and all types of [ingredient](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") fish and both [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Dartwing "Skyrim:Blue Dartwing") and [orange dartwings](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing") found around the docks. There are several dock workers wandering the docks at [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") who will talk about the Riften Fishery, stating their opinions on their jobs. With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") creation, two [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies") and a [Fishing Rod](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Rod "Skyrim:Fishing Rod") can be found here. Fish from [Temperate Lakes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_(activity)#Biomes "Skyrim:Fishing (activity)") can be caught here.

### Riften Fishery

Fishery interior

Both doors are adept-locked only at nights. Most of the people who work in the Fishery live at [Haelga's Bunkhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga%27s_Bunkhouse "Skyrim:Haelga's Bunkhouse"). Inside the building, a pool of water in the middle contains a large number of salmon. Around the pool is a walkway with railings around the pool, except at the southern end where there are stairs descending into the water. There are numerous open crates around the room containing salmon. With even more hanging from the railing or from ropes strung around the room above the walkway and pool. There are at least forty-five whole [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") that can be harvested, available in this room, not including any in the [fish barrels](/wiki/Skyrim:Barrel "Skyrim:Barrel"). There are also a [river betty](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Betty "Skyrim:River Betty"), [silverside perch](/wiki/Skyrim:Silverside_Perch "Skyrim:Silverside Perch") and [cyrodilic spadetail](/wiki/Skyrim:Cyrodilic_Spadetail "Skyrim:Cyrodilic Spadetail") in an open crate along the east wall.

There are several fish barrels around the room, these can contain any of the small ingredient fish, fillets of salmon meat, [clam meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam_Meat "Skyrim:Clam Meat") and [salt piles](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"). On top of one of these in the northeastern corner is a piece of [mudcrab chitin](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab_Chitin "Skyrim:Mudcrab Chitin"). There is a narrow table against the west wall with two fillets of [salmon meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Meat "Skyrim:Salmon Meat"), a whole salmon and [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") with a whole [slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Slaughterfish") from which can be harvested [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales"), on a wooden block beside the table.

At the northern end of the room are doors into an office area with a long wooden table against the west wall holding the [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel") and a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"). Against the north wall is a copy of *[Olaf and the Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_and_the_Dragon "Skyrim:Olaf and the Dragon")* on a crate and against the northeast corner is another long wooden table with an apprentice-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"), a salmon steak, a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a bottle of alto wine, a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Things_to_Do "Skyrim:Things to Do") that appears to be written by Bolli and a copy of *[Pirate King of the Abecean](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate_King_of_the_Abecean "Skyrim:Pirate King of the Abecean")*.

## Notes

- With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") Creation, [crab meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Crab_Meat "Skyrim:Crab Meat") can also be found in the fish barrels here. This applies to the fish barrels inside the building, and the outside ones at the dock.
- Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks everything on the docks surrounding the building as owned by the Fishery, regardless whether or not they were originally marked as such.

## Bugs

- The fishery is not flagged as a public location, which can lead to trespassing crimes during the related quests.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.0, fixes this bug.

## Overview

Riften Jail

**Riften Jail** is the jail in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") found below [Mistveil Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistveil_Keep "Skyrim:Mistveil Keep").

There is an entrance at the right-hand side of the main entrance of Mistveil Keep, the Jarl's Residence.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Riften Guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Guard "Skyrim:Riften Guard") (Guard)  [Molgrom Twice-Killed](/wiki/Skyrim:Molgrom_Twice-Killed "Skyrim:Molgrom Twice-Killed") (Prisoner)  [Sibbi Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar") (Prisoner)  [Threki the Innocent](/wiki/Skyrim:Threki_the_Innocent "Skyrim:Threki the Innocent") (Prisoner)  [Brand-Shei](/wiki/Skyrim:Brand-Shei "Skyrim:Brand-Shei") (Prisoner) [†](#intnote_Brand-Shei)  [Romlyn Dreth](/wiki/Skyrim:Romlyn_Dreth "Skyrim:Romlyn Dreth") (Prisoner) [†](#intnote_Romlyn) |

[†](#note_Brand-Shei)This person only becomes a resident after completing the relevant [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Chance_Arrangement "Skyrim:A Chance Arrangement") for the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"). However, it is possible to join the Thieves Guild without framing Brand-Shei for theft. This is done by dropping Madesi's ring onto the ground instead of reverse pickpocketing it onto Brand-Shei. This will fail the objective to plant the ring on him during A Chance Arrangement, but Brynjolf will still allow you to join the Thieves Guild and Brand-Shei will remain free.

[†](#note_Romlyn)This person becomes a resident if you report him to [Indaryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Indaryn "Skyrim:Indaryn") during [Under the Table](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_the_Table "Skyrim:Under the Table") with version 1.2.4 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch").

## Related Quests

- **[The Lover's Requital](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lover%27s_Requital "Skyrim:The Lover's Requital")**: Help [Sibbi Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar") locate his former [fiancée](/wiki/Skyrim:Svidi "Skyrim:Svidi"), so he can kill her.
- **[Promises to Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Promises_to_Keep "Skyrim:Promises to Keep")**: Help [Louis Letrush](/wiki/Skyrim:Louis_Letrush "Skyrim:Louis Letrush") get [Frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost "Skyrim:Frost") from [Sibbi Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar").

### Riften Jail

Upon entering there is a corridor with a dresser in front of you, with a chair beside it. On the dresser is a copy of *[A Dance in Fire, v4](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v4 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v4")* and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). The corridor turns to the east and descends a few stairs to a door with a [Riften guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Guard "Skyrim:Riften Guard") sitting on a chair beside it. The first time you enter you will be required to pass a persuasion test in order to be granted access. There are several barrels and sacks all containing [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") along this corridor and around the jail. Beyond the door there is a small set of shelves holding only clutter on your left. There are doors to the north and south and a corridor to the east. In the middle of this area is a table and a couple of wooden benches against the walls. On the right-hand wall ahead is another set of shelves holding a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and cheese. Past this there is a walkway around the room passing two cells on each side with a view down to a lower level in the middle.

Before the first cell to the north there is a cupboard and crate containing clutter. The first cell on the north side is adept-locked and contains two single owned beds, a dresser and table. On the floor, in a wooden bowl is a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"). Just outside the cell is a barrel. The next cell is [Sibbi Black-Briar's](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar") and is nicely furnished with a large double bed in the northeast corner, a wardrobe containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") to the left against the north wall and a long [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot at the foot of the bed. There is a small wardrobe with a [red mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), a [jug](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug"), a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") and [goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet") on top and a wash basin in front of that. Against the west wall is a chair, small table and small bookcase. On the table is a bottle of alto wine and a goblet, the bookcase holds copies of *[Sovngarde: A Reexamination](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde:_A_Reexamination "Skyrim:Sovngarde: A Reexamination")*, *[Of Crossed Daggers](/wiki/Skyrim:Of_Crossed_Daggers "Skyrim:Of Crossed Daggers")*, *[Nightingales: Fact or Fiction?](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingales:_Fact_or_Fiction%3F "Skyrim:Nightingales: Fact or Fiction?")*, *[Cats of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Cats_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Cats of Skyrim")*, a bottle of wine, a bottle of alto wine and several goblets. In the northwest corner is a table holding two bottles of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead"), a [plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate") and [platter](/wiki/Skyrim:Platter "Skyrim:Platter") holding two [cooked beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooked_Beef "Skyrim:Cooked Beef") steaks, two portions of grilled leeks, a couple of loaves of bread, a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [honey nut treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat") and a jug.

The cell opposite Sibbi's is the one that you'll be sent to if you get arrested and decide to serve your time. There is a single bed in the northwest corner, a dresser against the west wall and a long wooden table against the east wall. On the table is a loaf of bread, some pieces of cheese and a lockpick. At the rear of the room is an  "Escape") Escape [Shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") (see [notes](#Notes)). The fourth cell is home to [Threki the Innocent](/wiki/Skyrim:Threki_the_Innocent "Skyrim:Threki the Innocent"), a female Nord thief. Her cell contains two single beds, one in the southwest corner, the other in southeast corner, a round wooden table and four chairs, two by the table, two against the walls. On the table is a bottle of wine and loaf of bread. To the right of this cell is a chair and wooden bench.

The door to the south leads into a room used by the guards. There is a fireplace opposite the door in the middle of the south wall, with a pile of firewood to the left and a small round wooden table and two chairs to the right. On the table is a bottle of Nord mead and a loaf of bread. Against the west wall is a dresser with a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), a [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and a [green apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") on top. To the north, against the wall is a long wooden table and chair with a bottle of alto wine and copies of *[Fall from Glory](/wiki/Skyrim:Fall_from_Glory "Skyrim:Fall from Glory")*, *[Rising Threat, Vol. I](/wiki/Skyrim:Rising_Threat,_Vol._I "Skyrim:Rising Threat, Vol. I")* and *[The Third Era Timeline](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Third_Era_Timeline "Skyrim:The Third Era Timeline")* on top of the table. There is also a door to the east that leads into a room containing the prisoner belongings and evidence chests. There are also two small cages hanging from the ceiling, a dresser against the northwest wall with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") on top and a long wooden table and bench against the north wall, with a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), three [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"), and an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe") on top, and a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") on the ground to the right of it. Under the table, on the bench is a pair of [leather bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Bracers "Skyrim:Leather Bracers"). Against the south wall is a sideboard with an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), two iron daggers, an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace") and a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") on top and a pair of [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") on the ground beside it.

Behind the door to the north is a bottle of alto wine on top of a dresser against the west wall, the corridor heads north, then turns to the east and descend a few stairs. At the next corner, where is turns to the south and descends further is a pair of sets of shelves. These hold several more common books, an iron war axe, three bottles of wine and two bottles of alto wine. The next stairs end with a long wooden table and chair against the south wall, where a guard usually sits. On the table is a copy of *[The Song of Pelinal, v4](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Song_of_Pelinal,_v4 "Skyrim:The Song of Pelinal, v4")*. The corridor turns to the east again and passes a cupboard on he left. This holds an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), a few more common books and an empty [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem").

Beyond this are another four cells, two to the north and two to the south. The first to the north is adept-locked and contains a single bed in the northeast corner, a dresser at the foot of the bed, a table against the west wall and a chair laying on its back on the ground. The second cell to the north has a barrel just outside and contains two single beds, one in the northwest and one in the northeast corners. An end table holding a bottle of Nord mead and a bottle of Wine. A set of shelves against the west wall and a square wooden table and chairs against the east wall. On this table is a portion of grilled leeks, a baked potato and an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"). Opposite is the cell [Brand-Shei](/wiki/Skyrim:Brand-Shei "Skyrim:Brand-Shei") get brought to after the Thieves Guild quest gets him arrested. It is adept-locked and contains two single beds one in the southeast and the other in the northwest corners, a round wooden table and two chairs against the east wall and a tall wardrobe against the west wall. The last cell is also adept-locked and has two single beds coming out from the south wall, an end table, a small square wooden table and two chairs in the northwest corner and a sideboard against the east wall.

## Notes

- There is an  "Escape") Escape [Shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") on the wall of the cell.
- The Sewer part can also be entered through an opening south of the Riften docks without going through the jail. It contains the [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Advances in Lockpicking‎](/wiki/Skyrim:Advances_in_Lockpicking "Skyrim:Advances in Lockpicking")* on a barrel.
  - You can enter the cell from the escape tunnel and passing through the wall. However this does not make the wall activate, so you will not be able to pass back into the tunnel.
- It is possible to enter [Sibbi Black-Briar's](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar") cell by interacting with the chair through the wall from the adjacent cell. Once inside the cell, you are unable to return as the door will not open, and the bed in the neighboring cell is owned and not usable in the same way.
  - You can exit the cell by alerting the guards (attacking Sibbi Black-Briar) and then sheathing your weapon. You need to submit to go to jail, and your stolen items will be put in the evidence chest.
- The Riften Jail key, which opens any of the empty cells, can be found just outside the evidence room (first right, then first left after entering).

## Bugs

- The trigger box that runs the secret exit from here respawns when it wasn't supposed to.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
- However, this fix won't take effect until the area resets.
- The sewer grate that leads to the prisoner belongings and evidence chests won't open due to the door having no activator text.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- The Broken Shackle button to open up the escape route is broken, making it impossible to use that escape route.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.9, fixes this bug.
  - The escape route may rarely work as intended, collapsing when the Broken Shackle is interacted with. What causes this is unknown. **?**
- A wall near the prisoner belongings chest in the sewers will bleed if struck by weapons or spells.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.10, fixes this bug.

Riften Stables

**Riften Stables** is a [stable](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables") outside the northern entrance to [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). It is owned and run by [Hofgrir Horse-Crusher](/wiki/Skyrim:Hofgrir_Horse-Crusher "Skyrim:Hofgrir Horse-Crusher") with the help of his assistant [Shadr](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadr "Skyrim:Shadr").

A dappled grey [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses") can be bought for 1000 gold.

## Related Quests

- **[Bloody Nose](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloody_Nose "Skyrim:Bloody Nose")**: Defeat [Hofgrir Horse-Crusher](/wiki/Skyrim:Hofgrir_Horse-Crusher "Skyrim:Hofgrir Horse-Crusher") in a [brawl](/wiki/Skyrim:Brawl "Skyrim:Brawl").
- **[Caught Red Handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Caught_Red_Handed "Skyrim:Caught Red Handed")**: Gather three marks of Dibella to help [Svana Far-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Svana_Far-Shield "Skyrim:Svana Far-Shield") against [Haelga](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga "Skyrim:Haelga").
- **[Horse Whisperer](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Whisperer "Skyrim:Horse Whisperer")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horses "Skyrim:Wild Horses"): Purchase a map that lets you find wild horses.
- **[Stabilized](/wiki/Skyrim:Stabilized "Skyrim:Stabilized")**: Help [Shadr](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadr "Skyrim:Shadr") clear his debt with [Sapphire](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_(person) "Skyrim:Sapphire (person)").

## Residents

| Name |
| --- |
| [Hofgrir Horse-Crusher](/wiki/Skyrim:Hofgrir_Horse-Crusher "Skyrim:Hofgrir Horse-Crusher") [Hostler](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Hostler")  [Shadr](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadr "Skyrim:Shadr")  [Sigaar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigaar "Skyrim:Sigaar") |

### Exterior

The stables are just to the right of the main gate into [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), with space for two [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse") in separate stalls. There is an empty cart and three barrels, two of which contain [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") and the third is a fish barrel that can contain raw [salmon meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Meat "Skyrim:Salmon Meat") fillets, various small [ingredient](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") fish, [clam meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam_Meat "Skyrim:Clam Meat") and [salt piles](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"). To the right of the stables, among some trees is where a [Khajiit Caravan](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders") lead by [Ahkari](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahkari "Skyrim:Ahkari") camp when they are at Riften. There is also a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") plant among the same trees and behind the stables towards the rear exit for [Honeyside](/wiki/Skyrim:Honeyside "Skyrim:Honeyside") is a [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root") plant near some rocks. There is also a [carriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Carriage "Skyrim:Carriage") in front of the stables driven by [Sigaar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigaar "Skyrim:Sigaar"), who is willing to take you to any of the main cities and towns.

| Crops | Animals |
| --- | --- |
| 1 [Gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd")  1 [Canis Root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root") | 2 [Horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse") |

### Riften Stables

Hofgrir's living quarters

Entering the stables takes you into the main living room, with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") against the opposite wall and a wall shelf above holding clutter. To the right of the cooking pot is a set of shelves holding a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), two [boiled creme treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), two [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), three loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), several pieces of cheese, a [green](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") and two [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"). There is a food barrel in the western corner. Against the northwest wall is a dresser with a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") on top and a green apple on the floor in front. In the northern corner is a small square wooden table and two chairs, with a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a loaf of bread and an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge") on the table and hanging from the ceiling above are two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, two bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and two bunches of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam").

There are a pair of double doors to the southeast that open into a bedroom consisting of two single owned beds in the northern and eastern corners, with a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") under the eastern one and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot, at the foot of the northern one. There is a wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") and a barrel with an apprentice-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") on top against the southeast wall. On the southwest wall is a wall shelf holding a bottle of wine and copies of *[Alduin is Real](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin_is_Real "Skyrim:Alduin is Real")*, *[An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:An_Explorer%27s_Guide_to_Skyrim "Skyrim:An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim")*, *[Of Fjori and Holgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Of_Fjori_and_Holgeir "Skyrim:Of Fjori and Holgeir")*, *[Cats of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Cats_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Cats of Skyrim")*, *[Watcher of Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Watcher_of_Stones "Skyrim:Watcher of Stones")*, *[A Gentleman's Guide to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Gentleman%27s_Guide_to_Whiterun "Skyrim:A Gentleman's Guide to Whiterun")*, *[Horker Attacks](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Attacks "Skyrim:Horker Attacks")* and *[A Dream of Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dream_of_Sovngarde "Skyrim:A Dream of Sovngarde")*.

## Notes

- Northeast of the stables, the ruins of a small, round tower can found nestled among the rocky ledges of a large hill. Within the fallen walls sits a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel") and a [Shrine of Zenithar](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Zenithar "Skyrim:Shrine of Zenithar") atop a stone table, next to a long-dead skeleton.
-  Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks the barrels outside the building as owned by the stables.

## Bugs

- If you buy a horse from [Katla's Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Katla%27s_Farm "Skyrim:Katla's Farm") and the horse is killed, attempting to purchase a new horse from the same stable results in 1000 gold being deducted, and [Geimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Geimund "Skyrim:Geimund") stating that your horse is "the one with the saddle", despite no saddled horse appearing at the stables there. Instead, your new horse spawns here.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
- The horses here are able to be taken for free if you befriend Hofgrir or Shadr, due to the horses being owned by the stables faction specifically. The problem is that horses cost 1,000 gold, making them way too valuable to let stablemasters let you ride them for free after completing a small favor.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=19062)) The ownership of the horses was changed to just Hofgrir, rather than the faction, preventing this issue.

# Skyrim:Riften Warehouse

## Overview
