Riften Warehouse

**Riften Warehouse** is a warehouse on Riften's docks, that is home to Riften's skooma dealer until you complete the relevant [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Raid "Skyrim:The Raid").

Located on the docks outside of Riften's walls, the warehouse is the base of operations of Riften's skooma dealer whom the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") cannot get rid of due to corrupt [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Guard "Skyrim:Riften Guard"). However, the player can take up a quest to get rid of them and discover where the skooma is coming from.

## Related Quests

- **[The Raid](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Raid "Skyrim:The Raid")**: Help the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") to uncover and stop the illegal [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") trade in town.

### Riften Warehouse

The warehouse is inaccessible before the quest: [The Raid](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Raid "Skyrim:The Raid"), as the door is locked and requires a key. Upon entering you'll be spotted and will have to deal with the skooma dealer and his bodyguard before you can explore further.

The whole warehouse appears disused and dusty with clutter scattered around the floors. There are many crates and sacks of [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") in the first room as well as a couple of barrels containing [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") and sets of shelves that have been knocked over. A doorway in the northeast corner leads to an office area with a long wooden table and chair, an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a couple of [ruined books](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book"), a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and a wooden plate containing three loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold").

In the main room, there is a bottle of Nord mead and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") on the set of shelves, with a second bottle of wine on the ground beside it. To the left of the shelves, against the south wall, a shelf holds more sacks. Next to the eastern wall is a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), while in the northeastern corner next to a couple of food barrels is a flight of stairs leading down to the cellar. The cellar is similar to the room above with crates, barrels, and sacks everywhere. A pair of locked double doors to the east require a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Sarthis%27s_Key "Skyrim:Sarthis's Key"), which can be retrieved from the body of [Sarthis Idren](/wiki/Skyrim:Sarthis_Idren "Skyrim:Sarthis Idren").

Behind the doors is a small room that seems to be the base of operations for Sarthis, the skooma dealer. A set of shelves opposite the doors against the east wall holds five bowls of [moon sugar](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Sugar "Skyrim:Moon Sugar") and six bottles of [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma"). At the north end of the room is a long wooden table and chair, a bottle of wine, another bowl of moon sugar, two more bottles of skooma and a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel") containing a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Shipment%27s_Ready "Skyrim:Shipment's Ready") needed for the relevant [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Raid "Skyrim:The Raid"). Another set of shelves lean back against the wall, holding two pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") and, on top of the unit, a [mammoth tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Mammoth Tusk"). Around the cellar are bottles of both Nord mead and [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine").

## Notes

- It is possible to interact with Sarthis's satchel *through* the stone wall in the basement.
- All the moon sugar and skooma respawn.
- Anything you take from here other than what is on the corpses of the 2 thugs will count as theft.
- According to [Wujeeta](/wiki/Skyrim:Wujeeta "Skyrim:Wujeeta"), the warehouse has been tightly locked up ever since the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") began.

## Bugs

- Although the key to the warehouse is given to you legitimately, entering it still counts as trespassing.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.

Riften

**Riften** is a major city in the southeast of Skyrim near the borders of [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind") and [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil"), and the capital of [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift"). It is home to the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), who inhabit the sewers beneath Riften known as the [Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway"), as well as [Honorhall Orphanage](/wiki/Skyrim:Honorhall_Orphanage "Skyrim:Honorhall Orphanage"). Riften is also the seat of a powerful noble family, the Black-Briars. [Maven](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar"), the head of the family, owns the [Black-Briar Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Meadery "Skyrim:Black-Briar Meadery") and has ties to the Thieves Guild and the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"). [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Laila Law-Giver](/wiki/Skyrim:Laila_Law-Giver "Skyrim:Laila Law-Giver") is the initial ruler of the Rift; if the Imperials take over the hold, Maven replaces Laila as jarl. Maven is widely feared, as [Maul](/wiki/Skyrim:Maul "Skyrim:Maul") notes: *"If she tells you to do something, you damn well better do exactly what she says."*

The market at Riften Grand Plaza is made up of stalls run by a few of Riften's citizens: [Madesi](/wiki/Skyrim:Madesi "Skyrim:Madesi"), an Argonian jeweler whom you can [assist](/wiki/Skyrim:Ringmaker "Skyrim:Ringmaker") in finding materials for his jewelry; [Grelka](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelka "Skyrim:Grelka"), a cranky armor merchant who offers expert [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") training; [Brand-Shei](/wiki/Skyrim:Brand-Shei "Skyrim:Brand-Shei"), an Argonian-raised [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") who sells a little bit of everything, and [Marise Aravel](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel "Skyrim:Marise Aravel"), who sells fresh meat and produce. [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf"), a merchant of ill repute, can also be found here. Down on the lower decks near the canal is [Elgrim's Elixirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim%27s_Elixirs "Skyrim:Elgrim's Elixirs"), run by [Elgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim "Skyrim:Elgrim") and his wife [Hafjorg](/wiki/Skyrim:Hafjorg "Skyrim:Hafjorg"). The forge is operated by [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund"), who seems quite proud of his work, along with his apprentice [Asbjorn Fire-Tamer](/wiki/Skyrim:Asbjorn_Fire-Tamer "Skyrim:Asbjorn Fire-Tamer"). The [Pawned Prawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Pawned_Prawn "Skyrim:Pawned Prawn") is run by [Bersi Honey-Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Bersi_Honey-Hand "Skyrim:Bersi Honey-Hand") and his wife, [Drifa](/wiki/Skyrim:Drifa "Skyrim:Drifa"). Finally, there's the Black-Briar Meadery and the town inn, [The Bee and Barb](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bee_and_Barb "Skyrim:The Bee and Barb"), operated by [Keerava](/wiki/Skyrim:Keerava "Skyrim:Keerava") and [Talen-Jei](/wiki/Skyrim:Talen-Jei "Skyrim:Talen-Jei").

When you approach Riften for the first time, the [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Guard "Skyrim:Riften Guard") will tell you to head to the northern gate, where you need to pay a tax to enter the city. You can either pay the tax (the amount depends on your level) or try to convince the guards to open the door for free. Another option is to commit a crime and be arrested, causing you to be taken to the city's [jail](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Jail "Skyrim:Riften Jail") inside the walls. Alternatively, you can enter the city through the Black-Briar Meadery's back door near the western gate, or through the sewer grate next to the docks that leads into the jail. Finally, with enough [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") skill, you can steal the key off the guard demanding the tax.

For more information on Riften, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Riften "Lore:Riften").

## Riften People

\* Only appear after various related quests
\*\* Only becomes a merchant if [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund") is killed

### Quests Starting Here

Most of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") quests start here. For details, see its page.

#### Side Quests

- **[Promises to Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Promises_to_Keep "Skyrim:Promises to Keep")**: Help [Louis Letrush](/wiki/Skyrim:Louis_Letrush "Skyrim:Louis Letrush") get [Frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost "Skyrim:Frost") from [Sibbi Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar").
- **[The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love")**: Help the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") spread the cause of love throughout Skyrim.
- **[Unfathomable Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfathomable_Depths "Skyrim:Unfathomable Depths")**: Uncover the [memories](/wiki/Skyrim:Lexicon "Skyrim:Lexicon") of the Dwemer.

#### Creation Club

- **[A Soul Divided](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Soul_Divided "Skyrim:A Soul Divided")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnfang_%26_Duskfang "Skyrim:Dawnfang & Duskfang"): Seek out a cursed Tsaesci blade in the Ratway.
- **[Blue in the Face](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_in_the_Face "Skyrim:Blue in the Face")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblins "Skyrim:Goblins"): Investigate rumors of the Blue God's return.
- **[Gambler's Edge](/wiki/Skyrim:Gambler%27s_Edge "Skyrim:Gambler's Edge")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Orcish_Scaled "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Orcish Scaled"): Search for an ill-fated gambler at the pit fights in [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern").
- **[Shadowfoot Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum_(quest) "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum"): Purchase a cozy sewer home ideal for a thief.
- **[The Gray Cowl of Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_of_Nocturnal "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl of Nocturnal")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_Returns! "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl Returns!"): Investigate the legend of the Gray Fox.

## Notes

- [Honeyside](/wiki/Skyrim:Honeyside "Skyrim:Honeyside") is a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase after completion of certain quests for the jarl. It may be purchased from the steward for 5,000 to 8,000 gold.
- With the [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") [add-on](/wiki/Skyrim:Add-ons "Skyrim:Add-ons") installed, a [clay deposit](/wiki/Skyrim:Clay "Skyrim:Clay") can be found along the shoreline just outside the city, southwest of the southern gate.
- With the [Shadowfoot Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, [Riften Docks](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Docks "Skyrim:Riften Docks") will get a map marker for ease of access to the sanctum.
- If the Rift is transferred to Imperial control during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"), you may find Imperial soldiers fighting with one or more Riften guards.
- Entering the city via the Meadery during the day for the first time and using the forge next to the market before Brynjolf approaches will cause him to ask his opening question a few times while you are in the smithing animation and then walk away, after which he will not approach you again. This can be used to prevent [A Chance Arrangement](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Chance_Arrangement "Skyrim:A Chance Arrangement") from being added to your journal.
- After completing [A Chance Arrangement](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Chance_Arrangement "Skyrim:A Chance Arrangement"), there is a 20% chance of [encountering](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions "Skyrim:World Interactions") a [thief](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Thief (Thieves Guild)") inside one of the stores or houses.
- According to the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")*, the unusable city gate in Riften's southeast corner is called the Dead Gate, so named due to the many people who died there during repeated bandit raids on the city.
- Riften also appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Riften "Arena:Riften")* and [ESO](/wiki/Online:Riften "Online:Riften").

## Bugs

- Attempting to persuade the guard to enter Riften always succeeds.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.0, fixes this bug.
- If the Empire takes Riften, you will routinely see the new Imperial guards fighting with Stormcloak guards who weren't disabled properly, similar to [Sarethi Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Sarethi_Farm "Skyrim:Sarethi Farm"). You will receive a bounty if you try to intervene. **?**
- If playing with a controller, after some time you may feel a large shake on it on entering Riften. Clearing [Lost Tongue Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Tongue_Overlook "Skyrim:Lost Tongue Overlook") and killing the dragon will stop the shaking. **?**

Riften

**Riften** is a major city in the southeast of Skyrim near the borders of [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind") and [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil"), and the capital of [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift"). It is home to the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), who inhabit the sewers beneath Riften known as the [Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway"), as well as [Honorhall Orphanage](/wiki/Skyrim:Honorhall_Orphanage "Skyrim:Honorhall Orphanage"). Riften is also the seat of a powerful noble family, the Black-Briars. [Maven](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar"), the head of the family, owns the [Black-Briar Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Meadery "Skyrim:Black-Briar Meadery") and has ties to the Thieves Guild and the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"). [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Laila Law-Giver](/wiki/Skyrim:Laila_Law-Giver "Skyrim:Laila Law-Giver") is the initial ruler of the Rift; if the Imperials take over the hold, Maven replaces Laila as jarl. Maven is widely feared, as [Maul](/wiki/Skyrim:Maul "Skyrim:Maul") notes: *"If she tells you to do something, you damn well better do exactly what she says."*

The market at Riften Grand Plaza is made up of stalls run by a few of Riften's citizens: [Madesi](/wiki/Skyrim:Madesi "Skyrim:Madesi"), an Argonian jeweler whom you can [assist](/wiki/Skyrim:Ringmaker "Skyrim:Ringmaker") in finding materials for his jewelry; [Grelka](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelka "Skyrim:Grelka"), a cranky armor merchant who offers expert [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") training; [Brand-Shei](/wiki/Skyrim:Brand-Shei "Skyrim:Brand-Shei"), an Argonian-raised [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") who sells a little bit of everything, and [Marise Aravel](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel "Skyrim:Marise Aravel"), who sells fresh meat and produce. [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf"), a merchant of ill repute, can also be found here. Down on the lower decks near the canal is [Elgrim's Elixirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim%27s_Elixirs "Skyrim:Elgrim's Elixirs"), run by [Elgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim "Skyrim:Elgrim") and his wife [Hafjorg](/wiki/Skyrim:Hafjorg "Skyrim:Hafjorg"). The forge is operated by [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund"), who seems quite proud of his work, along with his apprentice [Asbjorn Fire-Tamer](/wiki/Skyrim:Asbjorn_Fire-Tamer "Skyrim:Asbjorn Fire-Tamer"). The [Pawned Prawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Pawned_Prawn "Skyrim:Pawned Prawn") is run by [Bersi Honey-Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Bersi_Honey-Hand "Skyrim:Bersi Honey-Hand") and his wife, [Drifa](/wiki/Skyrim:Drifa "Skyrim:Drifa"). Finally, there's the Black-Briar Meadery and the town inn, [The Bee and Barb](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bee_and_Barb "Skyrim:The Bee and Barb"), operated by [Keerava](/wiki/Skyrim:Keerava "Skyrim:Keerava") and [Talen-Jei](/wiki/Skyrim:Talen-Jei "Skyrim:Talen-Jei").

When you approach Riften for the first time, the [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Guard "Skyrim:Riften Guard") will tell you to head to the northern gate, where you need to pay a tax to enter the city. You can either pay the tax (the amount depends on your level) or try to convince the guards to open the door for free. Another option is to commit a crime and be arrested, causing you to be taken to the city's [jail](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Jail "Skyrim:Riften Jail") inside the walls. Alternatively, you can enter the city through the Black-Briar Meadery's back door near the western gate, or through the sewer grate next to the docks that leads into the jail. Finally, with enough [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") skill, you can steal the key off the guard demanding the tax.

For more information on Riften, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Riften "Lore:Riften").

### Quests Starting Here

Most of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") quests start here. For details, see its page.

#### Side Quests

- **[Promises to Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Promises_to_Keep "Skyrim:Promises to Keep")**: Help [Louis Letrush](/wiki/Skyrim:Louis_Letrush "Skyrim:Louis Letrush") get [Frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost "Skyrim:Frost") from [Sibbi Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar").
- **[The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love")**: Help the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") spread the cause of love throughout Skyrim.
- **[Unfathomable Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfathomable_Depths "Skyrim:Unfathomable Depths")**: Uncover the [memories](/wiki/Skyrim:Lexicon "Skyrim:Lexicon") of the Dwemer.

#### Creation Club

- **[A Soul Divided](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Soul_Divided "Skyrim:A Soul Divided")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnfang_%26_Duskfang "Skyrim:Dawnfang & Duskfang"): Seek out a cursed Tsaesci blade in the Ratway.
- **[Blue in the Face](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_in_the_Face "Skyrim:Blue in the Face")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblins "Skyrim:Goblins"): Investigate rumors of the Blue God's return.
- **[Gambler's Edge](/wiki/Skyrim:Gambler%27s_Edge "Skyrim:Gambler's Edge")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Orcish_Scaled "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Orcish Scaled"): Search for an ill-fated gambler at the pit fights in [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern").
- **[Shadowfoot Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum_(quest) "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum"): Purchase a cozy sewer home ideal for a thief.
- **[The Gray Cowl of Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_of_Nocturnal "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl of Nocturnal")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_Returns! "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl Returns!"): Investigate the legend of the Gray Fox.

## Notes

- [Honeyside](/wiki/Skyrim:Honeyside "Skyrim:Honeyside") is a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase after completion of certain quests for the jarl. It may be purchased from the steward for 5,000 to 8,000 gold.
- With the [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") [add-on](/wiki/Skyrim:Add-ons "Skyrim:Add-ons") installed, a [clay deposit](/wiki/Skyrim:Clay "Skyrim:Clay") can be found along the shoreline just outside the city, southwest of the southern gate.
- With the [Shadowfoot Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, [Riften Docks](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Docks "Skyrim:Riften Docks") will get a map marker for ease of access to the sanctum.
- If the Rift is transferred to Imperial control during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"), you may find Imperial soldiers fighting with one or more Riften guards.
- Entering the city via the Meadery during the day for the first time and using the forge next to the market before Brynjolf approaches will cause him to ask his opening question a few times while you are in the smithing animation and then walk away, after which he will not approach you again. This can be used to prevent [A Chance Arrangement](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Chance_Arrangement "Skyrim:A Chance Arrangement") from being added to your journal.
- After completing [A Chance Arrangement](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Chance_Arrangement "Skyrim:A Chance Arrangement"), there is a 20% chance of [encountering](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions "Skyrim:World Interactions") a [thief](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Thief (Thieves Guild)") inside one of the stores or houses.
- According to the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")*, the unusable city gate in Riften's southeast corner is called the Dead Gate, so named due to the many people who died there during repeated bandit raids on the city.
- Riften also appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Riften "Arena:Riften")* and [ESO](/wiki/Online:Riften "Online:Riften").

## Bugs

- Attempting to persuade the guard to enter Riften always succeeds.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.0, fixes this bug.
- If the Empire takes Riften, you will routinely see the new Imperial guards fighting with Stormcloak guards who weren't disabled properly, similar to [Sarethi Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Sarethi_Farm "Skyrim:Sarethi Farm"). You will receive a bounty if you try to intervene. **?**
- If playing with a controller, after some time you may feel a large shake on it on entering Riften. Clearing [Lost Tongue Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Tongue_Overlook "Skyrim:Lost Tongue Overlook") and killing the dragon will stop the shaking. **?**

Riften

**Riften** is a major city in the southeast of Skyrim near the borders of [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind") and [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil"), and the capital of [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift"). It is home to the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), who inhabit the sewers beneath Riften known as the [Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway"), as well as [Honorhall Orphanage](/wiki/Skyrim:Honorhall_Orphanage "Skyrim:Honorhall Orphanage"). Riften is also the seat of a powerful noble family, the Black-Briars. [Maven](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar"), the head of the family, owns the [Black-Briar Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Meadery "Skyrim:Black-Briar Meadery") and has ties to the Thieves Guild and the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"). [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Laila Law-Giver](/wiki/Skyrim:Laila_Law-Giver "Skyrim:Laila Law-Giver") is the initial ruler of the Rift; if the Imperials take over the hold, Maven replaces Laila as jarl. Maven is widely feared, as [Maul](/wiki/Skyrim:Maul "Skyrim:Maul") notes: *"If she tells you to do something, you damn well better do exactly what she says."*

The market at Riften Grand Plaza is made up of stalls run by a few of Riften's citizens: [Madesi](/wiki/Skyrim:Madesi "Skyrim:Madesi"), an Argonian jeweler whom you can [assist](/wiki/Skyrim:Ringmaker "Skyrim:Ringmaker") in finding materials for his jewelry; [Grelka](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelka "Skyrim:Grelka"), a cranky armor merchant who offers expert [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") training; [Brand-Shei](/wiki/Skyrim:Brand-Shei "Skyrim:Brand-Shei"), an Argonian-raised [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") who sells a little bit of everything, and [Marise Aravel](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel "Skyrim:Marise Aravel"), who sells fresh meat and produce. [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf"), a merchant of ill repute, can also be found here. Down on the lower decks near the canal is [Elgrim's Elixirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim%27s_Elixirs "Skyrim:Elgrim's Elixirs"), run by [Elgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim "Skyrim:Elgrim") and his wife [Hafjorg](/wiki/Skyrim:Hafjorg "Skyrim:Hafjorg"). The forge is operated by [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund"), who seems quite proud of his work, along with his apprentice [Asbjorn Fire-Tamer](/wiki/Skyrim:Asbjorn_Fire-Tamer "Skyrim:Asbjorn Fire-Tamer"). The [Pawned Prawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Pawned_Prawn "Skyrim:Pawned Prawn") is run by [Bersi Honey-Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Bersi_Honey-Hand "Skyrim:Bersi Honey-Hand") and his wife, [Drifa](/wiki/Skyrim:Drifa "Skyrim:Drifa"). Finally, there's the Black-Briar Meadery and the town inn, [The Bee and Barb](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bee_and_Barb "Skyrim:The Bee and Barb"), operated by [Keerava](/wiki/Skyrim:Keerava "Skyrim:Keerava") and [Talen-Jei](/wiki/Skyrim:Talen-Jei "Skyrim:Talen-Jei").

When you approach Riften for the first time, the [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Guard "Skyrim:Riften Guard") will tell you to head to the northern gate, where you need to pay a tax to enter the city. You can either pay the tax (the amount depends on your level) or try to convince the guards to open the door for free. Another option is to commit a crime and be arrested, causing you to be taken to the city's [jail](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Jail "Skyrim:Riften Jail") inside the walls. Alternatively, you can enter the city through the Black-Briar Meadery's back door near the western gate, or through the sewer grate next to the docks that leads into the jail. Finally, with enough [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") skill, you can steal the key off the guard demanding the tax.

For more information on Riften, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Riften "Lore:Riften").

\* Only appear after various related quests

### Quests Starting Here

Most of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") quests start here. For details, see its page.

#### Side Quests

- **[Promises to Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Promises_to_Keep "Skyrim:Promises to Keep")**: Help [Louis Letrush](/wiki/Skyrim:Louis_Letrush "Skyrim:Louis Letrush") get [Frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost "Skyrim:Frost") from [Sibbi Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar").
- **[The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love")**: Help the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") spread the cause of love throughout Skyrim.
- **[Unfathomable Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfathomable_Depths "Skyrim:Unfathomable Depths")**: Uncover the [memories](/wiki/Skyrim:Lexicon "Skyrim:Lexicon") of the Dwemer.

#### Creation Club

- **[A Soul Divided](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Soul_Divided "Skyrim:A Soul Divided")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnfang_%26_Duskfang "Skyrim:Dawnfang & Duskfang"): Seek out a cursed Tsaesci blade in the Ratway.
- **[Blue in the Face](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_in_the_Face "Skyrim:Blue in the Face")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblins "Skyrim:Goblins"): Investigate rumors of the Blue God's return.
- **[Gambler's Edge](/wiki/Skyrim:Gambler%27s_Edge "Skyrim:Gambler's Edge")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Orcish_Scaled "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Orcish Scaled"): Search for an ill-fated gambler at the pit fights in [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern").
- **[Shadowfoot Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum_(quest) "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum"): Purchase a cozy sewer home ideal for a thief.
- **[The Gray Cowl of Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_of_Nocturnal "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl of Nocturnal")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_Returns! "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl Returns!"): Investigate the legend of the Gray Fox.

## Notes

- [Honeyside](/wiki/Skyrim:Honeyside "Skyrim:Honeyside") is a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase after completion of certain quests for the jarl. It may be purchased from the steward for 5,000 to 8,000 gold.
- With the [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") [add-on](/wiki/Skyrim:Add-ons "Skyrim:Add-ons") installed, a [clay deposit](/wiki/Skyrim:Clay "Skyrim:Clay") can be found along the shoreline just outside the city, southwest of the southern gate.
- With the [Shadowfoot Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, [Riften Docks](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Docks "Skyrim:Riften Docks") will get a map marker for ease of access to the sanctum.
- If the Rift is transferred to Imperial control during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"), you may find Imperial soldiers fighting with one or more Riften guards.
- Entering the city via the Meadery during the day for the first time and using the forge next to the market before Brynjolf approaches will cause him to ask his opening question a few times while you are in the smithing animation and then walk away, after which he will not approach you again. This can be used to prevent [A Chance Arrangement](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Chance_Arrangement "Skyrim:A Chance Arrangement") from being added to your journal.
- After completing [A Chance Arrangement](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Chance_Arrangement "Skyrim:A Chance Arrangement"), there is a 20% chance of [encountering](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions "Skyrim:World Interactions") a [thief](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Thief (Thieves Guild)") inside one of the stores or houses.
- According to the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")*, the unusable city gate in Riften's southeast corner is called the Dead Gate, so named due to the many people who died there during repeated bandit raids on the city.
- Riften also appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Riften "Arena:Riften")* and [ESO](/wiki/Online:Riften "Online:Riften").

## Bugs

- Attempting to persuade the guard to enter Riften always succeeds.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.0, fixes this bug.
- If the Empire takes Riften, you will routinely see the new Imperial guards fighting with Stormcloak guards who weren't disabled properly, similar to [Sarethi Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Sarethi_Farm "Skyrim:Sarethi Farm"). You will receive a bounty if you try to intervene. **?**
- If playing with a controller, after some time you may feel a large shake on it on entering Riften. Clearing [Lost Tongue Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Tongue_Overlook "Skyrim:Lost Tongue Overlook") and killing the dragon will stop the shaking. **?**

Riftweald Manor

**Riftweald Manor** is a house in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") owned by [Mercer Frey](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey").

You must infiltrate this house when completing the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") quest [The Pursuit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pursuit "Skyrim:The Pursuit").

## Related Quests

- **[The Litany of Larceny](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Litany_of_Larceny "Skyrim:The Litany of Larceny")**: Find items for [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") throughout the [questline](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Primary_Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").
- **[The Pursuit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pursuit "Skyrim:The Pursuit")**: Break into [Mercer Frey](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey")'s house and search for clues.

## Walkthrough

Riftweald Manor is a relatively well-secured property that was given as a gift to [Mercer Frey](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey") after the Black-Briars confiscated it from its previous owners. It is immediately next to the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") and the [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Riften) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Riften)"), and conveniently near the Thieves Guild secret entrance.

Mercer commissioned the design and installation of a unique ramp system at the rear of the house, probably designed for quick escapes. The ramp provides you with a singular point of entry, as it can be lowered externally by firing an arrow, ranged magic, or the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") at the operating mechanism under the balcony. The ramp leads to an expert-locked door which can be opened with the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer%27s_House_Key "Skyrim:Mercer's House Key") found on [Vald](/wiki/Skyrim:Vald "Skyrim:Vald"), an easily dispatched guard hired by Mercer to protect the property. Vald can be dealt with in a number of ways; see the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pursuit "Skyrim:The Pursuit") for details.

When you enter the manor via the ramp, you will be on the second floor of the home. The first room is full of crates, barrels, and sacks, most with items of clutter on them. There is a wall shelf holding a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and a few goblets, and two of the barrels contain random meat. In the northwestern corner are double wooden doors. Through these doors you are likely to face at least one of the three leveled [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") employed to guard the house. The room has a locked barred pair of doors blocking access to a balcony, and contains an empty table and chair, an empty set of shelves, a wooden bench with a small table beside it holding a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and a pair of chairs with another small table between them. There are two doorways off of this room, and a flight of stairs leading down.

Mercer's bedroom

The first doorway is to the right of the barred doors, and leads into a small storeroom containing a tall wardrobe of random [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), a long end table, several rolled up rugs, and some disused furniture. The second doorway leads into the master bedroom, which contains an owned double bed in the southeastern corner. There is an unlocked long [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of the bed, a wall shelf holding a bottle each of alto wine, wine, and [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), two tall wardrobes containing a selection of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"), and three sets of shelves holding a copy of *[The Amulet of Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Amulet_of_Kings "Skyrim:The Amulet of Kings")*, a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of wine, two bottles of Nord mead, a selection of fine crockery, a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), and three loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). There are also two chairs pulled up in front of a lit fireplace.

Dining room

Down the stairs is another large room with a locked barred pair of doors preventing access from the street. To the right of the barred doors, opposite the bottom of the stairs, is a set of shelves holding a [Dibella statue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dibella_Statue "Skyrim:Dibella Statue") and three bottles of [Black-Briar Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead"). A [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel is in the corner to the right. Under the stairs you've just descended are several crates and two food sacks. Beside these is a cupboard with a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") on the shelf. There is a wooden bench to the left of a pair of closed unlocked double doors, and opposite is a long end table holding a copy of *[Nords Arise!](/wiki/Skyrim:Nords_Arise! "Skyrim:Nords Arise!")* and flanked by two chairs. To the left of the end table is a disused [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"). Farther to the east, a table with four chairs arranged around it has been laid with four [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a bottle of alto wine, and an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"). Against the wall behind the table is a set of shelves holding more fine crockery, a bottle of alto wine, and a bottle of Nord mead. Behind this wall is a flight of stairs leading down into the cellar. By the top of the stairs is a set of shelves holding a [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") of [minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a potion of [minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), two [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), a sweet roll, four [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), three loaves of bread, and five wheels of cheese.

Descending the stairs to the cellar leads to a single room without any other exits. Under the stairs is a bale of straw, a cupboard holding a bottle of wine, and a food barrel. An L-shaped counter with two shelves underneath runs almost the entire length of the room, and holds a [boiled creme treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), a sweet roll, an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), a kettle containing two cabbages, three loaves of bread, two bulbs of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), several pieces of cheese, a cast iron pot containing five potatoes, a loose cabbage, a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), another cast iron pot containing two [raw rabbit legs](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), and a bottle of Nord mead. There is yet another cast iron pot on the floor in front of the counter containing a bottle of Nord mead. To the right of the counter is a pile of firewood, with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") lying beside it. Hanging from the ceiling are three bunches of [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam"), two bunches of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear"), and two [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braids "Skyrim:Garlic Braids"), with a third braid hanging from the corner of a wall shelf.

Returning upstairs to the previous room, the unlocked double doors lead into a room with a long wooden table holding a [ruined book](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a bottle of wine, a food sack, a loaf of bread, a cheese wheel, and a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:To_The_Owner "Skyrim:To The Owner") from the engineer, identified as Kiltinius Dandoril, who completed the balcony ramp and floor mechanism. Against the walls are a stack of crates with two food sacks on top, a set of shelves holding a medium coin purse and two bottles of wine, a food barrel, and a tall wardrobe containing fine clothes and boots. Another locked barred pair of doors is to the east. To the left of the barred doors is a suspicious cabinet, which contains a pair of fine boots and a false back panel. This panel may also be activated by a pull chain on the pillar to your left as you face the cabinet, or by a pull bar behind the panel on the right.

Beyond the panel is a food barrel at the top of a flight of stairs leading down into another part of the cellar. This part of the cellar is very dirty, with cobwebs everywhere. At the bottom of the stairs is a room with some crates, sacks, and unusable barrels. There is also a long wooden table holding a random potion. A hole in the west wall leads into the sewer network. As you enter the passage, there are metal bars in front of you, with a wooden chest behind the bars. In front of the bars is a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that triggers a [spear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") from the floor behind the bars. The passage continues to the left and enters a room where most of the floor is rigged with [flame spout traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Spout_Trap "Skyrim:Flame Spout Trap"). There is a safe path; however, if you decide to run straight through, the damage is quite minor if you are prepared properly. The safe route is to start at the far southern end, then move three squares west, turn north and walk to the end, turn west and walk to the end, and turn south and walk to the end, where the passage continues.

Treasure-filled room

The next passage has another pressure plate that triggers a [poison dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") to fire from the ceiling. Continuing along the passage, on your right is a short passage that brings you to the unlocked wooden chest seen through the bars. The passage turns to the left after a short distance; as you proceed, [swinging blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades") and a [battering ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram") will start to swing across the passage ahead. Level with the ram are alcoves on both sides of the passage containing various crates, sacks, and barrels. Once past the blades, you come to a flight of stairs leading down to the south. At the bottom of the stairs are bars on your left, and an expert-trapped door ahead. If tripped, the trap will fire a massive amount of poisoned darts rapidly from the ceiling; jumping back is the easiest way to avoid the darts. Through the door is a room that contains a wooden table and chair with *[Mercer's Plans](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer%27s_Plans "Skyrim:Mercer's Plans")*, the [Bust of the Gray Fox](/wiki/Skyrim:Bust_of_the_Gray_Fox "Skyrim:Bust of the Gray Fox") (which you can sell to [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") as part of the Thieves Guild quest [The Litany of Larceny](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Litany_of_Larceny "Skyrim:The Litany of Larceny")), a bowl containing various gems, a [gold necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Necklace "Skyrim:Gold Necklace"), and a [gold ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ring "Skyrim:Gold Ring"), a copy of the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Red Kitchen Reader](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Red_Kitchen_Reader "Skyrim:The Red Kitchen Reader")*, a copy of *[The Lusty Argonian Maid, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lusty_Argonian_Maid,_v1 "Skyrim:The Lusty Argonian Maid, v1")*, four loose septims, and a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Many_Thanks "Skyrim:Many Thanks") from R to M (presumably M for Mercer) discussing a successful theft. To the right of the table is a [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") and an expert-locked display case containing [Chillrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Chillrend "Skyrim:Chillrend"), a unique weapon. To the left of the table is an unlocked Dwemer chest and a set of shelves holding nine common books, a gourd, and a food sack.

An alternative passage leads out of this room on the other side of the bars seen before the door. The passage leads to the top of a flight of stairs, with a door at the bottom that leads into the [Ratway Vaults](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway_Vaults "Skyrim:The Ratway Vaults"). Beyond the door is a hole in the floor where you can drop down; inscribed on the edge of the hole is a  "Danger") Danger [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"). Dropping down the hole will deposit you in an alcove on the top level of the three-leveled room within the vaults. Following the path to the right leads back to the [Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon").

## Notes

- The house will remain open to access after completing the quest. The bandits will respawn, along with the food, coin purses, and potions within.
- There is a  "Danger") Danger shadowmark by the cellar entrance to the Ratway Vaults, and a  "Guild") Guild shadowmark by the front and back doors.
- Three leveled generic bandits guard the inside of the manor. However, three unused unique NPCs may have once been intended for this task. Three Nord bandits named [Hrolmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Unused_NPCs#Hrolmir "Skyrim:Unused NPCs"), [Reves](/wiki/Skyrim:Unused_NPCs#Reves "Skyrim:Unused NPCs"), and [Skeggr](/wiki/Skyrim:Unused_NPCs#Skeggr "Skyrim:Unused NPCs") exist in the game files, but they are very unfinished. All of their editor IDs are prefixed with `TG07`, the editor ID of the quest The Pursuit.

## Bugs

- It is possible to access the building without joining the Thieves Guild. To do so, jump up onto the brazier outside the Temple of Mara closest to the house, then hop up onto the temple's roof. Scale the roof until you can jump down onto the locked gate, then balance yourself over the gate and leap onto the manor's roof; alternatively, you can reach the manor's roof from the temple's roof by using [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint"). From there, scale the roof, hop down onto the tiny balcony, and pick the lock on the door. All items will be present inside the house if it is entered in this way, with the notable exceptions of *Mercer's Plans* and the Bust of the Gray Fox.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, addresses this issue. It is now impossible to access the building before The Pursuit without console commands. A barrel that allowed early access has also been removed.
- One of the gates in the back alley behind the building is Expert-locked, while the other two require Mercer's House Key. This allows the area behind the manor to be accessed prior to The Pursuit by picking the expert level lock, which is likely unintentional.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, addresses this issue. The lock level setting on the aforementioned gate has been changed, and the key is now required for all 3 gates.
- If you enter the building before starting The Pursuit, *Mercer's Plans* may already be present in the treasure room.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, addresses this issue. The note will now be disabled until then. The fix from USKP 1.0 that blocked roof access prior to the quest has also been undone.

# Skyrim:Rimerock Burrow

## Overview

Rimerock Burrow

**Rimerock Burrow** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing an [atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach") and the powerful conjurer [Sebastian Lort](/wiki/Skyrim:Sebastian_Lort "Skyrim:Sebastian Lort"). It contains only one zone, *[Rimerock Burrow](#Rimerock_Burrow)*.

## Related Quests

- **[A Daedra's Best Friend](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Daedra%27s_Best_Friend "Skyrim:A Daedra's Best Friend")**: Help [Barbas](/wiki/Skyrim:Barbas "Skyrim:Barbas") reunite with his [master](/wiki/Lore:Clavicus_Vile "Lore:Clavicus Vile").

### Exterior

The rough path leading to the cave takes you over a wooden bridge spanning a crevice in the cliff wall just before the entrance. The path branches off the larger road east of [Pinefrost Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinefrost_Tower "Skyrim:Pinefrost Tower"), with the fork marked by a pile of rocks; the fork can nevertheless be easily missed, as there is likely to be an encounter as you near the junction. It is advisable to have a light source before entering the cave.

### Rimerock Burrow

Rimerock Burrow interior

Upon entering, there is a dark tunnel leading down to the main cavern on the lowest level. There are raised areas in front and to your right. A leveled atronach patrols from the raised area to your right down to the lower level. This area contains nothing of interest. Sebastian will be found on the raised area in front of you, normally working at the arcane enchanter. To get to Sebastian, you will have to climb a ramp on the far left of the cave against the wall. There is a large stone table on your left with an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") near it. On the table is a [scroll of conjure familiar](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Familiar "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Familiar"), a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), a goblet, and a bowl containing a sample of [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") and a [pine thrush egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"). If sent here by [Clavicus Vile](/wiki/Skyrim:Clavicus_Vile "Skyrim:Clavicus Vile"), the [Rueful Axe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rueful_Axe "Skyrim:The Rueful Axe") will also be lying on the table. If you are here prior to accepting the related quest, the Rueful Axe will be replaced with an ordinary [steel battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Steel Battleaxe").

Between the table and arcane enchanter is a tunnel heading south then west leading to a storage and bedroom area. On your right before reaching the end of the tunnel is Sebastian's bedroom containing a single unowned bed and an end table next to it. On the table is a copy of the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Hearth Fire, v9](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Hearth_Fire,_v9 "Skyrim:2920, Hearth Fire, v9")*, an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). Next to the end table are two barrels, one of which contains ingredients; a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and some [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear") are hanging over them.

Just after the bedroom area is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing leveled loot and any items you are sent here to recover. At the end of the tunnel there are two sets of shelves. The shelves hold copies of *[The Firmament](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Firmament "Skyrim:The Firmament")*, *[Darkest Darkness](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkest_Darkness "Skyrim:Darkest Darkness")*, *[The Wolf Queen, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen,_v2 "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen, v2")* and *[v5](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen,_v5 "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen, v5")*, *[The Real Barenziah, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Real_Barenziah,_v2 "Skyrim:The Real Barenziah, v2")*, *[Dwemer Inquiries Vol I](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Inquiries_Vol_I "Skyrim:Dwemer Inquiries Vol I")* and *[Vol II](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Inquiries_Vol_II "Skyrim:Dwemer Inquiries Vol II")*, *[Pirate King of the Abecean](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate_King_of_the_Abecean "Skyrim:Pirate King of the Abecean")*, *[Ruins of Kemel-Ze](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Kemel-Ze "Skyrim:Ruins of Kemel-Ze")*, *[The "Madmen" of the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_%22Madmen%22_of_the_Reach "Skyrim:The \"Madmen\" of the Reach")*, *[The Song of Pelinal, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Song_of_Pelinal,_v1 "Skyrim:The Song of Pelinal, v1")* and *[v6](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Song_of_Pelinal,_v6 "Skyrim:The Song of Pelinal, v6")*, *[Biography of Barenziah, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Biography_of_Barenziah,_v1 "Skyrim:Biography of Barenziah, v1")*, two copies of *[v2](/wiki/Skyrim:Biography_of_Barenziah,_v2 "Skyrim:Biography of Barenziah, v2")* and one of *[v3](/wiki/Skyrim:Biography_of_Barenziah,_v3 "Skyrim:Biography of Barenziah, v3")*, *[A Kiss, Sweet Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Kiss,_Sweet_Mother "Skyrim:A Kiss, Sweet Mother")*, *[The Firsthold Revolt](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Firsthold_Revolt "Skyrim:The Firsthold Revolt")*, *[A Children's Anuad](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Children%27s_Anuad "Skyrim:A Children's Anuad")*, *[The Ransom of Zarek](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ransom_of_Zarek "Skyrim:The Ransom of Zarek")*, *[A Dance in Fire, v4](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v4 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v4")*, *[Myths of Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Myths_of_Sheogorath "Skyrim:Myths of Sheogorath")*, and *[Brief History of the Empire, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:Brief_History_of_the_Empire,_v2 "Skyrim:Brief History of the Empire, v2")*. In addition to the books, there is also a sample of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), a filled [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem"), two bowls, a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a bowl of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a [troll skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull"), and a set of [small antlers](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_Antlers "Skyrim:Small Antlers"). Between the shelves is a barrel containing ingredients.

## Notes

- Sebastian Lort respawns along with the rest of the cave.
- Despite being considered a werewolf lair in the game data, no [werewolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf "Skyrim:Werewolf") are ever found in the eve.

## Bugs

- Rimerock Burrow isn't marked as a cave, so cave-based radiant quests won't target it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.

| **Help [Madesi](/wiki/Skyrim:Madesi "Skyrim:Madesi") make jewelry.** | |

| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Madesi](/wiki/Skyrim:Madesi "Skyrim:Madesi") |
| Location(s): | None |
| Reward: | 400 gold, leveled necklace |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Madesi](/wiki/Skyrim:Madesi "Skyrim:Madesi")) |
| ID: | FreeformRiften18 |

Madesi in his stall

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Madesi](/wiki/Skyrim:Madesi "Skyrim:Madesi") in his stall in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").
2. Gather one [mammoth tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Mammoth Tusk"), one [gold ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore "Skyrim:Gold Ore"), and two [flawless sapphires](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Sapphire "Skyrim:Flawless Sapphire").
3. Return to Madesi.

## Detailed Walkthrough

All the necessary components

Speak with [Madesi](/wiki/Skyrim:Madesi "Skyrim:Madesi") and ask him about his [jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Jewelry "Skyrim:Jewelry"). You will learn that he is running low on supplies due to heavy [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") presence on the roads and needs help gathering some components. He requires two [flawless sapphires](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Sapphire "Skyrim:Flawless Sapphire"), one [mammoth tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Mammoth Tusk"), and one piece of [gold ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore "Skyrim:Gold Ore").

Flawless sapphires, like all [gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems"), can be randomly found or [mined](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining"). One guaranteed sample can be stolen from the shelves in the Inner Sanctum of the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella") in Markarth.

Mammoth tusks can be looted from slain [mammoths](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth"), as well as bought from [hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter "Skyrim:Hunter") and certain merchants. Three guaranteed samples can be found in the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)")'s [Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum"); eight guaranteed samples can be found in [Halted Stream Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Halted_Stream_Camp "Skyrim:Halted Stream Camp"). The closest one is in [Black-Briar Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Meadery "Skyrim:Black-Briar Meadery"), where it can be stolen from the shelves of a cupboard in [Indaryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Indaryn "Skyrim:Indaryn")'s bedroom.

Gold ore can be found randomly in containers or in buildings, but an easy place to find some gold veins is in [Kolskeggr Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine"). There's also [Lost Prospect Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Prospect_Mine "Skyrim:Lost Prospect Mine"); while the latter is closer, it doesn't have as many veins as Kolskeggr Mine. Alternately, one can just use [the Transmute spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Transmute_Mineral_Ore "Skyrim:Transmute Mineral Ore") to turn one Iron Ore into one Gold Ore.

You can return the items to Madesi as you find them, or all at once. He will give you 100 gold for each item returned (i.e., 200 for the two sapphires). Once you've returned them all, ask Madesi if he needs anything else and he will thank you with a leveled necklace.

## Notes

- Completing this quest counts towards your eligibility for becoming [Thane of the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Rift "Skyrim:Thane of the Rift").
- On a purely money-making basis, this quest is a financial loss. Even at the lowest speech level, you can sell flawless sapphires (including to Madesi himself) for more then the quest reward of 100 per sapphire. At higher speech levels, you can sell a mammoth tusk for more than 100 gold. Purchasing the items for this quest will make the money loss even worse.
- Madesi will accept stolen goods in fulfillment of this quest, which may be useful if you are trying to avoid dealing with [fences](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Fences "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") or spending a perk point on the [fence perk](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Fence "Skyrim:Speech").
- You cannot toggle the objective in your journal for individual items; doing so will instead toggle all 3 items at once or the remaining two if you delivered one.
- [Halted Stream Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Halted_Stream_Camp "Skyrim:Halted Stream Camp") is the location of a [bounty quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Bandit_Boss "Skyrim:Bounty: Bandit Boss"), possible location of a [Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Bandits) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Bandits)") quest from [Amren](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren "Skyrim:Amren"), and possible location of the [Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon") quest, making it easy to complete multiple quests at once if you choose to find your mammoth tusk there.

## Bugs

- There are no quest markers for delivering the items back to Madesi.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- The quest may continue to prompt the objective to bring Madesi his items if the objective to do so is in your quest journal.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.9, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Ringmaker (FreeformRiften18) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Find 2 flawless sapphires for Madesi (<Global=FFR18GemCount>/2)  *Objective 20:* Find a mammoth tusk for Madesi (<Global=FFR18TuskCount>/1)  *Objective 30:* Find gold ore for Madesi (<Global=FFR18OreCount>/1) |
| 30 |  | *(Brought two flawless sapphires)* |
| 40 |  | *(Brought a mammoth tusk)* |
| 50 |  | *(Brought a chunk of gold ore)* |
| 60 |  | *Objective 40:* Speak to Madesi |
|  |  | *(Assigned as you acquire the relevant objects)* *Objective 15:* Bring the flawless sapphires to Madesi  *Objective 25:* Bring the mammoth tusks to Madesi  *Objective 35:* Bring the gold ore to Madesi |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 200, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformRiften18 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformRiften18`.

## Overview

| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [The Bloodstone Chalice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bloodstone_Chalice "Skyrim:The Bloodstone Chalice") |  | | |

The Ring of the Beast and the Ring of the Erudite

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with [Feran Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Feran_Sadri "Skyrim:Feran Sadri").
2. Find the two rings.
3. Report back to Feran.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Speak with [Feran Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Feran_Sadri "Skyrim:Feran Sadri") in [Volkihar Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep"), who sends you to retrieve two ancient vampiric rings, the [Ring of the Erudite](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_the_Erudite "Skyrim:Ring of the Erudite") and the [Ring of The Beast](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_The_Beast "Skyrim:Ring of The Beast"). The rings are held by two leveled targets in two random locations. After retrieving the rings, return to the castle to receive your reward (you get to keep the rings).

## Bugs

- If a previously slain enemy is chosen as a bearer of one of the rings, or a previously cleared dungeon is chosen as the destination, it may be impossible to complete as the body may have disappeared, meaning the ring cannot be obtained.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.1.1, fixes this bug.
  - Reload a save made before receiving the mission from Feran Sadri, and then initiate the quest again to be assigned different ring locations.
  -  Add the missing ring via console to the inventory `player.addItem ITEM_ID 1` (where `ITEM_ID` can be looked up like this: help "Ring of the Beast"). Advance the quest stage via console. Try stages 10, 110, 120 (e.g. command `setstage DLC1RV08 110`). If this works as intended and both rings are in your possession, you should be able to report back to Feran.
- The location given for finding one of the rings may be the Katariah. The ship does not arrive until the Hail Sithis quest, rendering the ring unattainable until you have reached that point of the Dark Brotherhood questline. Thus if you choose to destroy the Dark Brotherhood, the ring becomes unattainable.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
- Sometimes the random leveled NPC chosen to hold the ring will be an essential character. In this case, the only way to obtain the ring is to pickpocket it from them.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1RV08 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1RV08`.
